asali mard aur mardangi ke aam samaajik-saanskritik paimaane par langot dharn karne aur dubli-patali kayaa vale mahatmaa gaandhi kahin tikte dikhai nahin dete haian vo barbr hiansk braitani samrajy ke samne ahiansa ki bat karate haian
is ahiansk jaddojhad mein unake hathiyaar haian satyaagrh, charakha, khadi, upavas aur anashana
puchhne vale aaj bhi puchhte hi haian ye kaun se hathiyaar hain?
islie kai tarah ke logon aur khaskar ek vichar valon ko unaki soch aur kam karne ke tarike mein namrdgi, napuanskata aur kayrata nazar aati hai
unhein darapok kaha jata hai aur sabako darapok banane ka iljam lagayaa jata hai
halaanki, gaandhi ke mutabiq unaki ahiansa, bahaduron ki ahiansa hai khair
jis tarah ki mardangi humaara samaaj aur humaari sanskriti purushon mein dekhna aur bona chahti hai, vo sunne aur dekhne mein chumbk jaisa aakarshn rakhati hai magar vah paida kyaa karati hai? vo gairbarabri aur hiansa hi to paida karati hai striyon ko apane se kamatar aur maathat maanti hai
to aazadi ke lie ahiansa ka rasta chunne ka matalab ek aisa desh banana tha, jahan hiansa se kisi bhi tarah ki chizein tay n hoti hoan
is ahiansa ka matalab ye bhi tha ki ghar ke dayre mein aur ghar ke bahr, purush samaaj striyon ke sath ahianska suluk karata hai yaa nahian
aisa nahin tha ki isse pahale aisi soch vale log nahin hue the magar rashtr ke taur par yah nai tarah ki mardangi gadhne ki bat thi
is jagah ki simaa hai islie hum khastaur par un kuchh baton ko hi dekheange, jo striyon ki ziandgi se juadi haian yaani gaandhi kisi purush ko stri jivn mein kis tarah ki mardangi ke sath dekhna chahte the shayd inse kuchh sanket milean
bat unaki zati ziandgi se shuru karate haian gaandhi apani aatmkatha mein shadi aur usake bad ki ziandgi ka zikr karate haian
unaka aur kasturbai ka bal vivah huaa tha vo bal vivah par sharmianda haian bad mein vo aise bal vivah ke zabaradast virodhi bhi bane vo batate hain ki kisi kitab mein padha tha, ek patni-vrt palna pati ka dharm hai
samgri upalabdh nahin hai
gaandhi ko laga ki agar mujhe ek patni vrt palna hai to patni ko ek pati ka vrt palna chahie main irshyaalu pati ban gayaa palna chahie mein se main palavana chahie ke vichar par pahuancha aur agar palavana hai, to mujhe patni ki nigrani rakhani chahie mujhe humesha yah dekhna chahie ki meri stri kahan jati hai? islie meri anumti ke bina vah kahin ja hi nahin sakati  yaani unake shabdon mein, maianne to pati ki satta chalana shuru kar diyaa
to kyaa patni ko kabu mein rakhane ke lie gaandhi ke yahi vichar the? gaandhi ji se hi javab maaanga jae
ve kahate hain, "bina anumti ke kahin bhi n ja sakana to ek tarah ki qaid hi hui par kasturba aisi qaid sahan karne vali thi hi nahian agar main us par dabav dalta hun to vah mujh par kyon n dale? yah to ab samajh mein aa raha hai us samay to mujhe apana patitv siddh karna tha"
yahan ek mard n sirf apani kamazori ka bayaan kar raha balki stri ki aazad satta ko svikar kar raha hai apane barabr maan raha hai yah kaisa mardana pati hai? kaisi mardangi hai?
ek naujvan gaandhi ko likhte hain ki main khadi praemi hun lekin patni ko khadi pasand nahin hai
vah puchhte hain ki kyaa main use khadi pahanane ke lie majabur karun? gaandhi ne to khadi ke lie bahut kuchh kiyaa videshi kapaadon ka bahishkar kiyaa charakha chalavayaa sut katavayaa unaka javab kyaa ho sakata hai? sochie
ve salah dete hain, "apani patni ko mohbbt se jitna hai, zor-zabaradasti kar haragiz nahian yaani aap apani patni ko khadi istemaal karne ke lie mazabur nahin kar sakate yaad rakhie jaise aap usaki jaydad nahin hain vaise hi aapaki patni aapaki jaydad nahin hai"
gaandhi kahate hain ki main yah samajhata hun ki kisi shauhr ko apani patni par yaa maan-bap ko baadi santanon par apani ray jabarn thopne ka adhikar nahin hai
vo 11 mein hi kah chuke the ki, "jab tak humaari striyaan mahaz humaare bhog ka samaan raheangi yaa humaare lie rasoiyaa banakar raheangi aur humaari ziandgi ki humsafr, ziandgi ki jaddojehd ki barabr ki sathi, sukh-dukh ki sathi nahin banatin unaki behtari ki humaari sari koshishon ka phel hona tay hai kuchh log apani stri ko janvar ke barabr samajhate haian striyon ko hin samajhane ki jo pratha paadi hui hai, humein use jaad se ukhaad pheankna hoga purush ko apani patni ke bare mein apana ravaiyaa badalana hoga"
isi tarah vo kai jagah kahate dikhte hain, "patni pati ki gulam nahin hai balki vah usaki sathi hai"
gaandhi se saval-javab bahut hota tha 1 ki bat hai ek laadki ne unase bahr niklane vali laadkiyon par laadkon ki taraf se hone vali chhiantakshi, fbtiyaan, behudgi aur hiansa ki charcha ki to unhoanne lanba javab diyaa
us javab mein laadkon ke bare mein ek bat kahi vah aaj bhi kam ahum nahin hai
unhoanne kaha, "sabase baada saval hai ki naujvan laadke samaany shishtachar bhi kyon chhoad dein jisse bhali laadkiyon ko unase utpiadn aur satae jane ka humesha dar laga rahe? mujhe yah jankar baada dukh hoga ki zyaadatr navayuvkon mein stri sammaan ki bhavna hi gayb ho gayi hai bataur yuvk varg, inhein to apani chhavi ke bare mein chiantit hona chahie yahi nahin, apane sathiyon ke bich paye jane vali striyon ke prati asabhyta ke aise har maamle ka ilaj karna chahie"
gaandhi ke lie aazadi ka aaandoln purushon ka mardana aaandoln nahin tha yah unaki mardangi ka prayog bhi tha
striyon ki bhagidari aasan nahin thi lekin dekhte hi dekhte ve aazadi ki muhim ka zaruri hissa ban gaian vo gaandhi ko bhi chunauti de rahi thian
is bat ko behtar samajhane ke lie hum 1 ki ek bat ka sahara le sakate haian
mridula sarabhai unase puchhti hain ki mahilaon par to dohra-tihra bojh paad raha hai unhein aazadi ke kam ke sath-sath ghar bhi sanbhalna paadta hai aapaka kyaa kahana hai?
javab mein gaandhi kahate hain, "main samajhata hun ki mahilaon ki yah ghar ki dasta humaari barbrata ki nishani hai meri ray mein bavrchikhane ki gulami mukhyta humaari barbr zamaane ki hi bachi hui nishani hai bahut ho chuka ab humaari mahilaon ko is dusvpn se aazad hona hi chahie kisi mahila ka sara vaqt ghar ke kam mein hi nahin lag jana chahie"
magar yah sab hoga kaise? barbr mardangi ke saanche mein dhale gae mard is nayi mardangi ko kaise apanaeange?
vo striyon ka sammaan kaise kareange? striyaan rasoi ki dasta se kaise nikleangi? stri ke kam ka mard sammaan kaise karega? baade hone par achank vah kaise sikhe? gaandhi ki potli se hi ek tarakib dikhti hai
jel mein rahane ke dauran gaandhi ne 1 mein ek balpothi likhi jankari ke mutabiq aangrez sarakar ne ise chhapne ki ijazat nahin di iska pahala prakashn  sal bat 11 mein ho payaa
gaandhi likhte hain, "pothi ki rachana mein dharna yah rahi hai ki balk jo kuchh sikhein, us par amal karean aisi koi chiz nahin di hai, jiska unhein roz anubhv n hota ho" yah pothi ek laadka aur usaki maan ke bich sanvadon par aadharit 1 path ki hai
gyaarhavan path hai ghar ka kam
kyon n ise hum sab milkar padhein?
   
dekho beta, jis tarah shaanta didi ghar ke kam mein madad karati hai, usi tarah tumhein bhi karni chahie
lekin maan, shaanta didi to laadki hai laadke ka kam hai khelna aur padhna
shaanta bol uthi kyaa humein khelna aur padhna nahin hota?
main inkar kab karata hun? lekin tumhein sath-sath ghar kam bhi karna hota hai
maa boli to kyaa laadka ghar kam n kare?
maadhv ne chat se javab diyaa laadke ko to baada hone par kamaana hota hai, islie yah zaruri hai ki vah padhne mein zyaada dhyaan de
maa ne kaha beta, yah vichar hi galat hai ghar ka kam karne se bhi bahut-kuchh sikhne ko milta hai tumhein abhi pata nahin ki agar tum ghar saf rakho, rasoi mein madad karo, kapaade dhoo, baratan maaanjo, to usase tumhein kitna sara sikhne ko mil sakata hai
ghar ke kam mein aankh ka, hath ka, dimaaga ka upayog kuchh kam nahin karna paadta lekin yah upayog sahaj hi ho jata hai islie humein usaka pata nahin chalata is tarah dhire-dhire humaara vikas hota rahata hai aur yahi humaari sachchi padhai hai
sath hi, agar tum ghar ka kam karate raho to usase tumhari yogyta aur kushlata badhti hai, sharir kas jata hai aur kam karne ka aadi banata hai aur phir baade hone par tum kisi ke mohtaj nahin rahate main to kahati hun ki ghar ka kam sikhne aur karne ki jitni zarurt shaanta didi ko hai, utani hi tumhein bhi hai
  
yahan gaur karne layk kuchh batein haian laadke ko ghar ke kam islie nahin karne hain ki ve striyon ki madad karean balki islie karein kyoanki ye unaki bhi utani hi zimmedari hai, jitni kisi stri ki
yahi nahin, gaandhi ke mutabiq aise kam laadkon ki khushhali ke lie zaruri hai unhoanne ghar ke kam ko kam ka darza diyaa hai use dimaagi kam maana hai
kyaa ismein humein aisi baton ka javab nahin milta hai tum ghar mein karati hi kyaa ho? tumhein kuchh nahin samajh mein aaega apana dimaag chulha-chauka mein hi lagao
yahi nahin, ismein shaanta yaani laadke ki bahan ki sakriy bhagidari aur aazad shakhsiyt hai vah apane bare mein khud bolti hai
dhyaan rahe, yah path aaj se lagabhag 1 sal pahale likha gayaa hai jeandr ki samajhadari ka daur hai n anaped domestik keyr vark ko samajhane aur ghar ke kam mein mardon ki bhagidari ki muhim ka magar yahan bat to vahi ho rahi hai
anaped domestik keyr vark yaani ghar mein dekhbhal aur rozana ke dusre kam, jise ghar ki mahilaon ki zimmedari maani jati hai aur in kamon ke lie alag se koi paisa nahin milta hai
to gaandhi ji aisa mard banana chahte the aise hi mard, nai mardangi ki nianv ban sakate haian aisi mardangi ki jaisi zarurt 1 sal pahale thi, usase jyaada aaj hai
not gaandhi ji ki anek baton ko aaj kasauti par kasa ja sakata hai kasa hi jana chahie unaki anek batein atapati yaa takaraati mileangi magar sabase baada saval hai ki kyaa mahatmaa gaandhi purushon ko mahilaon ka hakim banana chahte the? agar nahin to baki chizon par bat ho sakati hai

jammu-kashmir pulis ne ek tvit kar batayaa hai ki charamapanthiyon ne anantnag ke upayukt karyaaly ke bahr ek grened humala kiyaa pulis ke anusar ghayl logon ko maamuli chot lagi hai 
pulis ne batayaa ki ilake ki gherabandi kar di gai hai aur talashi abhiyaan chalayaa ja raha hai
samaachar ejeansi pitiaai ne ek pulis adhikari ke havale se batayaa hai ki charamapanthiyon ne subh karib 11 baje anantnag ke bhari surksha vale disi fis ke bahr ek gashti dal par grened pheanka
pulis adhikari ne batayaa ki grened saadk kinare ja phata aur isse nikle chharron se log ghayl ho gae
abhi tak kisi bhi gut yaa vykti ne is humale ki zimmedari nahin li hai
gaurtalab hai ki karib do mahine pahale jammu kashmir ko vishesh rajy ka darja dene vale anuchchhed  ko nishprabhavi kar diyaa gayaa tha jiske bad se jammu-kashmir mein lagi pabandi ab bhi jari hai 
anuchchhed  hataye jane ke bad rajy mein ashaanti ki aashanka ke karn ghati ke alagavvadi aur rajnitik dal ke netaon ko bhi najaraband kar liyaa gayaa tha

gair yojnabddh tarike se base patana mein zamin ati simit hai aur pradesh ki aabadi ke badhne ki raftar bhi sabase tez hai
qrib 1 karoad ki aabadi vale bihar mein lagabhag har sal barish se janleva jalajamaav, badh, sukha aur aaparadhik maamlon mein badhotri hoti rahati hai
vyvasthit aur svchchh shahar ke maapdand se koson dur rahane ke bavjud is rajy ke har vykti ke man mein yah ichchha hoti hai ki rajdhani patana mein usaka aashiyaana ho
varishth vastuvid jeke lal ka maanna hai ki bihar ke log patana mein islie basana chahte hain kyoanki yahan rahane ke bavjud vah apani mul jagah se zyaada juada rahate hain aur unhein apane mul sthan se adhik suvidha bhi upalabdh hoti hai
yahan zamin-makan khridne se logon ka unake mul sthan se bhaugaulik aur bhavnatmk juadav bana rahata hai
vo kahate hain, "patana ek purana shahar hai aur nae patana ke lie taun planiang ko lekr sambndhit vibhag sanvednashil nahin rahe haian atikrman ki samsyaa smaart siti banane mein baada roada raha hai"
udhar varishth chartrd akauanteant nirj kumaar lal ka maanna hai ki keandr ki nareandr modi sarakar ke navanbr, 1 mein notbandi lagu karne ke bad zamin ka bazar bhav sarkil ret ki tulna mein kam ho gayaa
unake anusar, "notbandi ke bad zamin ke bhav ke sandrbh mein bat pahale ki tarah nahin rahi sath hi kaade bildiang baylaj, makan ka naksha pas karane ki pechidgi aadi karnon se zamin ka bazar bhav yaa to sthir ho gayaa yaa kam ho gayaa"
ve kahate hain, "patana mein jis do katthe ki zamin ka bhav notbandi ke pahale do karoad rupye tha vo aaj bhi usi dar mein bik rahi haian isse jahir hai ki notbandi ke bad kale dhan ko hold kar liyaa gayaa hai isse patana mein zamin ka bhav sthir ho gayaa hai"
thoadi si barish mein shahar ke kuchh hisse dub jate hain aur yah samsyaa kai dashak se bani hui hai sarakar ko yah maalum hai, lekin is morche par sarakar viphl rahi hai
rajy ke any jila mukhyaalyon ki tulna mein patana mein suvidhaen zyaada haian yahan behtar skul-kalej aur asptal hain islie rajy ke any hisson ke log yahan aakar basate haian patana mein mahangi zamin rahane ka ek karn yah hai
dusra karn sarkl ret sarakari dara aur bazar bhav mein bhari aantr rahana hai zamin ka sarakari bhav kam rahana aur bazar muly adhik rahane se ek khas tabake ke lie jamin mein nivesh karna aasan hota hai 
is karn bhi yahan zamin mahangi hai
jeke lal ki baton se spsht hai ki bazar aur sarakari bhav mein bhari aantr patana mein zamin-makan mein kale dhan ko nivesh karne ke raste aasan bana rahe haian
vahin varishth patrkar esae shad ke anusar patana mein aasamaan chhute zamin ke dam ke do karn ginate haian 
vo kahate hain, "any rajyon ki tulna mein bihar ka janasankhyaa ghanatv sabase adhik hai yahan karib 11 vykti prati varg kilomitr mein log rahate-basate hain jabaki rashtriy ausat  ka hai vahin patana mein 1 vykti prati varg kilomitr mein haian aise mein aavasiy bhumi ki bhari kami hai 
pichhle ek dashak se adhik ki avadhi mein bihar ka bajat , karoad se badhkar do lakh karoad ka ho gayaa hai 
is dauran khasa nirmaan kary huaa hai jiske lie banane vale dipiaar mein 1 se 11 pratisht ki rashi bataur munafa milti hai isse ek bahut baadi rashi bajar mein aati hai 
vahin dusri or rashtriy pichhada varg aayog ne  ke dashak mein ek riport diyaa tha jismein kaha gayaa tha ki sarakari yojnaon se juadi rashi ka  pratisht bhrshtachar ki bheant chadh jata hai 
agar ise  pratisht bhi maan liyaa jae to is bat ka aandaza aasani se lagayaa ja sakata hai ki itne dinon mein kitna kala dhan bajar mein aayaa hoga 
patana mein zamin mahangi hone ka yah mukhy karn hai, jise log kharidne ko taiyaar hain, jabaki bhumi ki upalabdhta ati-simit hai
inki baton se jahir hai ki mukhymantri nitish kumaar bhale hi yah dava karate hain ki bhrshtachar par unaka ziro tolreans rahata hai, lekin vastvikta to yah hai ki bhrshtachar ko rokne mein yahan ki sarakarein lagatar viphl rahi haian
isse lagatar akut kala dhan paida hota raha hai aur is kale dhan ko nivesh karne ka sabase sugm rasta logon ko zamin-makan mein najar aata hai
varishth patrkar kumaar dinesh patana mein zamin aur flait ke dam bethasha badhne ke tin baade karn ginate haian 
unake anusar,"pahala karn desh mein dusri sabase aabadi vale rajy bihar mein janasankhyaa vriddhi ki tej raftar, dusra sarakari yojnaon mein belgam bhrshtachar aur tisra rajdhani patana mein zamin yaa makan ko samaajik haisiyt se joadna 
inmein se pahali do batein yaani janasankhyaa niyantrn aur bhrshtachar par rok lagane mein lagabhag har sarakar ka viphl hona ek aisi paristhiti banata hai jismein logon ka kala dhan patana ke simit aavasiy bhu-bhag ke dam ko aasamaan par pahuanchane mein sahayk rahi haian
rahi bat janasankhyaa niytrann ki to ye lagabhag sabhi dalon ke rajnitik ejeandon se bahr hai
purv mukhy sachiv vies dube ka maanna hai ki sarakar ne ekadh apavadon jaise rajendr nagara-kankadbag ke kuchh hisse ko chhoad kar patana shahar ko viksit nahin kiyaa hai 
patana mein shahari vikas ko lekr sarakar ne kuchh nahin kiyaa hai yah shahar niji logon ke prayaas se viksit huaa hai aur jyaadatr hisson mein patana ka yojnabddh tarike se vikas nahin ho payaa hai     
dube kahate hain, "yahan behtar svasthy-shiksha ki vyvastha hai aur kuchh had tak vyaapar bhi hai jab bihar ka har ek aadami patana mein basana chahega to utani jamin upalabdh kahan se hogi? zahir hai, isse jamin ki kimt badhegi 
unaka maanna hai ki patana mein itni mahangi jamin kahin se tarkik nahin hai 
chuanki sarakar ki or se shahar ko viksit karne aur muhlle basane ke lie koi yojna nahin hai islie saadk, bijli aur nale hon yaa n hon log iski chianta kiye bagair jamin kharidte haian 
yah sab atydhik maaang aur nyuntam aapurti kshmata par hi aadharit hai is karn bhi zamin ke dar aasamaan chhu rahe haian
eshiyn devlapameant risrch ianstityut aadri ke nideshk praofesr pipi ghosh ka maanna hai ki patana ke shaharikran ki samsyaa janasankhyaa se sambndhit hai 
vo kahate hain, "atirikt janasankhyaa ko samaahit karne ke lie atirikt sadhn chahiye iske lie aarthik sadhn aur zamin chahiye, lekin durbhagyvash patana ke sandrbh mein zamin ki samsyaa bahut ganbhir hai
pipi ghosh ke mutabiq, "patana shahar ko purb ki or vistarit nahin kiyaa ja sakata kyoanki udhar purana patana hai pashchim mein militri kaiantonmeant hai, uttr disha mein ganga nadi hai aur dakshin ki or ki zamin kaphi niche hai
"rahi bat aarthik sansadhnon ki to vah dusri samsyaa hai patana ke shaharikran ki samsyaa janasankhyaa aur yahan par aarthik gatividhi aur jamin ka atisimit rahana hai yahan flaiovar banane ke lie kafi kharch kiyaa gayaa, lekin us tulna mein drenej par dhyaan nahin diyaa gayaa praathmikta hi galat hai" 
patana mein dilli ke str ka ems asptal nahin hai javahr nehru vishvvidyaaly nahin hain, dilli vishvvidyaaly nahin hai beangluru-haidrabad shaharon jaise aaiti hab nahin hai aur n hi muanbi jaisi aarthik gatividhi hai phir bhi yahan zamin-makan kafi mahange haian aisa kyon hai?
ispar praofesr ghosh kahate hain ki kisi bhi pichhade rajy mein jahan iandstri nahin hai, vahan gair krishi gatividhi seva kshetr mein hi hoti hai seva kshetr shuruaati daur mein vahin viksit hota hai jahan prashasnik mukhyaaly ho patana ke sandrbh mein bhi yahi ho raha hai
yahan baiank, asptal aur yunivrsiti hain jiska fayda lene ke lie rajy ke dusre shaharon se log patana mein palayn kar rahe haian us tulna mein zamin ki aapurti nahin ho pa rahi jabaki palayn har din ho raha hai islie jamin ki kimt badh rahi hai

is ilake mein peadon ki katai ko lekr kar pahale se chal raha virodh shukrvar ko shuru hui katai ke bad aur baada ho gayaa shanivar ko yahan baadi sankhyaa mein paryaavran samarthk virodh pradarshn karne utar gae
virodh kar rahe paryaavran karykartaon ki pulis ke sath hathapai hui aur ilaqe mein tanav ko dekhte hue tainat puliskarmiyon ki sankhyaa badha di gai aur sath hi pure ilake mein dhara 1 laga di gai
is bich pulis ne virodh kar rahe  se adhik karykartaon ko girftar kiyaa aur any kai logon ko puchhtachh ke lie hirast mein liyaa
brihn muanbi nagar nigm biemsi ki tri athariti ne  agast 1 ko aare kaloni mein metro praojekt ke lie kar shed banane ki manjuri di thi iske lie qrib ,1 pead kate jane haian iske alava 1 peadon ko yahan se dusri jagahon par shipht bhi kiyaa jana hai shahar mein kisi bhi jagah par ek sath  se adhik peadon ki katai ke lie praadhikran ki manjuri anivary hai
metro  pariyojna ke tahat prastavit metro karshed ke lie aare kaloni ke dakshini bhag mein  hekteyr zamin ka istemaal kiyaa jana hai
metro praojekt ke lie kar shed banane ki manjuri die jane ke bad se hi iska virodh ho raha hai ise lekr hai kort mein kai yaachikaen dali gain lekin kort ne sabhi yaachikaen kharij kar dian
bambe hai kort ne shukrvar ko aare kaloni ko jangl nahin maante hue biemsi se yahan ke , se adhik peadon ki katai ki manjuri ke faisle ko radd karne se inkar kar diyaa iske bad peadon ki katai ka kam shuru huaa hai
udhar keandriy paryaavran mantri prakash javadekr ne aare kaloni mein peadon ki katai ko lekr kaha ki "bambe hai kort ne faisla diyaa hai ki yah jangl nahin hai"
unhoanne kaha, "jab dilli mein pahale metro steshn bana to - pead kate jane ki zarurt thi tab bhi logon ne virodh kiyaa tha, lekin kate gae pratyek pead ke badale paanch pead lagae gae dilli mein kul 1 metro steshn bane, sath hi jangl bhi badha aur  lakh logon ki paryaavran purk sarvjanik yaatayaat ki vyvastha hui yahi mantr hai, vikas bhi aur paryaavran ki raksha bhi, donon sath-sath"
peadon ki katai ka virodh karne mein aam janata, paryaavran samarthk se lekr balivud ke kai sitare bhi aage aae haian lekin sattarudh bhartiy janata parti ko khud apani sahayogi shivsena se sabase baade virodh ka samna karna paad raha hai shivsena pramukh uddhv thakre aur unake bete aadity thakre aare kaloni mein peadon ki katai ke virodh mein utar aae haian
uddhv ne yah kahate hue peadon ki katai ka virodh kiyaa ki bhari virodh ke karn metro karshed ka hashr nanar grin riphaynari jaisa hi hoga unhoanne vada kiyaa ki agar satta mein dobara vapsi ki to iske lie zimmedar logon ke khilaf karrvai ki jaegi 
unhoanne kaha, "mere lie aare philhas sabase baada mudda hai jo kuchh aaj ho raha hai, jo kal huaa aur jo bhavishy mein hoga main samuchi sthiti ki vistrit suchna luanga aur majabuti se is mudde par sidhe boluanga aane vali sarakar humaari hogi aur jaise hi hum ek bar phir satta mein aate hain hum aare ke janglon ke hatyaaron se har sanbhv tarike se nipteange"
uddhv ke bete aur shivsena neta aadity thakre ne bhi is par apani kaadi pratikriyaa di hai aadity ne kaha ki keandr sarakar ko agar aare kaloni ke jangl ki chianta nahin hai to unhein paryaavran bachane ko lekr bhi nahin bolna chahie
aadity thakre ne tvit kiyaa, "peadon ko jis tezi se kata gayaa, use dekhte hue muanbi metro ke adhikariyon ko pioke mein kyon nahin tainat kiyaa jana chahie? unhein peadon ko nasht karne ki jagah aatankvadi addon ko nasht karne bhej dena chahie"
unhoanne tvit kiyaa, "kai paryaavranavid aur yahan tak ki aas pas ke kai sthaniy shivsena karykartaon ne ise rokne ki koshish ki lekin pulis ki bhari tainati ke bich jis tarah se in janglon ki katai ho rahi hai, usase muanbimetro vo sab kuchh nasht kar raha hai jise bhart ne paryaavran ke bare mein sanyukt rashtr mein kaha tha"
thakre se pahale kaangres, enasipi aur emaenaes samet kai samaajik karykarta aur filmi jagat ki kai jani maani hastiyon ne bhi iska virodh kiyaa hai
balivud abhinetri aur kaangres ki tikt par 1 ka loksabha chunav laad chuki urmila maatoandkar ne peadon ki katai ko nirashajnak batayaa unhoanne tvit kiyaa ki peadon ki katai raat mein hi shuru karne se yah spsht hota hai ki unhein bhi pata hai ki yah bhayaank galati hai 
abhinetri diyaa mirja ne bhi is bare mein tvit kar likha hai, "notis adalt ki anumti ke 1 din bad tak hona chahie notis ko aadhikarik vebsait par apalod kiyaa jana chahie lekin aisa nahin ho raha hai"
paryaavran karykarta zoru bhathena ne aare kaloni mein metro karshed ke nirmaan ke lie , peadon ko katne ke muanbi mahangarapalika ke faisle ko adalt mein chunauti di thi
karykartaon ka dava hai ki yaachika nirst hone ke kuchh hi ghanton ke bhitr  se zyaada peadon ko gira diyaa gayaa
ilake mein rahane vale ek karykarta, prakash bhoir ne bbc ko batayaa, "raat lagabhag  baje, prashasn aandr aayaa, unhoanne karshed sthl par peadon ko katna shuru kar diyaa"
yahan ke sthaniy nivasi aur paryaavran praemi is karshed ko dusri jagah sthanaantrit karne ki maaang kar rahe haian
unhoanne aashanka jatai hai ki is kar shed se ilaqe ki jaiv-vividhta nasht hogi aur ilaqe mein aur nirmaan ke lie zamin par qbze ka rasta khulega
paryaavran karykartaon ka kahana hai ki adalt ki anumti ke bad pead ko katne ke lie pandrh dinon ka samay diyaa jana chahie
halanki muanbi metro ke prabandh nideshk ashvini bhide ne tvit kar iska javab dete hue likha hai, "adalt ki anumti ke bad, jhuthi jankari phailai ja rahi hai ki peadon ko katne ke lie 1 din ka notis dena hoga iska koi kanuni aadhar nahin hai "
muanbi metro rel karporeshn ka kahana hai ki yah ek mahatvpurn pariyojna hai aur is ilaqe mein lokl tren ki yaatra ke dauran har din 1 logon ki maut hoti hai
muanbi metro ke ek pravakta aashutosh kuanbhkoni ne adalt ko batayaa ki is pariyojna ke pura hone se is sthiti par niyantrn pai ja sakegi

akhbar ne paanch aktubr ke aank mein eshiyaa sekshn mein yah lekh prakashit kiyaa hai paanch aktubr ko bhart prashasit kashmir mein lagi pabandiyon aur sanchar maadhymon par lagi rok ke do mahine pure ho gae
bhart sarakar ne jammu-kashmir ko vishesh darja dene vale anuchchhed  ko nishprabhavi karne se pahale paanch agast 1 se hi rajy mein kaadi pabandiyaan laga di thian 
mobail-fon-iantrnet par niyantrn ke sath hi vahan baadi sankhyaa mein netaon aur any logon ko girftar yaa hirast mein liyaa gayaa yaa phir nazaraband kar diyaa gayaa

in do mahinon mein kashmir mein jo kuchh huaa us par aantrarashtriy midiyaa ki nigahein bhi lagatar bani hui thian 
aanttarashtriy midiyaa ne shuruaat se kashmir se juadi khbaron ko pramukhta se prakashit kiyaa aur vistrit sanpadkiy lekh bhi chhape

ismein likha hai ki bhart ke nyaayaadhish kashmir mein ho rahe utpiadn ko nazaraaandaz kar rahe haian 
hirast mein lie gae logon mein vakil aur patrkar bhi shamil haian kashmiriyon ke utpiadn aur unhein pite jane jaise ganbhir aarop bhi samne aae haian 
bhart ne rajy mein fon aur iantrnet seva bhi band kar di hai jisse lakhon log alaga-thalag paad gae haian 
nyuyrk taims ne likha hai, "pradhanmantri modi ne sanyukt rashtr mahasbha mein die apane bhashn mein kashmir ka zikr nahin kiyaa lekin isse kuchh dinon pahale hyustn mein ek raili mein unhoanne kaha ki anuchchhed  hatae jane ke bad kashmiriyon ko baki bhartiyon ke barabr adhikar mil gae haian
akhbar ka dava hai ki is riport ke lie kashmir ke 1 gaanvon ke 1 logon ka iantravyu kiyaa gayaa
akhbar likhta hai, "maanvadhikar karykartaon ka kahana hai ki kashmir duniyaa ke sabase adhik sainyikrit kshetron mein se ek hai yahan lanbe vaqt se aazadi yaa pakistan mein shamil hone ki maaang rahi hai, jiska natija bhari surkshablon ki tainati ke rup mein dekhne ko milta hai
lagabhag 1 shabdon ki is riport mein akhbar ne likha hai, "paanch agast se kashmir mein hatasha, gussa aur dar badhta hi ja raha hai pahale se hi bhari surkshablon ki maujudgi vale is rajy mein bhart sarakar ne sthaniy logon se virodh ki aashanka mein hazaron sainik aur tainat kar rakhe haian"
iske sath hi akhbar ne pichhle do mahinon mein hue ghatanakrmon par shuru se aakhir tak nazar dauadai hai 
inmein se ek tasvir mein skul-kalej band hone ki vajah se bachche ek sthaniy msjid mein padhai karate dikh rahe haian
ek dusri tasvir mein chhah sal ki bachchi dikh rahi hai jiski dain aaankh mein rabar ki goliyon se chot lagi hui hai 
ek any tasvir mein ek bachchi khiadki se jhaankti hui virodh pradarshn dekh rahi hai
ejeansi ne bhartiy lekhika aur maanvadhikar karykarta aruandhti ray ka ek iantravyu bhi chhapa hai jismein unhoanne  kaha  hai ki kashmir mein aavaz uthane vale har shakhs ko girftar kiyaa gayaa hai
iske alava vebsait par bhartiy grihmantri amit shah ke us bayaan par aadharit khbar bhi hai jismein unhoanne kaha tha ki agale 1 varshon mein kashmir bhart ke sabase zyaada viksit rajyon mein se ek hoga 
ejeansi ki vebsait par chhapi khbar kahati hai, " agast se lekr ab tak jammu-kashmir lagabhag puri tarah se qaid mein hai pradarshn kar rahe patrkaron ne rajy mein mobail aur iantrnet seva bahal kie jane ki maaang ki jo pichhle do mahinon se band hai"
filhal bhartiy supraim kort ki ek sanvaidhanik beanch anuchchhed  khtm kie jane aur kashmir se juadi any yaachikaon par javab dene ke lie keandr sarakar ko  dinon ka vaqt diyaa hai adalt ne maamle ki agali sunvai ke lie 1 navanbr ki tarikh tay ki hai
sarvochch nyaayaaly mein mein jammu-kashmir ko vishesh darja dene vale anuchchhed  ko hatae jane ko chunauti dene, praes ki aazadi, sanchar suvidhaon par rok, lakadaun ki vaidhta aur aane-jane par pabandiyon aur maanvadhikaron ke kathit ullanghn se juadi kai yaachikaen dayr ki gai haian
keandr shasit pradesh laddakh aur jammu-kashmir aupacharik rup se 1 aktubr, 1 ko astitv mein aa jaeange 
is bich jammu kashmir kishor nyaay samiti juvenail jastis kameti ne apani ek riport mein kaha hai ki ghati mein kisi bachche ko avaidh hirast mein nahin rakha gayaa hai
supraim kort ko sauanpi riport mein samiti ne kaha hai ki  agast ko jammu kashmir ka vishesh darja khtm kie jane ke bad se vahan 1 nabaligon ko girftar kiyaa gayaa tha, jismein  aur 11 sal ke bachche bhi shamil the

 fravari ko jammu-kashmir ke badagam mein pakistan ke sath havai sanghrsh ke dauran vayu sena ne apane hi mi-1 v helikptr ko maar girayaa tha jismein vayu sena ke chhah javanon aur ek aam nagrik ki maut ho gai thi

isi sal 1 agast ko chhattisgadh ke mukhymantri bhupesh baghel ne any pichhada varg ke lie aarakshn ka dayra 1 pratisht se badha kar  pratisht karne ki ghoshna ki thi 
is badhotri ke sath hi rajy mein aarakshn ka dayra badhkar  pratisht ho gayaa tha
rajy sarakar dvara any pichhada varg ke aarakshn ka dayra badhae jane ke khilaf dayr yaachika par sunvai ke bad mukhy nyaayaadhish piaar ramchandr menn ki pith ne badhe hue aarakshn par rok laga di hai
yaachikakrta ke vakil palash tivari ne kaha, "supraim kort ne iandira sahni aur en nagraj ke maamle mein sunvai ke bad aarakshn ki simaa  pratisht rakhe jane ke spsht nirdesh die haian lekin rajy sarakar ne pichhadepn ka havala dekr, bina kisi janaganana ke, enaesaesao ke ek sarve ko aadhar bana kar aarakshn ka dayra  pratisht kar diyaa haikort ne is par rok laga di hai"
is maamle ki sunvai ke dauran haikort ne aarthik rup se kamazor samaany jatiyon ko 1 pratisht aarakshn diye jane ko lekr koi tippni karne se yah kahate hue inkar kar diyaa ki yah maamla supraim kort mein lambit hai
sthaniy nikay chunav ki taiyaari ke bich aae haikort ke is faisle par rajy ke mukhymantri bhupesh baghel ne kaha hai ki rajy sarakar is faisle ka adhyyan karake adalt mein apana paksh rakhegi
unhoanne kaha, "adalt ne abhi  pratisht svikar kiyaa hai anusuchit jati ka jo ek pratisht badhayaa tha, use adalt ne svikar kar liyaa hai ab jo bacha huaa 1 pratisht hai, vah humaare pichhada varg ke lie tha, usake bare mein bhi sarakar apana paksh rakhegi"
chhattisgadh mein aadivasiyon ko  pratisht, anusuchit jati ko 1 pratisht aur any pichhada varg ko 1 pratisht aarakshn ka labh milta raha hai kuchh mahine pahale hi mein rajy sarakar ne anusuchit jati ke aarakshn mein ek pratisht ki badhottri ki thi yah sab mila kar rajy mein  pratisht aarakshn lagu tha 
iske bad isi sal 1 agast ko mukhymantri bhupesh baghel ne rajy mein any pichhada varg ke lie aarakshn ki simaa 1 pratisht se badha kar  pratisht karne ka faisla liyaa pichhle mahine ki  tarikh ko ek adhyaadesh jari kar ise lagu bhi kar diyaa gayaa tha
is tarah aarthik rup se kamazor savarnon ko bhi 1 pratisht aarakshn die jane ke bad rajy mein aarakshn ki simaa  pratisht ho gai thi
pichhada varg ko 1 ke bajae  pratisht aarakshn die jane ke chhattisgadh sarakar ke faisle ka pichhada varg ne desh bhar mein svagt kiyaa tha yahan tak ki is faisle ke lie mukhymantri bhupesh baghel ko chhattisgadh ke alaga-alag shaharon ke alava bihar aur dilli mein bhi sammaanit kiyaa gayaa tha lekin haikort ke taza aadesh ne sarakar ke nirny par saval khaade kar die haian 
sarakar ke aarakshn ke faisle ke khilaf yaachika dayr karne valon mein se ek kunal shukla ne bbc se kaha, "jatigt aarakshn ke alava purv sainik, divyaaang, svtantrta sangram senani aadi ko milne vale aarakshn ko joad dein to chhattisgadh mein aarakshn ki simaa  pratisht pahuanch gai thi yah sanvidhan ki mul bhavna ke khilaf hai"
unhoanne kaha ki haikort ka yah aadesh supraim kort aur sanvidhan ke praavdhan ke tahat hai 
kunal shukla ne kaha ki haikort ke faisle se rajy ke ek baade varg ko raht milegi

neshnal jyudishiyl epvyantmets kamishn aikt ko asanvaidhanik qrar dene vale jajameant mein  jastis josef kuriyn ne jab ye likha tha to iski ummid kam hi logon ko rahi hogi ek din usi supraim kort mein gautm navalakha ka maamla aaega aur ye saval phir se sabake samne hoga ki aakhir jaj bina koi vajah batae kyon sunvai se alag ho rahe haian
isi somvar  sitanbra ko pahale chif jastis ranjn gogoi, manglavar ko jastis enavi ramanna, jastis bi subhash reddi aur jastis biaar gavai, aur guruvar ko jastis raviandr bhat ne bhi gautm navalakha ke kes ki sunvai kar rahi beanch se alag hone ki ghoshna kar di

bhimaa koregaanv hiansa maamla girftari ke ek sal bad na to jamaant aur na hi sunvai
bhimaa koregaanv hiansa ke sal bhar bad kaisa hai hal
bhimaa koregaanv hiansa se pahale yalagar parishda mein kyaa huaa tha?
kisi kes ki sunvai se kisi jaj ka alag hona koi nai aur anuthi bat nahin hai iski nyaayik paranpra rahi hai aur ise dalilon ke aadhar par vajib thaharayaa ja sakata hai
supraim kort mein praaiktis karne vale edavoket surt sianh kahate hain, "kes se khud ko alag karate samay iski vajah batai jani chahie iski ek vajah hiton ka takarav ho sakata hai kai bar jaj atit mein bataur vakil kisi parti ke lie pairvi kar chuke hote haian agar jaj ko kisi qism ka koi khtara mahasus ho raha hai kes se kisi tarah ka juadav yaa maamle se juadi kisi parti se koi sanbandh ho to inmein se koi bhi vajah hoti hai lekin humein is maamle mein iski vajah nahin maalum hai" 
jyudishiyl praopraiti nyaayik maapdand ke staiandrd pahale se bane hue haian

isi sal fravari mein sibiaai ke aantrim dayrektr ke taur par em nageshvr rav ki niyukti ko chunauti dene vali yaachika par sunvai se chif jastis gogoi ne khud ko alag kar liyaa tha aur unake bad jastis sikri aur jastis enavi ramanna bhi is kes se hat gae the
halaanki tab unake hatane ki koi aadhikarik vajah nahin batai gai thi par bad mein ye batein samne aain ki chif jastis nae sibiaai dayrektr ko chunne ke lie bani selekshn kameti ka hissa the aur jastis sikri sibiaai dayrektr aalok varmaa ko hatane ki sifarish karne vale painl mein the 
jastis ramanna ne ye kahate hue maamle se khud ko alag kar liyaa tha ki "nageshvr rav mere grih rajy se hain aur main unaki beti ki shadi mein sharik ho chuka huan" 
kuchh sal pahale supraim kort mein pharmaa kanpni novartis kes par sunvai se pahale jastis maarkandey katju aur bad mein jastis dalavir bhandari ne khud ko alag kar liyaa tha tab novartis kes mein jastis katju ke ek purane lekh ka zikr aayaa tha jismein unhoanne bahurashtriy dava kanpniyon ko udarta se pharmaa peteant die jane ka virodh kiyaa tha 
iantelekchual praparti onars esosieshan ke ek iantrneshn kanfreans mein jastis bhandari ke bhag lene ke karn unhein svasthy karykartaon ke virodh ka samna karna paada tha daraasal, novartis is esosieshan ka hissa tha
maratha sena aur ist iandiyaa kanpni ke bich hue yuddh ki vin salgirh ke mauqe par 1 disanbr, 1 ke din bhimaa koregaanv shaury divs praerna abhiyaan ke bainr tale kai dalit sangthanon ne milkar ek raili aayojit ki thi is laadai mein ist iandiyaa kanpni ki taraf se mahar rejimeant laad rahi thi jismein zyaadatr dalit sainik the
bhimaa koregaanv ki raili maratha sena ke khilaf inhin daliton ki shaury ki yaad mein aayojit ki gai thi  iska nam yalagar parishd rakha gayaa shanivar vaada ke maidan par hui is raili mein loktantr, sanvidhan aur desh bachane ki bat kahi gai divangt chhatr rohit vemula ki maan radhika vemula ne raili ka udghatn kiyaa tha 
ismein kai nami hastiyaan msalana- prakash aaanbedkar, haikort ke purv chif jastis biji kolse patil, gujraat se vidhayk jignesh mevani, jeenayu chhatr umar khalid, aadivasi ektivist soni sori aadi maujud rahe inke bhashnon ke sath kabir kala manch ne saanskritik karykrm bhi pesh kie 
agale din jab bhimaa koregaanv mein utsv manayaa ja raha tha, aasa-pas ke ilaqon- msalan, sansavaadi mein hiansa bhaadk uthi aur ek naujvan ki jan chali gai is maamle mein hiandutvvadi sanstha samst hiand aghaadi ke neta miliand ekabote aur shiv pratishthan ke sansthapk sanbhaji bhiade ke khilaf bhi efaaiaar darj ki gai 
efaaiaar darj hone ke bad lanbe samay tak miliand ekabote aur sanbhaji bhiade ki girftari nahin hui, unhein zamaant par chhoad diyaa gayaa isi dauran yalagar parishd se juadi do aur efaaiaar pune shahar ke vishrambag pulis thane mein darj ki gaian 
pahali efaaiaar mein jignesh mevani aur umar khalid par bhaadkau bhashn dene ka aarop lagayaa gayaa tha dusri efaaiaar tushar damagude ki shikayt par yalagar parishd se juade logon ke khilaf darj ki gai is efaaiaar ke sanbandh mein jun mein sudhir dhavale samet paanch samaajik karyrtaon ko girftar kiyaa gayaa 
ise bad  agast ko pune pulis ne gautm navalakha, sudha bhardvaj, varavara rav, arun frera aur varnan gonzalvis ko girftar kar liyaa, ye sabhi log jane-maane samaajik aur maanvadhikar karykarta haian

subh ke aath baje hain aur hum baadvani zile ke bhilkheada gaanv mein rahane vale kailash aavasiyaa ke ghar pahuanche chuke haian 
apani bakariyon aur murgiyon ke sath kagazon se bhari ek moti si fail hathon mein lie kailash apane ghar ke daravaze par humaara iantzar kar rahe haian 
milte hi vah halka sa muskura kar hath milate haian lekin unake chehre par kisi lambi yaatra se nishphl lautne ki si udasi hai 
daraasal, saradar sarovr baandh ke dub kshetr mein aane vale apane kheton ke badale uchit muaavaze ke lie laad rahe kailash aavasiyaa ki laadai, is desh ki thaka deni vali nyaay vyvastha ke khilaf ek aam aadivasi ki laadai hai
kuchh hi der mein hum kailash ke kheton ki taraf nikl paadte haian bhilkheada gaanv se kuchh dur kapas aur arahar ke kheton se guzarate hue vah zamin ke ek talabnumaa tukade ke pas aakar ruk jate haian 
phir pani ki or ishara karate hue kahate hain, "yahan se vahan tak pura mera khet tha jo ab saradar sarovr baandh ke baik pani mein dub gayaa hai ab itna upar tak pani bhar gayaa hai to ye puri fsal bhi saad jaegi is tarah se eka-do din aur pani bhara raha to mera pura khet bhi retila ho jaega" 
kailash ke kheton ko adhigrhit karake 1 sal tak apane pas rakhane ke bad, narmda vaili divelpameant athariti yaa enavidie ne bina muaavaza die unaki dubi hui zamin ko vaps kar diyaa 
sal 1 mein unaki zamin ko dinotifai yaa lautate hue sarakar ne kaha ki unaki zamin dub mein nahin aa rahi jabaki zamin par aaj kailash ki  pratisht se zyaada zamin dub chuki hai 
visthapn niti ke anusar vah krishi ki zamin ke badale krishi ki zamin ke adhikari haian lekin nyaay bite 1 salon se bhart ki alaga-alag adalton mein apana muqdamaa laad rahe kailash ko apane paksh mein panch nyaayik aadesh jutane ke bad bhi, aaj tak zamin ka muaavaza nahin mila
muqdame se juade kagazat dikhate hue vah kahate hain, " mein jab bhuarjn huaa aur punrvas ki bat shuru hui thi, tabhi se humaari zamin aur purn punrvas ki maaang rahi hai sarakar se mere pas hath mein panch jajameant haian tin jiaarae griviyeans riadaresl authoriti yaa shikayt nivarn praadhikrana ke, ek supraim kort ka aur ek hai kort ka" 
"sarakar ke sare dakyumeant mere pas hain jo ye sabit karate hain ki unhoanne khud mujhe muaavaze ki patrta di hui hai lekin 1 sal hone ke bad bhi humako zamin ke badale zamin nahin mili ulta dubi hui zamin ko unhoanne dinotifai kar diyaa"
idhar saradar sarovr ki dub mein aayi apani zamin ke muaavaza ke lie salon se qanuni laadai laad rahe kunvr sianh, aath dinon tak apane dube hue ghar mein khaade rahe virodh jatane ke lie unhoanne janghrava gaanv mein bane apane pushtaini ghar ka sara samaan dub ke pani mein saadne diyaa 
apane dube hue ghar ke samne baith kar bat karate hue unhoanne kaha, "mera ghar dub chuka hai hum ismein aath roz pani mein khaade rahe humaari zamin aur kheti bhi dub gayi hai dub ke karn humaara pura ghar barbad ho gayaa ham aath roz pani mein islie khaade the kyoanki humein gussa tha humane soch liyaa tha ki jab tak humein zamin ke badale zamin nahin deange, tab tak hum pani mein khaade raheange lekin phir enavidie ke adhikari ghar aae aur unhoanne humein aashvasn diyaa kuchh sarve bhi kiyaa lekin ab tak vah aashvasn sirf aashvasn hi hai"  
dub aane ke bad se muaavaza ki in lambi qanuni laadaiyon se thak gae log ab narmda ghati mein beghr hue visthapiton ke lie bane 1 tin shed kaianps mein rahane ko majabur haian 
bbc ne baadvani zile mein bane soandhul tinshed kaimp nam ke ek aise hi kaimp ka daura kiyaa jahan filhal tin sau se zyaada parivar rahate haian sarakar ne saradar sarovr ki dub mein aae inke gaanvon se punrvasit karake inhein yahan basayaa tha lekin is tin shed kaimp ka ek baada hissa aaj bhi duba huaa hai 
amalali gaanv ki gaytri ko tin shed ke is nirash maahaul mein apana duba huaa ghar bahut yaad aata hai 
pashuon ke baade jaise chhote se shed mein sham ki sabzi banate hue gaytri kahati hain, "humaara kachcha makan tha lekin humein bahut pyaar tha khula khula aaangn tha vahaankhub jagah thi lekin vo ghar to humaara baandh ke pani mein dub gayaa abhi vahan se humako adhikari log bula kar yahan lae aur yahan tin shed mein lakr patak diyaa ab hum yahan kaise din bita rahe hain yah to hum hi jante hai" 
tin shed ke duruh jivn ke bare mein joadte hue gaytri kahati hain, "yahan par laitrin-bathrum jane mein dikqt hoti hai kyoanki koi thik vyvastha nahin hai islie shauch ke lie humein pahaad par jana paadta haian laken ab to vahan par bhi gandgi dikhne lagi hai barish hoti hai to vo puri gandgi pahaad se phislakar niche tin shed mein aati hai yahan koi kaise ji sakata hai?"
sarakar ne in asthayi kaimpon mein khane-pine ki vyvastha to ki hai lekin yahan rah rahe visthpiton ne humein batayaa ki unako diyaa jane vala khana bhi khane layq nahin hai
amalali gaanv ke hi ek visthapit batate hain, "rikshe mein khana aata hai aur sabako apane bartn lekr jana paadta hai aur lain mein lagana paadta hai lekin jo khana aata hai usamein mitti bhi aata hai, kankad bhi aata hai khane ki maatra bahut kam hoti hai har aadami ko sirf panch roti aur ek chammch dal dete hain" 
sabase gahari nirasha in kaimpon mein rahane ko majabur yuvaon mein haian baadvani zile ki rahane vali 1 sal ki jamuna chauhan ko skul bhi chhoadna paad gayaa apane dube hue ghar ko yaad karate hue unaki aankhon mein aansu tair jate haian "humaara ghar aur khet to sab dub gayaa, ab hum kahan raheange? yahan tin shed mein humaare sath humaari dadi hai -vo bhi bahut bimaar kuchh pata nahin chal raha ki humein yahan aise kab tak rahana paadega mujhe apane ghar ki bahut yaad aati hai"
enavidie aur rajy sarakar ke uchch adhikariyon ke pas pradesh ke in nirash yuvaon ko dene ke lie aashvasn ke siva kuchh bhi nahian 
"saradar sarovr se prabhavit sabhi vanchit parivaron ka dobara sarve karake unhein supraim kort dvara tay muaavaza diyaa jaega tin shed ek tatkalik asthayi vyvastha hai parivaron ke sampurn punrvas ke lie prayaas jari hain" - madhypradesh prashasn

1 ke vidhansabha chunavon ke apavad ke sath, shivsena aur bhajpa 1 ke bad se chunav laad rahe haian 1 se  ke vidhansabha chunavon mein shivsena paroksh rup se "baade bhai" ki bhumika mein rahi hai
shivsena netaon ne bar-bar kaha hai ki rajy ki rajniti mein ve ek baade bhai ki bhumika mein haian varishth patrkar yogesh pavar kahate hain, "lalkrishn aadavani humesha shivsena se kahate the ki vah shivsena ram hai aur hum lakshmn haian islie, ye bhi sach hai ki bijepi shivsena ko maharashtr mein baada bhai maanti thi" 
lekin ab yah samikran badalata dikh raha hai is sal ke chunav mein shivsena ko 1 sitein mili haian gathabandhn ke itihas mein pahali bar, shivsena ko 1 se kam sitein di gai haian parinamsvrup, yah bahas shuru ho gai hai ki kyaa shivsena ab aadhikarik taur par chhota bhai hai
varishth patrkar prakash akolkar kahate hain, "bhajpa ke pas  mein  sitein thin jabaki 1 mein use 1 sitein milian yaani bhajpa ko shivsena ke sath bina gathabandhn ke bhi  ke mukable tin guna zyaada saphalata hasil hui" 
"dusri or,  aur 1 ki tulna ki jae to shivsena ko  se  sitein hi hasil huian usi samay, shivsena chhota bhai ban gai thi"
akolkar ka kahana hai ki 1 mein, shivsena ne bhi apratyksh rup se svikar kar liyaa ki vo ek chhota bhai hai
akolkar kahate hain, "shivsena ne kaangres-enasipi se adhik sitein hasil kin aur 1 mein apane dam par chunav laadne ke bad pramukh vipkshi parti ban gai aur ekanath shiande vipkshi neta ban gae lekin ek mahine bad hi shivsena ne ghutne tek die aur gathabandhn sarakar mein shamil ho gai"
bharatakumaar raut maharashtr taims ke purv rajnitik sanpadk hain aur varishth rajnitik vishleshk haian vah shivsena ke rajysabha saansd bhi the 
ve kahate hain, "1 ke chunavon mein, donon dalon ne alaga-alag laadai laadi aur bhajpa ko shivsena ki lagabhag doguni sitein milian isi ki vajah se baada bhai chhota bhai ka samikran hi badal gayaa"
maharashtr chunav kamazor ho chuki enasipi mein kitna dam baqi hai?
raut kahate hain, "shivsena-bhajpa gathabandhn ke sutr pramod mahajn aur balasaheb thakre ke shabdon par aadharit the koi nishchit pharmula nahin tha donon ek sath baithkar charcha kareange aur donon paksh sahumat ho gae" 
prakash akolkar kahate hain, "bhajpa keandr mein satta chahti thi ve maharashtr mein satta mein dilchaspi nahin rakhate the jab pramod mahajn ne 11-11 pharmule ka istemaal kiyaa, iske pichhe unhein keandr mein satta lane ke lie shivsena ka samarthn aur maharashtr mein parti ke vistar ka uddeshy tha"
bhart kumaar raut kahate haian "shivsena pratishtha chahti thi jabaki bhajpa kevl shahari, madhym varg ki parti thi islie bhajpa ko apani parti ko aage le jana tha islie donon dal ek sath aae shivsena logon tak pahuanch gai thi aur balasaheb thakre ke pas netritv ka gun tha bhajpa ke pas aisa netritv nahin tha aur aisi sthiti  tak bani rahi iske bad sab badal gayaa"
" mein pahali bar bhajpa ne kam siton par chunav laadkar adhik saansd jiti usi vaqt, bijepi havi ho gai"
kahin enasipi mein akele to nahin rah jaeange sharad pavar?
bhart kumaar raut kahate hain, "shivsena ek sangthan ke rup mein kamazor nahin hui shivsena ek sangthan ke rup mein majabut thi isi dauran bhajpa bhi vistar kar rahi thi shivsena apani rananiti mein kamazor paad gai shivsena apani chunavi saphalata badha nahin pai"
prakash akolkar kahate hain, "shivsena ka hath thamne se, pramod mahajn ne maharashtr mein bhajpa ka vistar kiyaa jabaki shivsena bhajpa ka hath pakaadkar jyaada vistar nahin kar pai"
vo kahate hain, "shivsena ne 1 se 1 ko chhoadkar humesha vipksh ki rajniti ki hai lekin shivsena ye ravaiyaa banae nahin rakh pai isi vajah se usane vipksh ki rajniti karne ka phaisla liyaa lekin janata samajh nahin pai is chunav mein shivsena ki is bhumika ka phaisla hoga"
vo aage kahate hain, "shivsena ne apamaanjanak rup se gathabandhn kiyaa hai kahin bhi  pratisht pharmula lagu nahin huaa use 1 siton par pura dhyaan lagakr adhik se adhik sitein jitni hoangi"
1 mein bhajpa rashtriy karykarini ne maharashtr mein shivsena ke sath gathabandhn banane ka phaisla kiyaa shivsena-bhajpa gathabandhn ne donon dalon ko kaangres aur phir maharashtr mein gathit rashtrvadi kaangres parti ko ek sanyukt chunauti dene lage
halaanki 1 ke loksabha chunav mein shivsena aur bhajpa gathabandhn ke rup mein samne aae, lekin maharashtr ko phatah nahin kar pae 
1 mein maharashtr mein vidhansabha chunav hue jismein shivsena aur bhajpa mein chunavi gathabandhn huaa
in chunavon mein, shivsena ne 1 siton aur bhajpa ne 1 siton par chunav laada tha
maharashtr vidhansabha chunavon mein donon partiyon ke bich siton ki sajhedari ka ek pharmula 1 mein bhi vaisa hi rakha gayaa tha halaanki bad ke chunav mein  gathabandhn ke frmule badalate dikhai die aur yahin se shivsena ke chhote bhai aur baade bhai ki kahani samne aati hai
1 mein, shivsena ne sahayogi dalon ko 11 mein se 1 sitein di thian  mein, shivsena ne sahayogiyon ko  aur bhajpa ko  sitein di thian  mein, shivsena ne apane sahayogiyon ko nau sitein dian
1 mein pahali bar gathabandhn ke itihas mein bhajpa aur shivsena ne alag alag rasta apanayaa aur  varshon mein pahali bar donon dal ek dusre ke khilaf maidan mein utare
bhajpa ne  siton par aur shivsena ne  siton par chunav laada 
halaanki, 1 mein bijepi ne  siton mein se 1 sitein jitin aur shivsena ne  mein se  siton par jit darj ki
ab 1 mein bijepi aur shivsena phir se gathabandhn mein laad rahe haian bijepi 1 siton sahayogiyon ki 1 siton ko chhoadkara par chunav laad rahi hai, jabaki shivsena 1 siton par chunav laad rahi hai

rajy mein ek sau pharenrs traibyunl pahale se hi chal rahein hai lekin bite 1 agast ko enaaarasi ki phainl list prakashit hone ke bad sarakar ne aur  nae traibyunl ka gathan kiyaa hai 
guvahati hai kort ke nyaaydhishon ke ek painl ne hal hi mein pharenrs trabyunl ke 1 sadasyon ka chayan kiyaa hai 
matalab ye ki pahale ke jin 1 traibyunl mein meanbra-jaj nahin the un padon ko bhi bhara gayaa hai keandriy grih mantraly ne hal hi mein asam mein 1 atirikt traibyunl ki sthapna ko manzuri di hai 
lekin in arddhnyaayik vyvastha vale pharenrs traibyunl ke kamkaj ko lekr lagatar saval uthate rahe haian 
daraasal, qanun ke jankaron ka ye maanna hai ki pharenrs traibyunl mein ritaryd jajon ki niyukti honi chahie varna nagrikta ki apil karne vale logon ko nyaay milne mein pareshani hogi
abhayaapuri sab divijnal kort mein sal  se praaiktiks kar rahe edavoket afzal husain ne bbc se kaha, "main avaidh pravasi nirdharna adhiniym 1 yaani aaiemaditi qanun ke samay se pharenrs traibyunl mein maamle laad raha huan" 
"daraasal, sarakar ko in traibyunl mein ritaryd jajon ki niyukti karni chahie thi, lekin jab se nae vakilon ko bataur meanbr niyukt kiyaa gayaa hai vahan kam thik se nahin chal raha hai" 
"mere ek muvvkil ne apani nagrikta se juade sare kagazat abhayaapuri ephati mein jamaa karava die hain, us par bahas bhi ho chuki hai lekin tin sal ke bad bhi ab tak us maamle mein koi faisla nahin aayaa hai main har mahine yaachika dayr karata hun lekin ephati meanbr koi rdr nahin de rahein haian is vajah se mere muvvkil tanav mein haian"
pratyek ephati ka netritv ephati adhiniym, 11 aur ephati rdr 1 ke tahat niyukt jajon ki niyukti ki jati hai jinhein pharenrs traibyunl ka meanbr kaha jata hai
lekin edavoket afzal husain ke anusar ephati meanbr ke praotokl ko bhale hi ek jaj ki haisiyt se milakr dekha jata hai lekin in meanbron ke kam karne ke taur tariqon mein kafi kamiyaan haian 
afzal husain kahate hain, "ek jaj yaa phir ritaryd jaj ke pas qanuni anubhv hota hai aur ve ek prakriyaa ke maadhym se kisi maamle ko sunte hain, usase juade dastavezon ki jaanch karate hai, vo karypaddhti ephati meanbr ke kam mein dekhne ko nahin milti jabaki in ephati ko kisi vykti ki nagrikta se juade faisle lene hote haian"
daraasal, edavoket afzal husain ke  sal ke muvvkil abdul qadr ephati ke samaksh ek aise hi maamle mein ulajhe hue haian jab bbc ne qadr se sanprk kiyaa to unhoanne batayaa, "mere pas 1 se lekr nagrikta se juade sare dastavez haian ephati kort ne jo bhi kagzat maaange the, maianne vo sare kagzat jamaa karavaen haian" 
"is maamle ko tin sal ho chuke hain lekin ab tak koi faisla nahin aayaa hai is maamle ki vajah se mera aur mere bachchon ka nam enaaarasi mein nahin aayaa hai main bahut pareshan huan pratyek tarikh par abhayaapuri jana paadta hai kort ke chakkr lagane ke lie paisa kahan se laean"
vo aage kahate hai, "mere tin bete hain aur ek beti hai patni ka nam enaaarasi ki phainl list mein aayaa hai lekin hum paanch logon ka nam nahin hai mere donon bete graijuet hain lekin enaaarasi mein nam nahin hone ke karn ve naukri ke lie kahin aavedn nahin kar pa rahein haian hum bhartiy hain aur pratyek chunav mein vot dalte haian" 
abdul qadr ne batayaa, "lekin enaaarasi ke karn hum sabaka bhavishy khatare mein paad gayaa hai tin sal se humaara pura parivar teanshn mein din gujar raha hai maianne apane vakil se kah diyaa hai, chahe svdeshi ho yaa videshi, humaara faisla karava dijie"
supraim kort ke ritaryd jaj madan bi lokur ne hal hi mein nai dilli ke iandiyn sosaiti aaph iantrneshnal la mein aayojit pipuls traibyunla namk ek karykrm mein spsht kaha tha, "asam mein pharenrs traibyunl ek manamaane tarike se kam kar rahe haian ye traibyunls apani prakriyaaon aur kamkaj ko apane dam par viksit kar rahe haian" 
"inmein kisi bhi tarah ki ekarupta nahin hai yahi karn hai ki do-tihai aadesh ekapakshiy hue hain kyoanki unake kamkaj mein ekarupta nahin hai garib aur anapadh log jatil prakriyaaon ko samajh nahin pate hain aur namon ki vartni mein maamuli galatiyon ne hajaron logon ko nagrikta ki aantim suchi se bahr kar diyaa hai"
isi pipuls traibyunla karykrm mein maujud samaajik karykarta tista sitlavaad ne bhi kaha, "traibyunl ke kamkaj mein dharmik aur bhashai aadhar ka ek paitrn hai sabase ahum bat ye hai ki pharenrs traibyunls ke meanbr ka karykal aur unake vetn aur bhatte pratyksh taur par sarakar ke faisle par nirbhr hota hai"
grih vibhag ki ek jankari ke anusar, shuru mein yahan 11 avaidh pravasi nirdharn nyaayaadhikran aaiemaditi the lekin supraim kort ne sal  mein avaidh pravasiyon nyaayaadhikranon dvara nirdharna adhiniym, 1 yaani aaiemaditi kanun ko radd kar diyaa tha jiske bad inhein ephati mein parivrtit kar diyaa gayaa 
iske bad sarakar ne 1 mein aur 1 ephati ka gathan kiyaa bad mein tatkalin mukhymantri tarun gogoi ki sarakar ne ephati mein jamaa hue maamlon ko niptane ke lie rajy mein traibyunls ki kul sankhyaa sau kar di in videshi traibyunls ke kamkaj ko lekr shuru mein kisi tarah ka vivad nahin tha 
kyoanki us samay inki sankhyaa kam thi aur inmein jyaadatr ritaryd jajon ko niyukt kiyaa gayaa tha lekin 1 ke bad se kaphi sankhyaa mein vakilon ko ephati meanbr ke taur par niyukt kiyaa gayaa aur tabhi se ephati ka kamkaj savalon ke ghere mein hai 
in traibyunls ke faislon ko lekr khaskar bangali bolne vale hiandu aur muslamaan donon mein narazagi hai daraasal enaaarasi se bahr hue 1 lakh se adhik logon ko ab apani nagrikta sabit karne ke lie ephati kort mein apil karni hogi 
ek jankari ke anusar in 1 lakh logon mein karib 1 lakh bangali bolne vale hiandu hai jabaki karib  lakh muslamaan hai kyaa ephati kort ki maujuda vyvastha mein itni baadi tadad mein apil karne vale logon ko aasani se apani nagrikta sabit karne ka mauka mil paega? 
is saval ka javab dete hue gvalpaada jila adalt mein lanbe samay se praaiktiks kar rahe edavoket nazarul islam kahate hain, "pharenrs traibyunls ki maujuda vyvastha mein apil karne vale logon ke lie prakriyaa sahaj nahin hogi ismein logon ko kaphi pareshani ka samna karna hoga" 
"iska karn hai ki logon ko enaaarasi ki list se bahr kiyaa gayaa hai lekin unaki nagrikta ab bhi khatm nahin hui hai unhein videshi nahin banayaa gayaa hai lekin jab ye log pharenrs traibyunls ke samaksh apil kareange us samay kaphi pareshani hone vali hai kyoanki pharenrs traibyunl ke meanbr ki bhumika nishpksh nahin hai" 
dhubadi zila adalt mein bite  sal se praaiktiks kar rahe varishth vakil abdul manan ka kahana hai, "traibyunl ko kort nahin kaha ja sakata vo ek karyaaly hai ve log n majistret hai aur n hi jaj haian jab tak ephati mein ritaryd jajon ki niyukti nahin ki jaegi tabatak ephati se nishpksh phaisle ki ummid nahin ki ja sakati"
halaanki guvahati hai kort ke varishth vakil kamal nayan chaudhri ko ephati vyvastha mein kanuni taur par koi kami najar nahin aati vo kahate hain, "puri duniyaa mein jab avaidh videshi nagrik ka pata lagayaa jata hai to usamein nyaayik aur arddh nyaayik prakriyaa ki aavashkta nahin hoti hai is kam ko karypalika ke log karate haian" 
"kevl asam mein hi iske viprit ho raha hai kanun mein jab videshi hone ki bat aati hai to us vykti ko khud yah sabit karna hota hai ki vo videshi nahin hai abhi rajy mein ephati prakriyaa ke jarie jo kam ho raha hai vo puri tarah kanuni hai aur us par saval uthana kahin se bhi sahi nahin hai" 
kaangres ke varishth neta evn asam ke tin bar lagatar mukhymantri rahe tarun gogoi ke karykal mein hi pharenrs traibyunl ki sankhyaa mein ijapha kiyaa gayaa tha, lekin ab ve khud ephati ki bhumika par saval utha rahein hai gogoi kahate hain, "asam mein pharenrs tribyunl jis kadar kam kar rahein hai usase logon ko nyaay nahin mil raha hai" 
"ephati kabhi kisi phauji ko videshi bana dete haian koi pulis adhikari hai to use videshi bana diyaa ja raha hai ye traibyunl nyaayik nikay ki tarah kam nahin kar rahein hai supraim kort ke purv jaj bhi bol rahein hai ki ye ephati sanvaidhanik athariti nahin hai maanv adhikar ke log bhi saval utha rahein haian"
ab saval yah bhi uth rahein hai ki pradesh mein mahaz  ephati 1 lakh se adhik logon ki nagrikta par phaisla lene mein kitna samay leange? iska javab dete hue bhartiy janata parti ke varishth neta vijy gupta kahate hain, "enaaarasi mein nam nahin aane ka matalab ye nahin hai ki vo vykti videshi hai"
"philhal rajy mein  ephati hain aur humaari sarakar aane vale dinon mein inki sankhyaa ek hajar karne vali hai lihaja log apane dastavej lekr ephati mein ja sakeange aur apana paksh rakh sakeange jahan tak saval ephati ke kamkaj ko lekr hai to guvahati hai kort ke varishth jajon ka painl ephati meanbr ka chayan karata hai" 
"ismein sarakar ka koi hath nahin hota yah puri tarah ek qanuni prakriyaa ke tahat hota hai iske alava jin logon ko ephati mein apil karne ke bad qanuni madad ki zarurt paadgi to humaari sarakar ne har zile mein nishulk qanuni madad karne ki vyvastha ki hai"
enaaarasi rajy samanvyak karyaaly ne hal hi mein jankari di hai ki jin logon ke nam enaaarasi ki phainl list mein shamil nahin kie gae hai un logon ko jald se jald karn batate hue pramaanit dastavez bheje jaeange taki ve ephati ke samaksh apani apil dayr kar sakean 
halaanki yah apil prakriyaa kab se shuru hogi ispar kuchh nahin kaha gayaa hai lekin enaaarasi se nam kharij vale dastavez praapt karne ke bad logon ke pas ephati mein apil karne ke lie 1 din ka samay rahega
lekin varishth vakil abdul manan ka kahana hai, "ephati ke pas ab jo 1 lakh logon ki apil aaegi usako 1 din mein niptana kisi bhi tarah sanbhv nahin hai ephati ke kamkaj ka ab tak jo tarika raha hai, is tarah to itne maamlon ko niptane ke lie agale  sal bhi kam paad jaeange"

is do aktubr ko mahatmaa gaandhi par ek lekh pradhanmantri nareandr modi ka bhi chhapa sidhe nyuyrk taims mein bhart aur gaandhi ko duniyaa ki zarurt kyon hai?lekin isi din tvitr par jo haishtaig treand kar raha tha, godse amar rahean
beshk, is haishtaig par aane vale bahut sare tvit gaandhi ko maanne valon ke bhi the jinhein godse ki amarata ka nara pasand nahin aa raha tha, lekin phir bhi is haishtaig ka is tarah treand karna kyaa batata hai? ve kaun log hain jo gaandhi ki 1vin jayanti par godse ko jilana chahte hain? bhart mein yah nai tvitr pidhi kahan se aa gai jo gaandhi ke hatyaare ki murtiyaan bana rahi hai, usaki puja kar rahi hai aur usako devta banane par tuli hai? 
yah aarop lagana aasan hai ki is kam mein bijepi ke kai neta aur saansd bhi lage dikhai paadte haian nathuram godse ki deshbhakti ko lekr bijepi saansd prajna thakur ke vichar sun kar pradhanmantri ne bhi kaha ki ve jivn mein unako dil se kabhi maaf nahin kar paeange
lekin is bahas mein ulajheange ki bijepi ne kyaa kaha aur kaangres ne kyaa kiyaa, to vah sutr kho jaega, jiske sahare yah samajha ja sakata hai ki aakhir gaandhi is desh ki kis mitti se paida huaa tha ki qbra mein samaata hi nahin- bar-bar nikl kar bahr aa jata hai khud gaandhi ji kaha karate the ki ve sava sau sal tak jina chahte hain aur apani qbra se bhi aavaz dete raheange
hiandi ke ek gitkar ke bhitr yah bahut talkh maayusi hai ki gaandhi ke dedh sau tukade kar die gae hain to bahut sare logon ke bhitr yah afsos hai ki unake hatyaare nathuram godse ki deshbhakti ko yah desh nahin samajh raha hai
daraasal, yahin se vah daravni phaank aur phaans shuru hoti hai jo gaandhi aur godse, desh aur manushyta aur rashtr aur rashtrvad ke bich ki samajh yaa nasmajhi ka fasla batati hai aur yah bhi yaad dilati hai ki gaandhi ka nam japate-japate unhein murti mein badal dene aur godse ko pujte-pujte use devta banane ki pariyojna lagabhag sath-sath chal rahi hai
chahein to yaad kar sakate hain ki pichhle tamaam dashakon mein godse ke praet ka aahvan karate hue ek mantr-sadhna jaise lagatar ki jati rahi hai aur yah taulne ki koshish bhi hoti rahi hai ki is praet ko desh apane pitr ki tarah svikar karata hai yaa nahian
dusri taraf, ek asuvidhajnak gaandhi ko chhoadkar ek suvidhajnak gaandhi taiyaar kiyaa ja raha hai jisse kisi vaicharik muthbhead ki naubt n aae yah kata-chhanta, chikna-sa gaandhi draiang rum ki mez ke lie hai, aur ghar ke bhitr jo pujaghr hai, usamein godse ki praan-pratishtha hogi
lekin aisa kahane ka aadhar kyaa hai? iska aadhar gaandhi-vichar ki vo vyaakhyaaen hain jo ki ja rahi haian msalan, yah sach hai ki gaandhi gay ko maante the ve chahte the ki gokshi n ho lekin unhoanne saf kah diyaa ki ve gay ko bachane ke lie iansan ki jan nahin le sakate, unhoanne gobhkton se kaha ki ve gay ko bachane ke lie apani jan de dein, lekin muslamaan ki jan n lean
isi tarah gaandhi gaanvon ko shaharon ki kripa par nirbhr upanivesh nahin banana chahte the- ve ek gramin bhart chahte the yah sapana vaki dushvar hai unake jite-ji nehru aur aanbedkar isse asahumati jatate rahe, lekin ve phir bhi gaandhi ka mol samajhate the aur asahumati ko gaandhi-vichar ka hissa hi maante the gaandhi aur nehru ke bich ki bahasein dekh lijie- yah bat baadi aasani se samajh mein aa jaegi
lekin ab sarakar gaandhi se bahas nahin karati, vah unaki puja karati hai yah vaisi hi puja hai jaisi sare pap dhone ke lie ki jati hai devtaon ke sath lekin ek mushkil yaa aasani yah hai ki ve bahut dur hain, unaki gavahi nahin li ja sakati gaandhi itne dur nahin hain, islie unaki gavahi mil jati hai aur phailae ja rahe jhuth ki kalai khul jati hai
gaandhi jaisa dushvar rashtrvadi milna mushkil hai jab pure desh mein aadhikarik nagrikta suchi ke bahane videshiyon ko khojne aur bahr karne ki muhim ke nam par ek chhupe hue alpsankhyk virodh ko hava di ja rahi hai tab yah kitna avishvsaniy lagata hai ki gaandhi videshiyon ki hi nahin, apane aakraanta samaaj ki jan-maal ki raksha ko lekr itne sanvednashil the ki ve sabaka virodh sahate hue bhi iski nianda kar sakate the 
rajmohn gaandhi ki kitab mohnadas batati hai ki jaliyaaanvala bag hatyaakaand ke bad 11 mein amritsar mein hi hue kaangres ke adhiveshn mein jab is hatyaakaand ka nianda prastav layaa gayaa to gaandhi ji ne ismein un paanch aangrejon ki hatyaa ki nianda ka prastav bhi juadvayaa jo is hatyaakaand se kuchh din pahale amritsar mein maar die gae the
pure adhiveshn mein isko lekr hangamaa ho gayaa yah ulahna diyaa gayaa ki yah kisi bhartiy maan ki kokh se janmi santan ka prastav nahin ho sakata gaandhi ne kaha- yah prastav kisi bhartiy maan ki kokh se janmi santan ka hi ho sakata hai yah prastav unaka hai
godse par lautean godse ke hath mein vah pistaul thi jisse gaandhi ko goli maari gai lekin godse ka hath gaandhi ki disha mein moadne vale hath kaun the- yah kisi se chhupa nahin hai, saradar patel bata gae hain ki gaandhi ki hatyaa us zaharile maahaul ke karn hui jise sangh ne taiyaar kiyaa tha
asagar vajaht ne apane ek natk mein kalpna ki hai ki godse ki goli se gaandhi ki maut nahin hui, ve ghayl hue unhoanne godse ki phaansi ka virodh kiyaa godse ko dilli ki jel mein rakh diyaa gayaa thik hokr gaandhi ek sudur gaanv mein apane loktantr ka prayog karne lage
yah prayog kaangresi sarakar ko itna nagvar guzara ki unako girftar karne ki naubt aa gai gaandhi ne maaang ki ki unhein bhi usi sel mein rakha jae jismein godse hai gaandhi ki zid ke aage sarakar ko phir ghutne tekne paade
asali kahani daraasal yahan se shuru hoti hai gaandhi aur godse ek hi sel mein haian gaandhi lagatar sanvad ki koshish karate hain, godse lagatar unase bachata hai gaandhi godse se puchhte hain, tumhari praiy kitab kaun hai
godse batata hai ki gita usaki praiy kitab hai gaandhi batate hain ki gita unaki bhi praiy kitab hai phir ve kahate hain, jis kitab ne tumhein mujhe maarne ki praerna di, usi ne mujhe yah sikhayaa ki main tumhein kshmaa kar duan
to jivn ke mahabhart mein apani-apani gita apane-apane dhang se hum sabako padhni hai yah hum par nirbhr karata hai ki hum manushyta ke paksh mein khaade hon yaa manushy virodhi tarkon ke qile mein apana ghar banaen, hum gaandhi se khijte hue, naraz hote hue bhi, unase ek purkhe ki tarah apana nata joadein yaa godse ko chupke se apana devta maanna shuru kar dean 
goliyon se gaandhi mare nahin, murtiyon se godse zianda nahin hoga lekin yah sach hai ki jis tarah godse ki bar-bar praan-pratishtha ki ja rahi hai, jis tarah gaandhi ko unaki puja karake svchchhta ke dut ki bhumika mein sameta ja raha hai, usase yah aashanka hoti hai ki log kahin godse ki hi vichardhara ko plastik sarjri ke zarie gaandhi n bana dalean 
lekin iske lie asali gaandhi ko gayb karna hoga to jis vichardhara ne gaandhi ki hatyaa ki, vah ab unaka apaharan karne par tuli hai halaanki gaandhi ab bhi itne vazani hain ki unase nahin utheange

bbc nyuz ke sath ek sakshatkar mein maaikrospht ke mukhy karykari satyaa nadela ne kaha ki rashtriy surksha chiantaon ke bavjud, chin se alag hona zyaada nuksan pahuanchaega
unhoanne kaha, "aartiphishl iantelijeans ke bahut sare shodh khuleaam hote hain aur duniyaa ko isse mili jankari ka labh bhi mil raha hai"
unhoanne batayaa, "mere lie yah punrjagran kal aur vaijnanik kraanti ke bad sabase baada sach hai islie mujhe lagata hai ki agar chin ke sath shodh aur anushandhan par pabandi lagai gain to isse sthiti mein sudhar ke bajae nuksan zyaada hoga"
chin mein maaikrospht ka pahala daftr iske sansthapk aur tatkalin siio bil gets ne 1 mein khola tha bijiang sthit iske hedkvartr mein  se adhik vaijnanik aur  se adhik vijitiang sklar evn chhatr karyrat haian maaikrospht is samay any kamon ke alava mashin larniang ke shodhkartaon ki bharti kar raha hai
apraail mein phaineanshiyl taims ne khbar di thi ki maaikrospht ke shodhkarta chin ke neshnal yunivrsiti f dipheans teknolji ki timon ke sath mil kar aartiphishiyl iantelijeans praojekt par kam kar rahe haian halaanki, kuchh bahri paryvekshkon ne chetavni di hai ki iska galat istemaal kiyaa ja sakata hai
ripblikn sinetr ted kruz ne samaachar patr se kaha ki "amariki kanpniyon ko yah samajhane ki zarurt hai ki chin mein vyaapar karna mahatvpurn aur kaphi jokhim bhara hota hai"
unhoanne kaha, "amariki kanpniyon ko chin ki kamyunist parti jasusi ka nishana bana sakati hain, iske alava chin ki kamyunist parti ke dvara maanvadhikar ke ullanghn ko badhava dene ka jokhim bhi amariki kanpniyon par badh raha hai"
nadela ne is jokhim ka anumaan hai unhoanne bbc se kaha, "hum jante hain ki koi bhi nai takanik yaa to ek upay ho sakati hai yaa phir hathiyaar"
unhoanne kaha, "saval ye hai ki aap ise kaise sunishchit kar sakate ki ye hathiyaar nahin baneange? mujhe lagata hai ki iske lie kai tarike haian pahali bat to yah ki ek nirmaata ke rup mein humein yah sunishchit karne ke lie naitik siddhaanton ko paln karna chahie ki hum jo eaai bana rahe hain vah is tarah surkshit ho ki koi us par shasn n kar sake aur n hi usaka kisi ek paksh ki taraph koi jhukav ho"
unhoanne batayaa ki unhein lagata hai ki unaki kanpni ka vivadaspd nai takanik ke istemaal par paryaapt niyantrn hai sath hi unhoanne yah bhi batayaa ki kanpni ne chin aur anytr kahin aisi kisi bhi pariyojnaon mein shamil hone se iankar kar diyaa hai jo use anuchit, takaniki rup se asakshm yaa naitik rup se chiantit karne vali lagi thi

puri duniyaa mein shiyaa muslamaanon ke sabase pavitr sthl karbla mein is tim ne char maulviyon se mulaqat ki charon maulviyon ko gupt rup se filmaayaa gayaa tin nikah muta ke lie mahilaen upalabdh karane ke lie taiyaar hue inmein se do maulvi ne kaha ki vo nikah muta ke lie yuva laadkiyaan deange
bagadad mein ek maulvi saiyyd rad ne bbc ke aandrakavar riportr ko batayaa ki shariyaa qanun ke tahat nikah muta ke lie koi tay samay simaa nahin rakhi gai hai
ve kahate hain, "ek purush chahe jitni bhi mahilaon se nikah muta kar sakata hai aap ek laadki se aadhe ghante ke lie nikah kar sakate hain aur jaise hi yah khtm hota hai aap turant dusra nikah kar sakate haian"
jab apani paadtal mein bbc ne sayyd rad se puchha ki kyaa ek nabaliga laadki se nikah muta kiyaa jana svikary hai, to unhoanne javab diyaa, "bas savdhan rahein ki vo apani varjiniti n khoe"

jab unase puchha gayaa ki agar laadki ko chot lag gai to kyaa hoga, maulvi ne apana kandha jhatakate hue kaha ki, "yah aapake aur usake bich hai ki vah kitna dard sah sakati hai"
karbla ke ek maulvi shekh salavi se sikret kaimre par puchha gayaa ki nikah muta ke lie 1 sal ki bachchi svikary hai to unhoanne kaha, "han, nau sal se upar ki laadki mein koi samsyaa nahin hai shariyaa ke mutabiq ismein koi samsyaa nahin hai"
saiyyd rad ki tarah hi unhoanne bhi kevl yahi kaha ki laadki ka kaumaary nahin tutna chahie phorple ki anumti hai aur yadi nabaliga laadki ne apani sahumati de di to apraakritik yaun sanbandh svikary hai itna dhyaan rakhate hue aap jo chahein kar sakate haian"
maulvi saiyyd rad to bina laadki se mile fon par hi yah nikah karavane ko razi ho gae aandrakavar riportr ke samne vo taiksi mein baith kar fon par vo laadki se puchhte hain ki kyaa use yah nikah qbul hai unhoanne ek din ke nikah ke lie use dedh lakh dinar ke raqm ka fr diyaa aant mein unhoanne kaha, "ab aap donon ka nikah ho gayaa hai sath rahana halal hai"
unhoanne kuchh minton ke is nikah ke lie aandrakavar riportr se  dalar lie aur is dauran unamein kalpnik laadki ko lekr koi chianta nahin dikhi
ajanabiyon se yaun sanbandh banane mein nikah muta ka istemaal karne vale ek shadishuda vykti ne bbc se kaha, "1 sal ki laadki milna beshqimti hai kyoanki vah ab bhi phresh hai lekin vah mahangi milegi, qrib  se  dalar ke bich, aur is umr ki laadki ke sath kevl maulvi hi nikah muta kara sakate haian"
unaka maanna hai ki iske lie unhein dharmik maanyta praapt hai ve kahate hain, "agar dharm se juada ek vykti yah kahata hai ki nikah muta halal hai to aisa karna pap nahin maana ja sakata"
iraq mein mahilaon ke aashry ka netvark chalane vali mahila adhikar karykarta yaanr mohmmd kahati hain ki laadkiyon ko iansanon ki bajay bechne ki vastu maana jata hai
ve kahati hain, "ismein laadkiyon ko kuchh khas tariqe se istemaal karne ki anumti hai lekin unaki varjiniti ko bacha kar rakha jata hai taki bhavishy mein unase baadi kamaai ho baadi kamaai ka matalab shadi hai"
ve kahati hain, "jab ek laadki ki varjiniti pahale hi khtm ho chuki hoti hai to use vivah ke yogy nahin dekha jata aur is bat ka khtara bhi rahata hai ki kahin usaka parivar use maar n dale chahe jo bhi ho qimt to laadki aur mahilaon ko hi chukani paadti hai"
dakyumeandri mein gupt rup se maulviyon ke sath batchit ko filmaayaa gayaa ismein vo nabaliga laadkiyon ko nikah muta ke lie dene ke lie apani tatprata dikha rahe haian

tim ne ek us maulvi ko filmaayaa jisne aandrakavar riportr ke samne us laadki ki numaaish ki jise usane  ghante ke nikah muta ke lie khrida tha

daraasal, bhart rus se ek misail sistm khridne vala hai - jiska nam hai esa- lekin amariki adhikariyon ka kahana hai ki agar bhart ne ye khridari ki, to us par amariki pratibandh lagane ka khtara hai
iska matalab ye hai ki amarika aur rus ke bich ki tanatni ka khamiyaaza bhart ko bhugtana paad sakata hai 
halaanki amarika daure par gae bhart ke videsh mantri es jayashankr ne kaha tha ki unhein lagata hai ki vo is saude ke lie amarika ko mana leange, lekin usi din amariki videsh mantraly ne d hiandu akhbar ko imel ke zarie batayaa ki aisa koi bhi sauda bhart ke lie musibt ban sakata hai aur amarika us par pratibandh laga sakata hai
is imel mein amariki videsh mantraly ke ek pravakta ne likha, "hum apane sahayogiyon se apil karate hain ki vo rus ke sath koi bhi aisa sauda karne se bachein,  jiski vajah se un par kauantriang amarikaz adavarsrij thru saiankshans ekt ke tahat pratibandh lagane ka khtara ho"
aisa nahin hai ki amarika aur bhart ke rishton mein koi tanav aa gayaa hai yaa ye pratibandh khas taur par bhart ke lie hai daraasal, ye pratibandh har us desh par lagu hoange jo amarika ke katsa qanun ka ullanghn karega 
jaisa ki is qanun ke nam se hi samajh aata hai ki amarika is qanun ke zarie apane virodhiyon par dabav banata hai aur unake saude tuadvane ki koshish karata hai amarika ke ghoshit virodhi hain rus, iran aur uttr koriyaa 
rus ke maamle mein amarika ka yah qanun un deshon ko rokta hai jo rus ke sath hathiyaaron ka sauda karate haian
donld tranp ke satta mein aane ke bad amariki sansd ne 1 mein is qanun ko pas kiyaa tha
 agast 1 ko jab se ye qanun lagu huaa hai tab se hi bhart mein ye atakalein lagai ja rahi hain ki isse bhart rus ke raksha sanbandhon, khas taur par esa- misail sistm ki sanbhavit khrid par kyaa asar paadega  
isse pahale amarika ne is qanun ke tahat chin ke seantrl militri kamishn ke ikvipmeant develpameant dipartmeant aur usake nideshkon par pratibandh laga diyaa tha chin par ye pratibandh islie lagae gae the, kyoanki usane rus se esayu- eyarakrapht and esa- sistm khrida tha  
rus mein banane vale esa- lang reanj saraphes tu eyar misail sistma ko bhart sarakar khridna chahti hai ye misail zamin se hava mein maar kar sakati hai 
esa- ko duniyaa ka sabase prabhavi eyar dipheans sistm maana jata hai ismein kai khubiyaan haian 
jaise esa- ek sath  jagahon par nishana laga sakata hai iske alava ismein staiand-f jaimr eyarakrapht, eyaraborn varniang aur kantrol sistm eyarakrapht hai yah bailistik aur kruz donon misailon ko girne se pahale raste mein hi nasht kar dega esa-  ko saadk ke raste kahin bhi le jayaa ja sakata hai aur iske bare mein kaha jata hai ki paanch se 1 mint ke bhitr ise tainat kiyaa ja sakata hai 
raksha vishleshkon ka maanna hai ki esa- ke aane se bhartiy sena ki taqt badhegi
bhartiy vayu sena ke lie bhart sarakar ne rus se paanch esa- sistm maaange haian esa- sistm ki aapurti ke lie kantrekt ho chuka hai
is dipheans sistm ke lie bhart ko kitni qimt chukani hogi, iski koi aadhikarik ghoshna abhi nahin ki gai hai lekin kuchh riports mein batayaa gayaa hai ki bhart ko iske lie  arab dalar se adhik khrch karne hoange
jaise hi is misail sistm ki pahali kisht chukai jaegi, vaise hi bhart par amarika ke pratibandh lagu ho sakate haian 
in pratibandhon se bachane ka ek tariqa hai, vo ye ki amarika ke rashtrpati bhart ko isse chhut de dean
lekin amariki adhikari lagatar ye kahate rahe hain ki bhart ko ye nahin sochna chahie ki use to ye chhut apane-aap hi mil jaegi amarika ye tay karega ki kyaa karna hai 
katsa ki dhara  mein 1 tarah ke pratibandhon ka zikr hai agar bhart rus ke sath len-den karata hai to amarika ke rashtrpati inmein se paanch yaa usase zyaada pratibandh bhart par laga sakate haian jaise -
inmein se das pratibandhon ka to bharta-amarika aur bharta-rus sanbandhon par zyaada frq nahin paadega lekin do pratibandh aapasi rishton par baada asar dal sakate haian 
inmein se ek hai ki baiankig traansekshns par pratibandh laga diyaa jaega jisse bhart esa- ke lie rus ko amariki dalar mein bhugtan nahin kar paega 
dusre pratibandh ka bharta-amarika rishton par gahara asar hoga iske tahat eksport yaani niryaat par pratibandh laga diyaa jaega matalab jis par pratibandh laga hai, amarika usase kisi chiz ka aayaat nahin karega aur na hi iske lie laiseans dega 
in do pratibandhon ki vajah se bhart aur amarika ke bich ki rananitik aur raksha sajhedari buri tarah prabhavit hogi 
dilchasp bat ye hai ki amariki rashtrpati donld tranp is qanun se zyaada ittefaq nahin rakhate haian unhoanne apani khushi se is qanun par hastakshr nahin kie the balki unhoanne ye bhi kaha tha ki is qanun mein kai gaadbaadiyaan haian 
donld tranp ne ye aashanka jatai thi ki katsa ke prabhav mein aane se amariki kanpniyon ke sath-sath unake sahayogi deshon ka bhi nuqsan hoga

mir usmaan ali khan ke pote aur maujuda nizam mukrrm jah ke chachere bhai najaf ali khan ne is faisle par apani pratikriyaa dete hue kaha, jastis maarks smith ke faisle ka svagt karate haian hai kort ne bhart ke aur haidrabad ke nizam vii ke vanshj ke paksh mein pakistan ke dave ko kharij kar diyaa parivar ko is faisle ka lanbe samay se iantzar tha 
landn ki adalt ke faisle par pakistan ne kaha hai ki vo faisle ka adhyyan kar raha hai
pakistani videsh mantraly ne ek bayaan jari kar kaha, ye aadesh paise traansphar karne ke etihasik sandrbh ko dhyaan mein nahin rakhata jab bhart ne aantrarashtriy qanun aur sabhi sabhy qanunon ka ullanghn karate hue haidrabad ko avaidh rup se haadp liyaa tha nizam ne sanyukt rashtr surksha parishd mein bhi ye msala uthayaa tha jo aaj bhi surksha parishd ke ejeande mein hai nizam ne ek svtantr shask ki haisiyt se pakistan se madad maaangi thi jo pakistani sarakar ne di 
bayaan mein kaha gayaa hai ki pakistan is aadesh ka vistar se adhyyan kar raha hai aur qanuni salah ke bad aage qdam uthayaa jaega

haidrabad 1 sitanbr 1 tak nizam shasn ke tahat unaki riyaast bana raha tha iske bad pareshn polo nam ke sainy abhiyaan ke zarie is riyaast ka vily bhart mein kar diyaa gayaa
us vakt haidrabad aasaf jah vansh ke satvein vanshj navab mir usmaan ali khan siddiqi ki riyaast huaa karati thi us daur mein vo duniyaa ke sabase dhani vykti maane jate the
pareshn polo ke zarie haidrabad ke bhart mein vily hone se pahale vo haidrabad riyaast ke satvein aur aakhiri nizam the
satvein nizam ke pote yuvraj mukrrm jah-aathavein ka pratinidhitv karne vali la sanstha vidrs varldvaid la pharm ke pal hevitt ne bbc ko batayaa tha, "pareshn polo ke dauran haidrabad ke nizam ke vitt mantri ne paison ko surkshit rakhane ke irade se qrib 1 lakh pauand us vakt pakistan ke hai kamishnr ke landn vale baiank khate mein traansphar kar die"
1 mein traansphar kiyaa gayaa yahi paisa bad mein satvein nizam ke uttradhikariyon aur pakistan ke bich qanuni jang ki vajah ban gayaa 
pal hevitt ke anusar, "jaise hi haidrabad ke satvein nizam ko paison ke traansphar ke bare mein pata chala to unhoanne pakistan se kaha ki unake paise jald lauta de lekin rahimtulla ne paise vapis dene se inkar kar diyaa aur kaha ki ye ab pakistan ki sanptti ban gai hai"
iske bad 1 mein satvein nizam aur pakistan ke bich ek qanuni jang shuru hui nizam ne apane paise vaps pane ke lie yuke ke hai kort ka rukh kiyaa aur qanuni prakriyaa shuru ki
hai kort mein maamla pakistan ke paksh mein chala gayaa aur iske bad nizam ko korts f apil mein jana paada jahan nizam ki jit hui 
lekin iske bad pakistan ne aage badh kar us daur mein yuke ke uchchtam nyaayaaly, haus f lards ka daravaza khatakhatayaa pakistan ki dalil thi ki ki nizam pakistan par kisi tarah ka muqdamaa nahin kar sakate kyoanki pakistan ek sanprabhu rashtr hai
haus f lards ne pakistan ke paksh mein apana faisla diyaa aur usaki dalil ko sahi thaharaate hue kaha ki nizam pakistan par muqdamaa nahin kar sakate lekin iske sath hi haus f lards ne 1 lakh pauand ki is vivadit rashi ko bhi phriz kar diyaa 
iske bad se habib ibraahim rahimtulla ke khate mein traansphar kie gae ye paise naitvest baiank ke pas haian 
1 mein haidrabad ke satvein nizam ki maut ho gai lekin paison ko vaps pane ki ye qanuni jang iske bad bhi jari rahi aur ise aage badhayaa unake uttradhikariyon ne
is qanuni laadai mein sal 1 mein pal hevitt tab shamil hue jab pakistani uchchayukt ne pakistan ke lie paise nikalne ki ummid mein baiank ke khilaf qanuni prakriyaa shuru kar di
iske bad baiank iske ke lie badhy ho gayaa ki vo is maamle se in paison par dava karne vale sabhi sanbandhit pakshon se bat kare aur ismein bhart samet nizam riyaast ke donon yuvraj bhi shamil the
pal hevitt ne batayaa tha ki donon yuvrajon ne hal mein is mudde par bhartiy sarakar ke sath charcha ki hai jo ek vakt in paison par dava kar chuki thi
ab tak nizam ke uttradhikariyon aur bhartiy sarakar ke bich charcha yaa samajhaute se sanbandhit koi dastavez samne nahin aayaa hai
bbc ne nizam ke uttradhikariyon se sanprk karne ki koshish ki thi lekin unhoanne bat karne se inkar kar diyaa tha

sal 1 mein dakshin afrika ke kep taun mein  sitanbr ke din do mahatvpurn ghatanaen ghatian

dusri ghatana thi, raat ko aayaa ek jabaradast bhukanp jisne dharati ko hila kar rakh diyaa tha

1 dinon tak ekaant karavas mein rahane ke bad  sitanbr ko imaam harun ne jel mein hi dam toada is dauran naslbhed ke khilaf sanghrsh mein unaki sanliptta ke bare mein unase rozana puchhtachh ki jati thi dakshin afrika mein sal 1 mein pahale ashvet rashtrpati, nelsn mandela ke chune jane ke bad vahan naslbhed khtm huaa tha
