unaka kahana tha ki imaam ki do tuti hui pasaliyaan aur unake sharir par  choton ke nishan ka unake sath koi lena-dena nahin hai, bavjud iske ki pulis logon par atyaachar karne aur maar-pit karne ke lie kukhyaat thi
imaam ke parivar ne kaha ki unhein pulis ka yah jhuth svikary nahin hai aur ve unaki maut ke  sal pura hone par ek bar phir se unake maut ke karnon ki jaanch ki maaang kar rahe haian
vizual aartist harun gun salaii is abhiyaan ka samarthn kar rahe haian imaam ke sammaan mein hi unaka ye nam rakha gayaa hai aur unhoanne imaam ke jivn aur mrityu se juadi ghatanaoein par kai aartvark banae gae haian
gun salaii ka hal hi mein kiyaa gayaa kam, kraiang phar jastis, kep taun mein kaisl f gud hop ke maidan mein lagayaa gayaa hai yah 11 achihnit kabraein hain jo rangbhed ke daur ke samay hirast mein marne vale logon ka pratik hai inmein se ek pratikatmk karb imaam harun ki yaad mein hai
batayaa jata hai ki in sabhi logon ko bina sunvai ke jel mein dala gayaa tha inki maut ke ke bare mein pulis ne kabhi kaha ki ve sidhiyon se gir gae yaa nahate samay phisl gae yaa khud hi khiadkiyon se niche chhalaang laga di
abhi tak hirast mein hui  mauton ke lie kisi ko bhi doshi nahin thaharayaa gayaa hai aur yah ek aisa jakhm hai jo unake parivar valon ko aaj bhi dard deta rahata hai 
mahal ki praachir se is aartvark ko dekhne par, gun saili dvara khodi hui kabra par jo shabd dikhega vo hai, nyaay?
gun saili kahate hain, "yah aartvark jitni kort se guhar hai utani hi jannt se bhi hai"
unhoanne batayaa, "yah ek tarah ka sarvjanik bayaan hai jo maaang karata hai ki atit se chijon ko phir nikala jae, phailon ko khoja jae, sabut dhuandhe jae jisse parivar ko is kes ka koi faisla, kisi tarah ka nyaay mil sake"
imaam abdulla harun ki  varshiy vidhva galimaa harun ka bhi ravivar ko unake pati ke aantim sanskar ke thik  sal bad nidhn ho gayaa hai galimaa ko bhi apane jivnakal mein is kes ka koi bhi faisla dekhne ko nahin mila
unhein shrddhaanjli dete hue afriki rashtriy kaangres ke saansd phaiz jaikbs ne kaha, "aisa pratit hota hai ki yah ek hatyaa thi jiske bad vidhva huin galimaa ne apane bachchon ko akele hi pala vah humesha sochti rahin ki unake pati ki mrityu kaise aakhar kaise hui"
vo kahate hain "agar rangbhedi shaskon ne socha ho ki ve galimaa ki aatmaa ko khtm kar sakate hain to vah galat sochte the vah nidr aur siddhaantvadi thian"
imaam harun dakshin afrika mein sabase kam umr ke imaamon mein se ek the 1 mein kevl  sal ki umr mein unhein kep taun ke stegmain rod msjid mein samuh ka netritv karne ke lie niyukt kiyaa gayaa tha
vo kep taun mein maujud rudhivadi mishrit nasl vale muslim samuday mein agrni neta the
unhoanne vayask shaikshnik kakshaon, charcha samuhon ki shuruaat ki, jahan yuva hi vishyon ka chayan karate the aur mahilaon ko usamein bhag lene ke lie praotsahit kiyaa jata tha
iske alava vo bachchon ko msjid mein pichhe baithne ki bajay aage baithne aur praarthnaon ka netritv karne ke lie aamantrit karate the
unhoanne muslim samuday se bahr ke logon ko bhi charchaon mein hissa lene ke lie aamantrit kiyaa inmein tred yuniyn aur udarvadi rajneta bhi shamil the vo chahte the ki sabhi log milkar yuvaon se batein karein ki dakshin afrika mein kyaa ho raha hai
peshe se patrkar, eenasi ke sashastr samuh ke purv sadasy aur aartist gun saili ke pita aniz saili kahate hain, "vah muslim maulviyon ke bane banae paitrn mein phit nahin baithte the"
saili 1 sal ki umr mein imaam ke aantim sanskar mein shamil hue the saili ne bbc ko batayaa, "imaam kaphi pragatishil aur apane samay se bahut aage the"
imaam harun ke tin bachchon mein sabase chhoti fatimaa harun-msoit haian jab imaam harun ki mrityu hui tab vah qrib chhah sal ki thian
unhoanne bbc ko batayaa, "vah ek bahut saumy, dayaalu, pyaare aur bhavnatmk rup se bahut milnasar vykti the"
jab imaam ki maut hui thi us samay unake bete muhmmd harun 1 sal ke the ab vah botsvana mein dharmshastr ke ek praophesr haian
vah apane pita ko ek baade aadhyaatmik vykti ke rup mein yaad karate hain ve kishoravstha se hi saptah mein do din upavas rakhate haian
unhoanne kaha, "unaki pahachan ek dharmik aur muslim paranpra ko maanne vale vykti ki thi"
"halaanki, vah ek samaaj sudhark bhi the aur aakarshk vyktitv ke dhani the vah shandar paridhan pahanate the aur phanake chehre par humesha ek mohk muskan hoti thi unhein ragbi, kriket aur sinemaa ka shauk tha"

imaam harun ki ichchha isai aur kamyuniston sahit any naslon ke logon ke sath gathabandhn banane ki thi
imaam ke ek chhatr aur ragbi ke purv khilaadi yusuph jova abraahm ko yaad karate hain ki imaam ne kis tarah rangbhed ke krur aur naslvadi qanunon se sabase zyaada prabhavit hone vale dakshin aphika ke kale logon ke lie aavaz uthai unhoanne muslim samuday mein is anyaay ke khilaf jagrukta failane ki koshish ki
abraahm ne bbc ko batayaa, "unhoanne humein batayaa ki humein nasliy divaron ko toadna hoga aur bhavishy ke lie kam karna hoga"
imaam jo upadesh dete the usaka khud abhyaas bhi karate the vah niymit rup se laanga, gugelthu aur nyaaanga jaise sthanon mein kale logon ke samudayon ke bich jate the
imaam hone ke sath-sath, harun ne kanphekshnari kanpni vilsn rontri ke lie ek vikreta ke rup mein bhi kam kiyaa
is naukri ka matalab tha ki vah qanuni rup se basti se bahr ja sakate the naslbhedi sarakar ne grup eriyaaz ekt jaise qanun se nasliy tarj par dakshin afrika ko alaga-thalag rakhane aur logon ki gatividhiyon par pratibandh laga rakha tha
mai 11 mein kep taun ke dril hal mein aayojit ek sarvjanik baithk mein imaam ne us qanun ko amaanviy, barbr aur gairislami bata kar nianda ki thi char sal bad, lakhon any dakshin afriki logon ki tarah, imaam aur unake parivar ko apane hi ghar se bahr kar diyaa gayaa
us vaqt adhikaansh dusre imaam is maamle mein bolne se darate the vo yah maante the ki damanakari sarakar ke lie khilaf khaada hona unaka kam nahin hai
lekin imaam harun ki soch isse alag thi aur unhoanne rangbhed virodhi gupt abhiyaan mein bhag lena shuru kar diyaa
unhoanne apani patni aur apane sath ke logon ko bachane ke lie janbujh kar is bat ko gupt rakha ki vo kis tarah se rangbhed virodhi gupt abhiyaanon mein bhag lete haian

maliha lodhi ki jagah ab munir akaram sanyukt rashtr mein pakistan ke sthayi pratinidhi hoange 
maliha lodhi ko pad se kyon hatayaa gayaa, ab tak pakistan ki or se is bare mein koi aadhikarik jankari nahin di gai hai na hi ye batayaa gayaa hai ki maliha lodhi ko ab kyaa zimmedari di gai hai
halaanki soshl midiyaa mein taraha-tarah ki atakalein lagai ja rahi haian 
kai logon ka maanna hai ki maliha pakistan ke mishn kashmir ko kamyaab banane mein buri tarah asaphal rahin, islie ye faisla liyaa gayaa hai 
kuchh log maliha ko hatae jane ke bad unaki unaki galatiyon ka zikr kar rahe hain jinki vajah se pakistan ko sarvjanik manchon par sharmiandgi ka samna karna paada tha 
sitanbr, 1 ki bat hai maliha lodhi ne sanyukt rashtr mein kaha, "main aap sabhi aur bhartiy videsh mantri ko aamantrit karati hun ki aaen aur sanyukt rashtr ke nakshe ko dekhie rajy par bhart ka sainy kabza avaidh hai"
unhoanne sabake samne ek tasvir laharaate hue kaha main aapako kashmir mein bhartiy barbrata ka chehra dekhti huan unhoanne jo tasvir laharai vo ek yuva jakhmi laadki ki thi laadki ka pura chehra jakhmon se bhara huaa tha
maliha ne dava kiyaa ki vo kashmir mein bhartiy krurta ka sabut pesh kar rahi thin aur vo pelet gan se ghayl laadki ki tasvir thi 
unhoanne is tasvir ko ritvit bhi kiyaa tha
magar jaldi hi pata chal gayaa ki vo tasvir kashmir nahin balki gaza patti ki thi tasvir mein dikh rahi laadki bhi kashmiri nahin balki 1 sal ki flastini laadki thi 
use chotein pelet gan se nahin balki bam ke golon se lagi thi 
israili humale mein ghayl hone vali is laadki ki tasvir avard viniang foto patrkar haidi lavin ne sal 1 mein khianchi thi
sanyukt rashtr mein kashmir ki frji tasvir pesh karne ke lie maliha lodhi ki duniyaa mein khub kirkiri hui thi 
khaskar pakistan ki soshl midiyaa mein iski kaadi aalochna hui thi pakistani logon ne kaha ki maliha lodhi ki is chuk se desh ki badanami hui hai 
pakistani akhbar d neshn ne to ise aaparadhik chuk tak kah diyaa tha 
iske alava maliha lodhi us vaqt bhi apani chuk ki vajah se charcha mein aai thin jab unhoanne apane ek tvit mein braitani pradhanmantri boris janasan ko braiten ka videsh mantri kahakar sanbodhit kiyaa tha
lodhi ne tvit kiyaa tha, "pradhanmantri imran khan ne aaj subh braiten ke videsh mantri boris janasan se mulaqat ki" unhoanne tvit ke sath donon netaon ke bich hui baithk ki ek tasvir bhi sajha ki thi 
halaanki lodhi ne karib ek ghante bad us tvit ko hatate hue galati ke lie maafi bhi maaang li thi
ab pad se hatae jane ke bad maliha lodhi ek bar phir surkhiyon aur charcha mein haian 
varishth pakistani patrkar ne unhein bavandra kahakar sanbodhit kiyaa hai aur tvit kiyaa hai, "maliha apamaanjanak thian vo apane se baadon aur chhoton sabaka apamaan karati thian vo behd mahatvakaankshi aur aatmmugdh thian pradhanmantri imran khan ne vo faisla liyaa hai jo unhein lena chahie tha munir akaram ko sanyukt rashtr mein niyukt karne ka faisla bahut achchha hai har sirphire vykti ka aakhiri din aata hai"
purv ra pramukh tilk deveshr ne tvit kiyaa hai, "maliha lodhi ko imran khan ke daure ke bad tuanrt sanyukt rashtr mein sthayi pratinidhi ke pad se hata diyaa gayaa hai isse pata chalata hai ki unaka sanyukt rashtr mein daura kaisa raha"
imran khan ne sanyukt rashtr mahasbha mein kashmir mudde par bhart ki kaadi aalochna ki thi aur kashmir mein lagi pabandiyon ko amaanviy batayaa tha 
iske javab mein bhart ne palatavar karate hue kaha tha kashmiriyon ki iski zarurt nahin hai ki koi dusra unake lie aavaz uthae, khaskar vo desh jisne apane yahan aatank ke udyog ko paida kiyaa hai

tiyaanjin mein rahane vale zao ziangjiyaa kagaz katkar chitr taiyaar karne mein maahir haian vo aadhunik chin ke janak kahe jane vale neta maaotse tuang ki tasvir bana rahe haian
zao chin mein kamyunist sarakar ke itihas se juadi tasvirein banate haian vo kahate hain, "chin ganarajy aur meri umr lagabhag ek hi hai main apane desh, apane logon aur apane netaon se behd pyaar karata huan"

sarasari nigah se dekhein to chin mein aayaa badalav asadharn nazar aata hai
1 aktubr, 1 ke din cheyramain maao tiyaanenmn chauk par khaade the aur apane bhashn se yuddh se tahasa-nahas, ardh-samanti desh se nae daur mein pravesh karne ki apil kar rahe the us samay hui pared khas nahin thi
magar batayaa ja raha hai ki is saptah hone vali pared mein duniyaa ki sabase adhik reanj vali iantra-kantineantl paramaanu misail aur suprasonik jasusi dron ko us samriddh aur ubharati dabang suprapavr ke pratik ke taur par darshayaa jaega jiske pas madhymavarg ki  karoad aabadi ki taqt hai

ye bat gussae salamaan khan ne ek midiyaa fotografr  se kahi

isi big-bas ki agali kaadi yaani big-basa-1 ka somvar ko muanbi ke aandheri metro yaard par dhamaakedar aagaz kiyaa gayaa
sho ko lanch kiyaa salamaan khan ne
is bar big bas ka lanch iveant karykrm kafi khas raha kyoanki iska aayojn metro steshn ke pas yaard par kiyaa gayaa tha
iske sath hi sho mein aise hi kai chijein hain jo pahali bar hone ja rahi haian
lanch iveant ke dauran salamaan khan ne sho se juadi kai batein sheyr kian
hal hi mein sho ka ek nayaa praomo rilij kiyaa gayaa jismein salamaan big basa-1 ke tivst eand tarn ke bare mein bata rahe haian 
jahan char hafton mein hi pratibhagi finale ki or badhne lageange 
is tivst ke bare mein bat karate hue salamaan tren mein savar hue nazar aate hain aur phatapht pratiyogion ki gaadi ko phainls mein pahuanchane ki bat kar rahe haian
sho mein char hafton ke bad hi vijeta ki trfi ke lie asali jang shuru ho jaegi
is bar big bas ke bare mein jo ek aur bat jo alag vo ye hai ki maharashtr ke lonavla mein banata tha aur sare pratiyogi vahin rahate the lekin is bar big bas 1 ka set muanbi ki film siti mein banayaa gayaa hai 
is par salamaan kahate hain ki, us set par muanbi ke traifik mein pahuanchna hi tin ghanton ka ekatarafa saphar hai, jismein do bar lonavla se aayaa jayaa sakata hai
salamaan ne ye bhi kaha ki is bar jahan big basa-1 ka set laga hai vahan khub spirits bhi hain, yaani bhutiyaa harakatein hoti rahati haian
big basa-1 ka praimiyr tivi par  sitanbr, ravivar ko raat  baje hoga salamaan khan sho ko host kareange aur sho ke kantesteant ke pratibhagiyon se logon ko milaeange

to vah pure nagrik samaaj ko usaka nishchhl bachapan chhine jane ka aparadhi thahara raha hai ye tamaam kirdar daraasal bhart mein jari ekatarafa shaharikran tatha kathit vikas ki prakriyaa ki bali chadhe kirdar haian

aur inmein sabase khas piku, jiske lie unhoanne apana navintam rashtriy purskar bhi jita mahila kirdar ke nam par aadharit is film ko ek mahila ne hi likha hai

film gali bvya ko lekr naizi kahate hain ki is film se unako jitni shohrat mili hai, utani unaki niji ziandgi bhi prabhavit hui hai 
gali bvya ko skr purskar ke lie bhart ki taraf se aadhikarik taur par namit kiyaa gayaa hai is film ka nirdeshn zoyaa akhtr ne kiyaa hai aur ranavir sianh ke alava aaliyaa bhatt ne bhi is film mein ahum bhumika nibhai hai 
skr ke lie namit hone ke bad ye film ek bar phir charcha mein hai film ke kalakaron ke sath ye khbar unake lie bhi ahum hai jinki ziandgi se praerit hokr film gali bvya ki kahani likhi gai ye hain divain aur naizi 
naizi maante hain ki gali bvya ki saphalata se unhein shohrat to mili lekin unaki niji ziandgi puri tarah se ulata-pult ho gai 
vo kahate hain ki niji ziandgi mein unhein bahut nuqsan uthana paada jiski bharapai koi nahin kar payega 
naved shekh urf naizi ne bbc hiandi se khas batchit mein kaha, "gali bvy ki riliz ke bad mujhe stardam mila mujhe ghar mila, gaadi mili aur to aur bahut shohrat bhi miliab main jahan bhi jata hun log mere sath selphi khianchvate hain aur mujhe pahachante haian lekin mera parsnal spes puri tarah se khtm ho gayaa meri niji ziandgi is film ke bad puri tarah se ulata-pult ho gai hai"
unhoanne aage kaha, " film mein meri kahani thoadi galat tariqe se dikhai gai hai film mein mera lav afeyr jo dikhayaa gayaa hai, mere maata-pita ke bare mein jo dikhayaa gayaa hai ye sab ek kapol kalpna hai ye sach nahin hai aur ye bat logon ko batane ke lie kafi samay lag raha hai logon ko lagata hai meri do garlphreand haian mere maata-pita ne do shadiyaan ki aur aisi kai sari afvahein hain jo mere niji jivn ko chot pahuancha rahi haian film mein sachchai nahin thi sachchai kuchh aur hai lekin log is bat ko maan hi nahin rahe 
ranavir sianh bane kapil dev to kyaa bola soshl midiyaa
naizi kahate hain ki unaki ziandgi mein jitni sakaraatmk batein hui hain, utani hi nakaraatmk bhi hui hai 
vo kahate hain, "ab mujhe napsand karne vale log bhi badh gae haian islie ziandgi ko santulit karne ki koshish kar raha huan"
ek daur tha jab bhartiy raipr aangrezi mein hi raip karate the lekin naizi nayaa aandaz lekr aae ise lekr vo kahate hain, "maianne bhi aangrezi mein raip karna shuru kiyaa tha maianne dekha ki iandiyaa mein kai raipr aangrzi mein raip karate hai jiske karn humaari pahuanch bahut kam logon tak hi rah gai thi aur jab maianne is bat ko samajha ki aadhe se zyaada log to humein sun hi nahin rahe hain tab maianne  hiandi mein raip karna shuru kiyaa"  
naizi kahate hain, "maianne jab hiandi mein raip shurukiyaa to 1 raipr aur the unhoanne mujhe dekha ki hiandi mein main saphal huaa to unhoanne bhi hiandi mein raip karna shuru kar diyaa aaj ye hal hai ki raip ab puri tarah se aangreji se hiandi mein shipht ho gayaa aise hi karate-karate dayra badhta gayaa aur aaj har koi hiandi mein raip kar raha hai"  
kyaa unhein balivud iandstri vahi sammaan deti hai jo kai baade lekhkon ko milta hai, is saval par naizi kahate hai, "mujhe gulzar sahb aur javed akhtr ji se tarif mili hai unhoanne mujhe batayaa ki main jis tarah likhta hun use kahate hain  aazad nazm jis tarah se sher-shayri hoti hai, git hote hain, usi tarah se humaara bhi ek varg hai aazad nazm ka, jahan main khule alfaz istemaal kar sakata huan"
naizi batate hain ki unhein shuru mein bahut dikqtein aaian kai logon ko unake likhne ka aandaz pasand nahin aayaa 
unake mutabiq, "kai logon ne kaha ye bahut muanhphat hai kaise-kaise shabd bolta hai lekin dhire-dhire logon ko mere shabdon mein gaharai dikhne lagi"
naizi kahate hain ki unhein bhartiy logon ki maansikta ko badalana hai 
vo kahate hain, "hum raipr jante hai ki humaara pahanava dusre lekhekon jaisa nahin hai ye thoada alag hai hum phaiansi kapaade pahanate hain lekin humaari jo jaadein hain vo vahi raheangi desi hip-hap hum kabhi nahin bhuleange hum raipr aandhe banakar amarika ko kapi nahin kar rahein hai balki apane hi kalchr ko nayaa rup dekr pesh kar rahe hai" 
naizi ne hal hi mein apana nayaa gana phatake riliz kiyaa hai jismein vo aaj ke bachchon ko samajhane ki koshish mein dikhte haian 
sau sal pahale kaise banati thin filmeanjanna chaheange aap

ye maana jata hai ki hiandi filmon mein kam kar rahe adhiktar abhinetaon ko hiandi bhasha nahin aati islie unhein film ki skript bhi romn mein likhkar di jati hai lekin manoj bajpeyi film ki patakatha devnagri bhasha mein hi lete haian

film-nirmaata rani skruvala aur siddharth ray kapur ne hal hi mein apani apakamiang film d skay iz piank ka postr riliz kiyaa tha jiske bad se zayra vasim ko lekr yah dava kiyaa ja raha hai
is postr mein praiyanka chopada, frahan akhtr aur rohit saraf ke sath zayra vasim bhi nazar aati haian ek riyl laif stori par aadharit yah film 11 aktubr 1 ko riliz honi hai
film ke is postr ke alava ektres praiyanka chopada ne bhi hal mein ek foto tvit kiyaa tha jise soshl midiyaa par film iandstri mein zayra vasim ki vapsi ke dave ke taur par sheyr kiyaa ja raha hai

lekin apani paadtal mein humane payaa ki zayra vasim se sanbandhit ye sabhi dave galat hain aur film ki puri tim ke sath unaki jo tasvir soshl midiyaa par sheyr ki ja rahi hai, vo purani hai
shonali bos ke nirdeshn mein bani film d skay iz piank ke pramoshn ka kam tri-shala nam ki ek kanpni dekh rahi hai
is kanpni ne film nirmaataon ke havale se bbc ko batayaa ki zayra vasim ab tak film ke kisi pramoshnal iveant mein nahin aai hain aur aage bhi nahin aaeangi
kanpni ke anusar maarch se apraail 1 ke bich film ki shutiang puri kar li gai thi jun ke aant mein jab zayra vasim ne film iandstri chhoadne ka faisla kiyaa tha, tab se film ki tim ka unase sanprk nahin hai
kanpni ne us praes riliz ka bhi havala diyaa jo d skay iz piank film ki nirmaata kanpni ray kapur films ne 1 julai 1 ko jari ki thi
is praes riliz mein likha tha, "zayra ek zabaradast kalakar hain jo humaari film d skay iz piank mein aayasha chaudhri ke kirdar mein dikheangi pichhle mahine film ka kam pura kar liyaa gayaa tha is dauran zayra ne praofeshnal tariqe se kam kiyaa ab jo nirny unhoanne liyaa hai, vo unaka vyktigt nirny hai jiska hum puri tarah sammaan karate haian hum har tarah se unaka saport karate hain aur humesha karate raheange"
soshl midiyaa par praiyanka chopada, frahan akhtr aur rohit saraf ke sath zayra vasim ki jo foto sheyr ki ja rahi hai, vo fravari 1 ki hai
frahan akhtr ki tim ne aur film nirmaata kanpni ne bbc se is bat ki pushti ki hai
ye tasvir aandmaan-nikobar dvip samuh ke haivlak aailaiand par khianchi gai thi jiska nam ab bhart sarakar ne svraj dvip kar diyaa hai
vayral foto mein film ki puri tim jin kapaadon mein nazar aati hai, unhin kapaadon mein kuchh tasvirein praiyanka chopada aur rohit saraf ne maarch aur phir julai 1 mein apane ianstagram praofail par sheyr ki thian
tvitr par zayra vasim ne aakhiri tvit  agast 1 ko kiyaa tha usi din bhart sarakar ne jammu-kashmir mein anuchchhed- ko nishprabhavi kiye jane ki ghoshna ki thi
zayra ne keandr sarakar ke is faisle par likha tha, "yah daur bhi gujr jayega kashmir"

aayushmaan ka maanna hai ki rashtriy purskar ki ghoshna ke bad un par ek khushi bhara dabav ban gayaa hai
bbc se batchit mein vo kahate hain, "film karne se pahale aap avards ke bare mein nahin sochte agar milta hai to aapako ek praotsahn mil jata hai ki aapake chayan sahi haian"
vo kahate hain, "main sirf skript ke sath jana chahta hun mujhe paravah nahin ki nirdeshk, nirmaata yaa mera saha-kalakar kaun hai? kabhi-kabhi aap baade nam sunkar bahak jate haian par baade se baada nirdeshk buri film de sakata hai aur nae se nayaa nirdeshk ek saphal film de sakata hai ye main samajh gayaa hun"
aayushmaan ko lagata hai ki jo filmein ve chunte hain, unhein chunne mein kisi abhineta ko sankoch ho sakata hai, par unhein kabhi sankoch nahin huaa 
vo maante hain ki jab tak vo kuchh alag nahin kareange, film iandstri mein apani jagah nahin bana sakeange
film iandstri ke nae pidhi ke sabhi abhinetaon ko amitabh bachchn ki chitthi ka iantzar rahata hai 
ab tak aayushmaan khurana ko bhi amitabh bachchn se do chitthiyaan mil chuki haian unhein pahali chitthi film dam lagake haisha ke lie mili thi aur dusri chitthi rashtriy purskar ke lie mili hai 
is par aayushmaan kahate hain, "bachchn sahb ki chitthiyon ka iantzar humesha rahata hai vo apane aap mein hi ek avard hai"
film iandstri mein aath sal gujrne ke bad aayushmaan ko amitabh bachchn ke sath shujit sarakar ki aagami film "gulabo sitabo" mein kam karne ka mauka mila 
bachchn sahb ke sath kam karne ke anubhv ko sajha karate hue aayushmaan kahate hai, "vo bahut hi sahayogi kalakar haian unaki filmein dekhkar baade hue hai to unako dekhkar dar lagata hai par unake sath jab kam karate hain to vo ek kalakar ko ijzat dete hai unase bahut kuchh sikhne ko mila vo apani pidhi ke iklaute suprastar hain jo ab bhi raj kar rahe haian"
aayushmaan khurana kamedi film drimgarl mein nazar aaeange jismein vo mahila ki aavaz nikalte dikheange 
is philm ki kahani ye hai ki log unaki aavaz ke kayl hokr unase pyaar kar baithte haian raj shaandiliyaa ke dayrekshn mein bani drim garl mein nusrat barucha, annu kapur bhi ahum bhumika nibha rahe haian

is batchit mein unhoanne anushka sharmaa ke sath hui apani pahali mulaqat ke bare mein batayaa virat batate hain ki anushka sharmaa se unaki pahali mulakat ek shaimpu ke aid shutiang ke dauran hui thi aur vo us dauran bahut narvs the 
virat ne kaha, "main anushka se pahali bar shaimpu ke aid shutiang ke dauran mila tha ye shutiang tin dinon tak chali thi mere mainejr ne batayaa tha ki ye aid anushka sharmaa ke sath karna hai ye sunkar main narvs ho gayaa tha maianne apane mainejr se kaha ki vo praophshanal ektres haian main unake sath kaise ektiang karuanga mere mainejr ne mujhe samajhayaa ki sab thik hoga aid ki skript mazedar hai lekin main phir bhi bahut narvs tha" 
"jab main anushka se pahali bar mila to narvs ho gayaa tha unhoanne hil pahani thi aur vo mujhse zyaada lanbi lag rahi thi aur maianne apane kad ko lekr ek bura jok maar diyaa tha isse sthiti aur ajib ho gai, jisse main aur narvs ho gayaa"
iske alava virat ne anushka aur apane rishte ke ab tak ke safr ko lekr bhi kai batein ki unhoanne batayaa ki donon ki ziandgi ek jaisi rahi hai, donon ke kariyr ki shuruaat bhi ek hi samay par hui  mein aur donon ke parivar bhi ek se haian 
virat aur anushka ki shadi ko lekr unake phaians mein bahut utsah tha ye bhart ki ek baadi shadi thi apani shadi ke bare mein virat ne kaha, "shadi ki sari taiyaari anushka ne ki thi main ek siriz ke bich mein tha anushka ne hi shadi ki jagah tay ki thi mujhe kaha gayaa ki shadi ki bat ko humein bas apanon ke bich hi rakhana hai"
virat ne batayaa ki unaki shadi mein kevl  log shamil hue the virat ki shadi itli mein hui thi itli se lautkar shadi ke do phankshn rakhe gae the ek balivud ke lie aur ek kriketrs ke lie
apane hanimun ke bare mein bhi virat ne ek bahut hi mazedar kissa sunayaa unhoanne batayaa ki ve bhiadbhaad se alag jana chahte the islie unhoanne phinlaiand jana tay kiyaa vo aisi jagah jana chahte the jahan unhoanne koi n pahachanta ho 
virat ne kaha, "hum kaphi pine ke lie gae the aur aapas mein bat kar rahe the ki puri duniyaa mein ek yahi jagah hai jahan humein koi nahin pahachanta hum logon ki nazaron aur kaimron se aazad haian lekin isi dauran meri nazar bagal ki tebl par baithe shakhs par paadi vo aadami pagaadi mein tha aur mujhe hi dekh raha tha hum uthakar aandr vale tebl par jakr baith gae kuchh der bad vo aadami humaare pas aakar bola ki aap logon se milkar bahut achchha laga aur mera sarnem bhi kohli hi hai" 
"us samay main ye soch raha tha ki hum ek aisi jagah kab ja rahe hain jahan koi humein n pahachan sake"

bahubli film ke bad abhineta prabhas ki dhamaakedar eantri ki ummid lete hue jab hum saho dekhne pahuanche to kevl maayusi hi hath lagi
ye film char bhashaon mein ek sath riliz hui hai zahir hai prabhas ke itne phains hain ki har shahar mein logon ne pahale hi is film ki bukiang kara rakhi thi
bahubli ke bad kuchh logon ko iantzar tha ki itne baade paimaane ki film ke bad ye film bhi baks phis par khari utaregi
aisa nahin hai ki film mein vaisa msala nahin hai jo is tarah ki film mein hona chahie film mein sathi kalakar ke rup mein jaiki shrph, tinu aanand, chanki paande, mandira bedi, arun vijy, prakash belavadi jaise kai manjhe hue kalakar haian par unake pas film mein kuchh khas karne ke lie nahin hai
ek tarah se dekha jae to ye sab kevl kuchh patron ko bharne ke lie hi rakhe gae haian
film ek kalpnik shahar vajipur se shuru hoti hai jahan par jaiki shrph ray nam ka aanpayr chalate haian vo kala dhandha karate hain aur unaki shakhaen desh-videsh mein phaili hui haian par kuchh izjt kamaane ke lie vo stil ki ek phaiktri lagana chahte hain jiske lie unako kuchh rajnitijnon ki madad ki zarurt paadti hai
unake dal ke kuchh sadasy aise hain jo unase badala lena chahte haian is ranjish mein jaiki shrph ki hatyaa ho jati hai iske bad kahani kai deshon mein ghumti hai jahan chin, aphrika aur kuchh bhart ke log bhi shamil haian
dusri or banbi mein kuchh pulis aphasar hain jo ray aanpayr ke phaile dhandhe se pareshan haian inmein shamil hain murli, shrddha kapur aur prabhas
jab prabhas than lete hain ki vo ray aanpayr ka khatmaa kar deange tab shuru hoti hai laadai pulis aur aandravarld ki ray aanpayr ek blaikbaks ki talash mein hota hai jiske khulne se unake hath bahut-si puanji lagegi lekin is blaikbaks ke bare mein pulis ko pahale se hi pata hota hai
iske bad film ki kahani ruk jati hai aur chuhe-billi ke khel ki tarah pulis aur aandravarld ke bich tanav shuru ho jata hai iske alava plt ke nam par film shuny hai
halaanki film ki gati to tez ho jati hai lekin us dauran hum sirf tamaam gaadiyaan uadte hue dekhte hain aur bahut tez ekshn ke chalate kuchh kirdaron ko aate-jate dekhte haian isi bich film mein do-tin gane aur nach thuansa gayaa hai
zahir hai ki prabhas ke sath shrddha kapur ka romaaans philm mein joadna zaruri tha isi dauran humein nil nitin mukesh bhi nazar aate hain jinko lekr ye sanshy bana rahata hai ki vo pulis ke aadami hain yaa aandravarld ke
prabhas puri film mein chhae rahate hain aur kuchh saspeans rakhate hue humein ye bhi nahin pata chal pata ki vo pulis mein hain bhi yaa nahian aise kai sin hain jahan daylag ki kami khalati hai
shayd unaki hiandi itni achchhi nahin hai isi vajah se vo ekshn karate hue zyaada nazar aate haian 
film mein sijiaai kanpyutr jenreted imezari ke zarie kuchh romaaanch se bhare drishy zarur hain jo vastvikta se bahut dur hain aur kevl darshkon ko khush karne ke lie rakhe gae haian
takaniki drishti se dekha jae to ye sin kisi bhi halivud film ki takkr ke haian kami hai to sirf ek kahani ki kyoanki kevl ekshn ke bal par tin ghante film ko jhelna mushkil ho jata hai
prabhas ko ek lokpraiy balivud nirdeshk ki film se shuruaat karni chahie thi lekin shayd bahubli ka prabhav itna adhik hai ki vo usi mein apane aap ko dhale hue haian kuchh salamaan aur akshy kumaar ki filmon ka bhi asar hoga
iske alava uttr bhart mein apana rang jamaane ke uddeshy se hi unhoanne aisi film ka chayan kiyaa hai jismein kevl unake siks paiks ebs, ek lain ki kahani, tin gane aur bahut sara ekshn hi film mein maujud hai film dekhne ke bad bas ek hi bat dil se niklati hai ki kash film mein ek plt bhi hota

prabhas ki aane vali film saho ko lekr unake faians mein kafi usah hai jab se unaki film ka trelr riliz huaa hai tabhi se faians  agast ke iantzar mein haian film ko riliz hone mein ab kuchh hi din ka samay bacha hai, aise mein har roz film se juadi koi n koi khbar samne aa rahi hai hal hi mein midiyaa se batchit karate hue prabhas ne film se lekr any kai baton se parde uthae 
prabhas ke anusar unhein laga tha ki saho film ki shutiang ek sal ke aandr khtm ho jaegi par aisa huaa nahian
vo kahate hain, planiang kar rakhi thi lekin vo to bahubli- ke liye bhi ki hui thi, par usake ekshns ki vajah se bahut taim lag gayaa saho mein  log halivud se aaye, ekshn ke kai sin aabu dhabi mein shut kiye gae, kvaliti ka pura dhyaan rakhate hue zyaada samay laga aur  sal bit gae par main is film ko do sal se zyaada samay nahin dena chahta tha"   
prabhas khud ko sharmila maante haian jab unase unaki niji zindgi ke bare mein puchha gayaa to sharmaate hue unhoanne kaha, main skul aur kalej mein kabhi laadkiyon se bat nahin karata tha aur pichhle sat salon se sab meri shadi ke pichhe paade hain, par ye to jab honi hogi ho jaegi 
jab prabhas se unaki bhasha ko lekr saval kiyaa gayaa to unhoanne kaha, main hindi likh aur padh sakata hun maianne saho ke lie bhi apane sare daylags hindi mein likhe aur phir padhe is film ke dayrektr sujit jinki saho sirf dusri film hai, vo bhi ye bat sunkar chauank gae lekin ye dekh kar unhein khushi hui  
aam taur par aaj kal filmein pure bhart mein dekhi jati hain, lekin jab film ko hit karavane ke tariqe ko lekr prabhas se saval kiyaa gayaa to javab mein prabhas ne kaha, film ki kahani supr hit honi chahie, chal vo apane aap jaegi meri maa ke ganv mein salamaan khan ki maianne pyaar kiyaa 1 dinon tak lagi hui thi, mere graiand fadr ki yah sabase phevret film thi
saho mein prabhas ke sath shrddha kapur bhi nazar aaengi ye joadi abhi se hi sabako pasand aa rahi hai tin din bad saho baade parde par aane ke lie taiyaar hai aur unaka letest gana bebi voant yu tel mi logon ke bich dhum macha raha hai

agar aapase puchha jae ki 11 mein aai is filmi git ka sangitkar kaun hai to javab hoga mashahur sangitkar khyyaam
vahi sangitkar khyyaam jinhoanne 1 mein shuru hue apane filmi kariyr ke pahale panch sal sharmaa ji ke nam se sangit diyaa
bhartiy sinemaa ke diggj sangitkar mohmmd zahur khyyaam hashmi ka somvar raat sadhe nau baje  sal ki umr mein nidhn ho gayaa
pichhle kuchh samay se saans lene mein diqqt ke karn unaka muanbi ke juhu mein ek asptal mein ilaj chal raha tha
pradhanmantri nareandr modi samet film, kala, rajniti aur any kshetron se juade logon ne khyyaam ke nidhn par shok jatate hue shrddhaanjli di hai
suprasiddh sangitkar khayyaam sahb ke nidhn se atyant dukh huaa haià¥¤ unhoanne apani yaadgar dhunon se anagint giton ko amar bana diyaaà¥¤ unake apratim yogdan ke lie philm aur kala jagat humesha unaka rini rahegaà¥¤ dukh ki is ghaadi mein meri sanvednaen unake chahne valon ke sath hainà¥¤
khyyaam sangitkar rahumaan ke sath milkar sangit dete the aur joadi ka nam tha sharmaa ji aur varmaa ji varmaa ji yaani rahumaan pakistan chale gae to pichhe rah gae sharmaa ji
bat 1 ki hai sharmaa ji kai filmon ka sangit de chuke the aur unhein ziyaa sarahadi ki film futpath ka sangit dene ka mauqa mila
dilip kumaar par filmaayaa gayaa gana tha -"sham-e-gam ki qsam aaj gamagi hain hum, aa bhi ja, aa bhi ja aaj mere sanama"
durdarshn ki ek purani iantravyu mein khyyaam batate hain, "ek din baton ka daur chala to ziyaa sarahadi ne puchha ki aapaka pura nam kyaa hai maianne kaha mohmmd zahur khyyaam to unhoanne kaha ki are tum khyyaam nam kyon nahin rakhate bas us din se main khyyaam ho gayaa"
inhin khyyaam ne film kabhi-kabhi, bazar, umarav jan, raziyaa sultan jaisi filmon mein behtarin sangit diyaa
1 fravari 1 ko panjab mein janme khyyaam ke parivar ka filmon se dur dar tak koi nata nahin tha unake parivar mein koi imaam tha to koi muazzin
lekin us daur ke kai naujvanon ki tarah khyyaam par keel sahagal ka nasha tha vo unhin ki tarah gayk aur ektr banana chahte the isi junun ke chalate ve chhoti umr mein ghar se bhagkar dilli chacha ke pas aa gae
ghar mein khub narazagi hui lekin phir bat is par aakar tiki ki mashahur pandit husnalal-bhagataram ki shagirdi mein vo sangit sikhegean
kuchh samay sikhne ke bad ve laadkapan ke nashe mein vo qismt aazamaane muanbi chale gae lekin jald samajh mein aayaa ki abhi sikhna baqi hai
sangit sikhne ki chah unhein dilli se lahaur baba chishti sangitkar gulam ahumad chishti ke pas le gai jinke filmi gharanon mein khub talluqat the lahaur tab filmon ka gadh huaa karata tha
baba chishti ke yahan khyyaam ek treni ki tarah unhin ke ghar par rahane lage aur sangit sikhne lage
durdarshn samet apani kai iantravyu mein khyyaam ye qissa zarur sunate hain, "ek bar biaar chopada baba chishti ke ghar par the aur chishti sahb sabako tanakhvah bant rahe the lekin biaar chopada ne dekha ki mujhe paise nahin mile chopada sahb ke puchhne par baba chishti ne batayaa ki is naujvan ke sath tay huaa hai ki ye sangit sikhega aur mere ghar par rahega par paise nahin mileange lekin biaar chopada ne kaha ki maianne dekha hai ki sabase zyaada kam to yahi karata hai bas biaar chopada ne usi vaqt mujhe 1 rupe mahine ki tanakhvah thamaai aur chopada khandan ke sath rishta ban gayaa"
khyyaam ne kai sangitkaron ki tulna mein kam kam kiyaa lekin jitna bhi kiyaa bemisal maana jata hai
ek sangit praemi ke nate jab bhi main unake gane sunti hun to unamein ek ajab sa thaharav, ek sanjidgi pati hun jise sunkar mahasus hota hai maano koi zakhmon par marahum laga raha ho yaa thapaki dete hue haule haule sahala raha ho

rishabh pant aur raviandr jadeja ne 1-1 rn banae jabaki hardik paandyaa ne 1 rn banae 
bhart kul  ovaron mein nau viket par kevl 1 rn bana pae dakshin afrika ki or se kagiso rabada ne sabase adhik tin viket lie 
vahin, jarn phartin aur biyurn heandriks ne do-do viket lie tabarez shamsi ne ek viket liyaa

isi pakki jagah par kriket khelne vale bachche iant ke upar iant rakhakar stanp banate hain aur pakka rasta pich ban jata hai 
is gaanv mein khel maidan nahin hai ek char divari ke aandr valibl khelne ke lie net laga hai 
do fsalon ke daramiyaan khali zamin ko sapat karake kriket turnameant karayaa jata hai 
duniyaa ki behtarin pichon aur shandar maidanon par khelne vale shubhman gil ke dimaag mein khetihr zamin par suhaga chalakr banayaa gayaa khel maidan kaisi chhavi banaega? 
jagadip sianh bachapan mein shubhman ke sath khela karate the jagadip sianh batate hain ki skul mein vah shubhman ko abhyaas karavate the
shubhman ke pita lakhaviandr sianh gil bhi unhein abhyaas karavane skul mein aayaa karate the ye sabhi shubhman ko geandbazi karate the 
jagadip abhi bhi chappl pahanakar geandbazi karate haian skul mein ballebazi ke dauran mid viket aur langn ke bich mein khela gayaa har shat shubhman ke ghar ki or jata hai 
grauand shat ko skul ki divarein rok leti hain aur uthakr maara gayaa har shat peadon mein phans jata hai shubhman us ghar se das sal pahale ja chuke haian
jaiml sianh ne ludhiyaana zile ke gaanv chuhadchak se aakar ye gaanv basayaa tha jaiml sianh ki chauthi pidhi mein didar sianh haian 
didar sianh ke dada pahalavan the aur vah khud kabaddi khelte the unhoanne lakhaviandr sianh ko bhi pahalavan banana chaha tha
lekin saadk hadse mein lakhaviandr ki jaangh ki haddi tut gai aur didar sianh ki ummidon par pani phir gayaa 
lakhaviandr sianh ne shubhman ko bachapan se hi kriket khelne mein laga diyaa 
shubhman ki buaa manaprait kaur greval batati hain, "humaare bhai ne humein use khilaune tak nahin dene die vo kahate the ki khilaunon ke karn usaka dhyaan kriket se hat jaega"
jaiml sianh vala mein gil jatt kheti karate hai is vakt kheton mein hath-hath lanbi geanhu ki phasal khaadi hai aur didar sianh ke ek baade kamare mein basmati chavl ki boriyaan bhari haian 
gaanv mein rahane vale raghuvir sianh batate hain ki sabhi jatt basmati chavl gharon mein bhar lete hain aur bad mein bechte haian 
vah shan se kahate hain ki is gaanv mein koi jatt baiank ka diphltr nahin hai gaanv ke nazadik jal bharav rokne ke lie nala bana hai 
ye nala, kheton mein khaadi gehun ki phasal aur gharon mein bhari basmati chavl ki boriyaan batati hain ki is gaanv mein harit kraanti abhi tak kamyaab hai 
gaanv mein baade-baade ghar pachas sal se purane nahin lagate pakki galiyon ki charcha mein sthaniy vidhayk sukhbir sianh badl ka nam aa hi jata hai 
gharon ke bahr ki koi divar rangdar nahin hai aur na hi kisi par palastr huaa hai 
 sal ke avatar sianh gil batate hain, "yah gaanv pahale kachcha tha" iske sath hi samajh mein aata hai ki pakke ghar kachchon jaise kyon dikhte haian 
gaanv ke ek taraph jate hue galiyaan tang ho jati hain aur ghar chhote ho jate haian in gharon ke bahr kuchh mard baithe haian 
jab patrkaron ko gaanv dikhate hue didar sianh yahan pahuanchte hain to yah mard khaade hokr sat shri akal kahate haian 
inhin gharon ke bahr balla lie tin-char laadkon ke sath jagadip sianh khaade haian jagadip ke pitaji peantr hain aur maan ghar sanbhalti haian vah khud kyaa karate hain? 
iske javab mein vo kahate hain, "ji main chanadigdh mein sikyoriti gard ki naukri karata hun aur kriket khelta huan"
shubhman ke phupha babbu sandhu kahate hain ki agar shubhman is pichhade hue gaanv mein rahate to unako itna baada mauka kabhi nahin mil sakata tha shubhman ne sabit kar diyaa hai ki qabiliyt ko dikhane ke lie agar mauka na mile to ye bemaani hai 
is bat se shubhman sahumat ho sakata hai lekin jagadip ke asahumat hone ki koi guanjaish nahin hai

guruvar ki dophar ke bad achank se soshl midiyaa mein em es dhoni ke sannyaas ko lekr atakalon ka daur shuru ho gayaa 
midiyaa mein is tarah ki khbarein aa rahi hain ki emaes dhoni guruvar ki sham mein is babt ek praes kaanphreans kar sakate haian 
halaanki dhoni ke sanyaas ki atakalon ki sabase baadi vajah tim iandiyaa ke maujuda kaptan virat kohli ka ek tvit hai 
virat kohli ne guruvar ko ek photo sheyr karate hue likha hai, "main ye maich kabhi nahin bhul sakata vo vishesh raat thi is aadami ne mujhe fitnes test ki tarah bhagayaa tha"
daraasal kohli is tasvir mein dhoni ke sajade mein jhuke nazar aae hain aur yah tasvir 1 ke varld ti- muqable mein streliyaa ke khilaf bhart ki shandar jit ki hai is muqable mein bhart ne dhoni-kohli ke siangls aur dabals ki badault 11 rnon ka mushkil lakshy hasil kiyaa tha 
kohli ke is tvit ke bad soshl midiyaa mein is bat ki afvah tezi se phaili hai ki emaes dhoni apane sannyaas ki ghoshna kar sakate haian
halaanki emaes dhoni ki patni sakshi sianh dhoni ne kuchh hi der bad tvit karate hue ise afvah bata diyaa

kriket streliyaa ke yutyub chainl par  maarch 1 ko post kie gae is vidiyo mein kai bar stiv smith ka gala bhar aayaa, aaansu bahr tak aa gae aur bolna mushkil hota gayaa lekin jaise-taise unhoanne khud ko sanbhala
dakshin afrika mein streliyaa ki tim jab bal se chheadchhaad karate pakaadi gai to vo smith ki kaptani mein hi khel rahi thi kaptani gai, sal bhar khelne par pabandi lagi aur kai halakon mein ye maan liyaa gayaa ki duniyaa ke sabase shandar ballebazon mein se ek smith ka kariyr ab nipt gayaa lekin aisa huaa nahian 
is vidiyo ko dekhne ke bad apani kalpnashkti ko dedh sal aage fast fravard kijie aur phir stiv smith ke bare mein sochie
in dinon vo ianglaiand mein ianglaiand ke geandbazon ko pani pilane mein lage haian eshej test siriz ke tin maichon ki paanch pariyon mein vo ab tak 1 rn bator chuke haian 
ek dohra shatak, do shatak aur do ardhshatak, ausat 1 ki chot ki vajah se ek maich mein vo bahr baithe, varna rnon ka aanbar aur uancha hota siriz ka paanchvan maich guruvar se shuru ho raha hai
stiv se juadi ek khbar ne bhartiyon ka dhyaan khas taur se khiancha hal mein apadet hui icc test raiankiang mein smith, bhartiy tim ke kaptan virat kohli se  aank aage nikl gae haian smith  par pahuanch gae hain jabaki kohli  par khaade haian
to kyaa is raiankiang mein pahale aur dusre paydan par khaade in do shandar ballebazon ke bich kisi tarah ki koi tulna ho sakati hai? kisi bhi jankar se puchh lijie, kahega nahian do ballebazon ke bich tulna bemaani haian donon shandar haian lekin zara der kuredne par javab thoada badalane lagata hai aur palaada smith ki or jhukne lagata hai
jane-maane kriket jankar ayaaz memn kahate hain, agar aap virat ki bat karein to sal 1 ke bad unaka pradarshn shandar raha hai lekin jahan tak stiv smith ka saval hai to vo baitiang jiniys hai takaniki taur par dekhein to smith ke ballebazi stail mein kuchh bhi paranpragt jaisa nahin dikhta
smith jaisi takanik kisi dusre ballebaz ke pas nahin hai kochiang mainual ki bat kijie yaa kisi koch se puchh lijie, aapako koi bhi is tarah ki teknik apanane ki salah nahin dega smith ki khas bat hai unaka phoks aur bal ko bahut jald pahachan jane ki unaki kshmata
memn ke mutabik, dan braaidmain ke bare mein kaha jata hai ki geand pich par paadte hi vo usaki lain-leanth bhaanp jate the, kuchh isi tarah ka maamla smith ke sath hai unaka stail dekhne mein bhale achchha na lage lekin asaradar zarur hai
jin braaidmain ke sath smith ke nam ka zikr kiyaa, unaka ek rikrd inhin ki vajah se khtare mein dikh raha hai sal 1 ki eshez siriz mein braaidmain ne  rn banae the, jo test siriz mein kisi bhi kriketr ka sabase adhik skor hai agar smith guruvar se shuru ho rahe oval test ki donon pariyon mein milakr  rn bana lete hain to ye  sal purana kirtimaan dhvst ho jaega
agar aur nanbron par gaur karein to smith, kohli se vahan bhi aage niklate dikhte haian 1 se ab tak unhoanne kul  test maich khele hain, jinmein 1 ki ausat se kul  rn banae haian inmein  shandar shatak aur  ardhshatak shamil haian
dusri taraf kohli ne 11 se ab tak  maichon mein  rn banae haian ausat smith se kafi pichhe 1 hai unhoanne ab tak  shatak aur  ardhshatak lagae haian aur smith ki tarif islie bhi karni hogi kyoanki bal taimpriang ki vajah se vo sal bhar se zyaada samay maidan se bahr bhi baithe haian
smith ko duniyaa ne rote hue dekha hai aur ab rn thoankte hue dekh rahi hai videshi maidanon par jab vo rn mashin ki tarah khelkar bar-bar balla uthate hain to kai darshk unhein hut karate haian is hutiang ko darakinar kar vo phir agali geand par rn batorne ki taiyaari mein jut jate haian
to kyaa smith aur kohli ke bich kriket ke nanbron ke alava maansik rup se mazabuti ka bhi koi mukabla ho sakata hai? 
varishth khel patrkar dharmeandr pant ka kahana hai, virat kohli kriket ke tinon praarupon mein achchhe hain, jabaki stiv smith test kriket mein shandar haian khas taur se unaki vapsi ne ye dikha diyaa hai ki vo kis tarah ke khilaadi haian
pant ke mutabik kohli tinon pharmet mein achchha khelte haian kisi bhi maidan par, kinhin bhi halat mein vo khelne ke lie taiyaar rahate haian lekin sath hi sath ye kahana bhi sahi hoga ki smith ne jis tarah vapsi ki hai, vo lajvab hai
unhoanne kaha, do daur mein humane smith ke do chehre dekhe haian ek vo samay, jab vo khud par kabu nahin rakh pae aur bal taimpriang jaise sharmnak kam mein jut gae aur dusra vo jo maidan ke bichoanbich khaade hokr hutiang ka samna kar raha hai, lekin use koi paravah nahin hai
pant ka kahana hai ki kriket kaushl yaa takanik ki bat karein to vo smith ke pas pahale se thi lekin bite ek sal mein jo maansik mazabuti yaa taqt unhoanne hasil ki hai, vo kohli yaa duniyaa ke kisi bhi dusre ballebaz se aage pahuanch gae haian 
ek sal ka fasla kitna aantr paida kar sakata hai, ye smith ka udahran dikhata hai sal 1 mein unhoanne char maichon ki sat pariyon mein mahaz  rn banae the aur ausat tha 1 ka is sal unhoanne tin maichon ki paanch pariyon mein 1 se jyaada ki ausat se 1 rn banakr eshez ka naksha badal dala hai 
memn ka kahana hai ki dedh sal pahale smith ka dhalan se girna aur is sal girkar uthana chauankane vala hai unhoanne kaha, vo sirf khilaadi nahin the vo duniyaa ki baadi timon mein se ek streliyaa ke kaptan bhi the, jo baadi bat hai lekin kaptani jana aur phir bain hona, kai khilaadi aise episod ke bad vapsi nahin kar pate
unhoanne kaha, mujhe yaad hai ki braaidmain ne ek test siriz mein  se zyaada rn banae the, phir viv richrds ne 1 ki siriz mein  se zyaada rn kie aur ab smith tin maichon mein  ka aaankada par kar chuke hain, jo hairt mein dalta hai
lekin memn abhi smith aur kohli ki tulna se bachana chahte haian unhoanne kaha, dekhie, in donon ballebazon mein behtar kaun hai, ye unake kariyr ke aant mein batayaa ja sakata hai do sal yaa tin sal ki avadhi ke bare mein bat ki ja sakati hai
memn ne kaha, in dinon duniyaa mein char ballebazon ki bat hoti hai stim smith, virat kohli, jo rut aur ken viliymsana lekin jab hum hai skor yaa baade rnon ki bat karate hain to smith philhal bis maalum hote haian
smith  sal ke hain aur aage paanch-sat sal kriket kheleange to ye aaankade mazabut ho sakate haian lekin agar aap tinon frmet dekheange to kohli ko nazaraaandaz nahin kar paeange to har khilaadi ke daur mein utar-chadhav aate rahate haian lekin seanchuri banane ki bat karein to is maamle mein smith aur kohli aage dikheange
memn ke mutabik,  maichon mein vo  shatak laga chuke hain aur unaka ausat  ka aaankada chhu raha hai, ye sabit karata hai ki smith koi aam ballebaz nahin balki jiniys haian

afganistan ki nazarein apane se kahin taqtavar maani jane vali tim ke khilaf pahali test jit hasil karne par tiki thin vahin dusri or mejban baangladeshi tim ki koshish kisi tarah maich dr kara lene ki thi afganistan ko jit ke lie char viket chahie the vahin dusri or baangladesh ka sara daromdar tim ke kaptan aur anubhvi khilaadi sakib al hasan ke balle par tha   
lekin din ki shuruaat chatagaanv mein barish se hui aur pahale satr mein koi khel nahin ho payaa lanch ke bad khel shuru huaa aur kuchh hi der mein barasat hone lagi aur khel badhit ho gayaa samay se pahale chay ka braek lena paada aakhir mein barasat thami lekin aasamaan mein ghane badl the aur roshni tezi se kam hoti ja rahi thi  
us vakt aisa lagane laga tha ki afganistan aur aitihasik jit ke bich mein barasat khaadi ho chuki hai lekin aanpayron ne aakhirkar khel shuru karane ka faisla liyaa, yah tay huaa ki adhiktam 1 ovaron ka khel sanbhv ho paega

iske bad tim ke kaptan aur star geandbaz rashid khan ne baangladeshi pari ko sametne mein der nahin lagai baangladesh ke char viket 1 ovar ke khel mein hi gir gae kaptan ke taur par apane pahale hi test maich mein rashid khan ne 11 viket chatakae kaptan ke taur par pahale test maich mein 1 se zyaada viket aur haf seanchuri lagane vale ve duniyaa ke pahale kriketr ban gae haian

afganistan ki kriket tim ki ye upalabdhi islie bhi bemisal hai kyoanki tim ke zyaadatr khilaadiyon ka bachapan sharanarthi shiviron mein gujra hai  
kisi bhi riphyuji kaianp mein rahana aasan nahin hota, aapako kai tarah ki pabandiyon mein rahana hota hai aur har din ke bhojn ke lie sanghrsh karna hota hai kaianpon mein rahane vale har din isse bahr niklane ki praarthna karate haian  
afganistan ke zyaadatr kriketr inhin riphyuji kaianpon se nikle haian in kaianpon se niklakar afganistan ke kriketr varld kap tak pahuanche haian vaise kriket ka khel afganistan ke lie koi nayaa khel nahin hai  
aitihasik rikrd ke mutabik braitesh sainik afganistan mein 1 mein kriket khela karate the lekin braiten ke dusre upaniveshon ke ulat kriket afganistan mein apani jaadein majabut nahin kar payaa  
agar aap yuddh mein ghayl ho gae hon, kisi tarah jan bachi ho, bhukh aur garibi ki chapet mein hon tab to riphyuji kaianp mein thoadi madad mil sakati hai lekin jahan rojana astitv ka sankt ho, vahan ke laadke kriket ke bare mein kaise soch paeange ?  ye asanbhv zarur dikhta hai lekin namumkin nahin hai kyoanki afganistan ki maujuda kriket tim ke adhikaansh khilaadiyon ne yah kar dikhayaa hai  
afganistan eshiyaa ke pashchimi aur dakshini hisse ke bichoanbich sthit hai kold var ke dauran amarika aur rus, donon ki najarein afganistan par thian 1 mein soviyt sangh ne aphaganistan par kabja karne ki koshish bhi ki 
afganistan ne rus ki aakramkata ka purjor virodh kiyaa donon deshon ke bich 1 sal tak sanghrsh chala is dauran soviyt sangh ke virodhi amarika ne afganistan ke kabilayaai logon ki madad ki jab soviyt sangh ko pata chal gayaa ki afganistan ka jitna sanbhv nahin hoga tab jakr  1  mein usane apani sena ko vaps bula liyaa yah vah daur tha jab afganistan mein amarika ki bhi dilchaspi kam hone lagi thi   
amarika aur soviyt sangh ki dilchaspi afganistan mein nahin rahi, aise mein vahan koi sakshm sarakar banane se pahale kattrapanthi jamaat ne pure desh par kabja kar liyaa 1 se 1 ke bich mein afganistan par talibaniyon ka shasn raha

yah kevl shuruaat bhar thi afganistan kriket sangh ko iantrneshnal kriket kauansil yaani aaisisi se sanbanddhta milne ke lie chhah sal ka iantzar karna paada tha, aaisisi ke praavdhanon ke mutabik kam se kam tisre levl par pahuanchne ke bad hi tim ko sanbanddhta di jati hai 
udhar pakistani riphyuji kaianp mein taj malik ko ek or apani aajivika ke lie rojana sanghrsh karna paad raha tha vahin dusri or unake kandhon par tim ko kochiang dene ki zimmedari bhi thi afganistan ke kriketron mein apani majaduri ke sath sath kriket khelna jari rakha in khilaadiyon ke pas na to abhyaas ki suvidhaen thin aur na hi pratiyogitaon mein hissa lene ki suvidha lekin in khilaadiyon mein janmjat taileant tha aur unhoanne apani kaadi mehnat se taileant ko nikhara bhi 
duniyaa bhar ki kai desh aaisisi se sanbanddh tim ke taur par kriket khelte haian unhein pratiyogitaon mein khelne ka mauka milta hai in timon ke sath khelna itna aasan nahin hota lekin afganistan ne apana sanghrsh jari rakha  mein afganistan tim ka chayan varld kriket lig ke divijn  mein khelne ke lie huaa 
agale hi sal, unhein  11  varld kap mein hissa lene ke lie davedari karne ka mauka mil gayaa halaanki kanada ke khilaf patrta maich har jane ke chalate unhein  11  ke varld kap mein hissa lene ka mauka nahin mil payaa lekin afganistan ke lagatar achchhe pradarshn ke chalate aaisisi ne tim ko vanade khelne ki patrta de di 
1 mein tim ne varld tveanti- mein khelne ki patrta hasil kar li tim is turnameant ke shuruaati daur se aage nahin badh pai thi lekin kuchh khilaadiyon ke pradarshn par duniyaa bhar ki nazarein gain thian

1 mein aaisisi ne aphaganistan ka darja badhakr use esosiet sadasy bana diyaa pakistan kriket bord ne aphaganistan ke sath ek samajhauta kiyaa, jiske tahat vah afganistan mein treniang kaianp, aanpayriang aur pich kyuret karne ke lie kaianp lagane ke sath sath pratibhaon ki talash ke lie karykrm chalane ke lie taiyaar tha

shuruaati charan ke chhah maichon mein tim paanch maich har gai halaanki tim ko sktalaiand ko harane mein kamyaabi mili ise ausat pradarshn hi maana jaega lekin mahaj  sal pahale jis desh mein kriket ki shuruaat hui ho us tim ka kriket ke sabase baade turnameant mein hissa lena bhi baadi upalabdhi se kam nahin hai 
afganistan tim ka pradarshn lagatar behtar raha, ise dekhte hue  jun, 1 ko aaisisi ne use test khelne ki patrta bhi de di pichhle sal 1 se 1 jun ke bich beangluru mein afganistan ne bhart ke khilaf apana pahala test maich khela tha afganistan mahaj do dinon ke aandr yah test pari aur  rnon se har gayaa tha  lekin usake bad tim ne do test maichon mein shandar jit hasil ki hai
surksha karnon ke alava aaisisi ke str vale stediym maujud nahin hone ke chalate afganistan ko apani mejbani vale maichon ka aayojn kisi tisre desh mein karana paad raha hai apane gharelu maidan mein khelne ka mahatvpurn fayda har tim ko hota hai mejban tim apane hisab se pich bana sakati hai amumn vipkshi timon ki kamajoriyon ko dekhte hue pichein taiyaar ki jati hain taki gharelu tim ko phayda ho  
apane maidanon par khelne se gharelu darshkon ka saport bhi milta hai stediym bhare hue hote haian mejban kriket bord ko tikt bechne se aarthik phayda bhi hota hai lekin afganistan ko abhi tak yah sab fayda nahin huaa hai, kyoanki usane tisre desh mein maichon ki mejbani ki hai 
shuruaati daur mein, afganistan ki tim ko shrilanka ke daanbula ke ranagiri iantrneshnal stediym mein khelne ka mauka mila iske bad sharjah mein spin ki madad vali pich ko dekhte hue tim ne kuchh maichon ka aayojn vahan kiyaa lekin yah bhi asthayi hi raha 
iske bad afganistan kriket bord aur bhartiy kriket bord ke bich samajhauta huaa jiske tahat bisisiaai afganistani kriket tim ko maich aur abhyaas ke lie stediym muhaiyaa karaati hai 
afganistan ki kriket tim ne pahale gretr noeda ke shahid vijy sianh pathik sports kaanplaiks mein khelna shuru kiyaa tha yahan ki behtarin suvidhaon ko dekhte hue afganistan kriket bord ne ise apana gharelu maidan ghoshit kar diyaa tha 
1 mein afganistan kriket bord ne isi maidan par aayaralaiand ke sath paanch maichon ki siriz ka aayojn kiyaa tha isi maidan par afganistan ne namibiyaa ke sath kuchh abhyaas maich bhi khele lekin yah silsila lanba nahin chal payaa bisisiaai ne is maidan par praaivet lig ke aayojn ka havala dete hue unase yah maidan le liyaa iske bad afganistan bord ke samne phir se apane lie gharelu maidan ki talash ki chunauti thi 
ye talash dehradun ke rajiv gaandhi iantrneshnal kriket stediym par jakr puri hui hai, ab yah maidan tim ka gharelu maidan hai halaanki kai prashanskon ko is maidan ke bare mein jankari nahin hai kyoanki yah ek nayaa stediym hai dehradun ke shaant ilaqe se afganistan ki tim ne aantrarashtriy kriket mein purn darja vala safr shuru kiyaa hai dehradun kabhi apane aavasiy skulon ke lie mashahur raha hai, lekin ab yah afganistan kriket tim ka bhi thikana ban chuka hai  
is stediym mein afganistan ki tim baangladesh aur aayaralaiand ke khilaph siriz khel chuki hai tim ko apane desh ke samarthkon ke samne khelne ka mauka nahin mil raha hai lekin ve upalabdh viklpon pajitiv najarie se apana behtarin pradarshn de raha haian 
afganistan ke dheron logon ko pravasiyon jaisi ziandgi bitani paadi hai aur kamobesh yahi hal afganistani kriket tim ka bhi hai unaka saphar shrilanka ke daanbula kriket stediym se shuru hokr ab bhart ke dehradun tak pahuancha hai agar unake apane desh mein halat behtar hote hain aur vahan iantrneshnal kriket maichon ka aayojn shuru hota hai tab jakr afganistan kriket ko ek thikane se dusre thikane tak pahuanchne ka safr pura hoga

inmein shrilanka ki ti- tim ke kaptan lasith malianga aur vana-de tim ke kaptan dimuth karunartne bhi shamil haian
maarch  mein lahaur mein ek test maich ke dauran shrilanka tim ki bas par hue charamapanthi humale ke bad kai deshon ki timon ne pakistan mein khelne se mana kar diyaa hai
shrilanka kriket bord ne batayaa ki khilaadiyon ko surksha ke iantzamon ke bare mein batate hue kaha gayaa tha ki pakistan ke daure par jane yaa na jane ka faisla khilaadiyon par hi chhoad diyaa gayaa tha
bord ne batayaa ki iske bad 1 khilaadiyon ne nahin jane ka faisla kiyaa
 sitanbr se shuru hone vale daure mein shrilankai tim ko pakistan mein tin vana-de aur tin ti- maich khelna tha
ye daura kriket mezabani mein alaga-thalag paade pakistan ke lie baada ahum batayaa ja raha hai
vaise  ke humale ke bad shrilanka ki tim ek bar aur pakistan ja chuki hai
1 mein aktubr mein shrilanka ne lahaur mein ek ti- maich khela tha
magar us maich mein tim ki kaptani kar rahe thisara parera ne is dafa pakistan jane se inkar kar diyaa hai
shrilanka ko pakistan ke sath do test maich bhi khelna hai magar usaki tarikh aur jagah ka elan abhi nahin kiyaa gayaa hai
halanki shrilanka ke khel mantri harin frnaando ne pakistan mein test maich nahin khelna chahie aur agar khelna hai to sanyukt arab amiraat mein khelna chahie jahan pakistan kai test siriz khel chuka hai
ye bhi padheanh
lahaur humale se juade ho sakate hain tar
shrilankai tim par nahin, kriket par humala

test maich mein yah tim ki dusri jit hai
isse pahale usane aayaralaiand ke khilaf jit darj ki thi  
tim ke kaiptn rashid khan ko pleyr ph d maich chuna gayaa unhoanne aantim ovar mein baangladesh ke 11vein khilaadi ko aaut kiyaa 
afganistan tim ki is jit ko lanbe vaqt tak yaad rakha jaega
afganistan ne kul  rn banae, vahin baangladesh ki tim  rn hi bana pai
kaptan rashid ne maich mein kul 11 viket lie
test maich ke itihas mein rashid khan sabase yuva kaptan ban gae hain, jinhoanne tim ko jit dilai hai rashid ne 11 viket ke alava pahali pari mein 1 rn banae the
afganistan ne pahali pari mein  aur dusri pari mein  rn banae shakib al hasan ki kaptani vali baangladeshi tim pahali pari mein  aur dusri pari mein 1 rn bana pai
afganistan ne tin taist maich khele hain , jinmein se yah iski dusri jit hai usane apana debyu maich bhart ke khilaf khela tha, jismein tim ko har ka samna karna paada tha

1vin shatabdi ke asptal sankrman phailane ke keandr huaa karate the in asptalon mein bimaar aur mar rahe logon ko mahaj sadharn suvidhaen milti thian  
us daur mein gharon mein ilaj karana behtar viklp huaa karata tha asptalon mein gharon mein ilaj karane ki tulna mein tin se paanch guna jyaada mautein huaa karati thian
asptal peshab, ultiyon aur any apashishton ke durgandh se bhare hote the yah durgandh itni jyaada huaa karati thi ki asptal ke stph nak par rumaal daba kar chala karate the 
daktr bhi na to apane hath dhote the aur na hi apane upakaranon ki saphai kiyaa karate the pareshn vale kamare aur usamein kam karne vale sarjn, ek samaan gande huaa karate the 
in sabaki vajah se, asptalon ko maut ka ghar kaha jane laga tha us jamaane mein log roganu ke bare mein kuchh nahin jante the, bavjud iske ek shakhs ne sankrman ko rokne ke lie vaijnanik tarikon ka istemaal kiyaa tha
ignaj semelvis namk hangri ke ek daktr ne 1 mein viyna mein hath dhone ki vyvastha ko lagu kiyaa tha, iske chalate maitrniti vard mein hone vali mautein kam ho gai thian 
yah ek ahum koshish thi lekin kamyaab nahin ho pai thi, kyoanki daktr ke sahayogiyon ne hi unaka sath nahin diyaa tha lekin tab tak ignaj ki pahachan navajat bachchon ko janm dene vali maaanon ko bachane vale daktr ki ban chuki thi 
semelvis tab viyna janaral haspitl mein kam karate the us haspitl mein bhi dusre haspitlon ki tarah niymit rup se marijon ki maut hoti thi 
duniyaa ko 1vin shatabdi mein roganuon ke bare mein pata nahin tha, tab daktr yah maanne ko taiyaar nahin hote the ki asptalon ki gandgi ki vajah se sankrman phailta hai 
nyuyaark yunivrsiti mein histri ph medisin ke ekspart bairn echa larnr ne bbc ko batayaa, "aisi duniyaa ki kalpna behd mushkil hai jab humalog roganu aur baiktiriyaa ke astitv ke bare mein kuchh bhi nahin jante the"
"1vin shatabdi ke madhy mein, maana jata tha ki bimaariyaan jaharile vashp se phailti hain, jismein hanikark kan maujud hote haian"
us vakt mein navajat bachchon ko janm dene vali maaanon ke sankrmit hone ka khatara sabase jyaada hota tha, khaskar un maaanon mein jinmein prasav ke lie chirphaad karne ki jarurt hoti thi iske chalate hone vale jakhm, un baiktiriyon ke pasandida thikana huaa karate the jinhein daktr aur sarjn apane sath lekr chalate the 
semelvis ne sabase pahale viyna janaral haspitl ke samaan suvidhaon vale do prasuti keandron mein hone vali mauton ke aantr ko notis kiyaa tha
ek keandr mein dekhbhal ki jimmedari purush medikl chhatron ke havale thi jabaki dusre keandr ki jimmedari daiyon ke havale thi jis keandr ki jimmedari purush medikl chhatron ke pas thi vahan 1 mein prati 1 janm mein  mautein huaa karati thin jabaki dusre prasuti keandr mein yah 1 janm mein kevl  tha  
is aanstuln ki vajah mein yah kaha jata tha ki apane marijon ke sath purush medikl chhatr kahin jyaada rukhe dhang se pesh aate the
purush medikl chhatron ke rukhe dhang se dekhbhal karne ke chalate maana jata tha ki mahilaon mein bukhar aa jata hai, yuters mein ianphekshn ho jata hai, is vajah se hi asptal mein navajat bachchon ko janm dene vali maaanon mein hone vali mauton ke lagabhag sabhi maamle samne aa rahe the   
semelvis aadhikarik spshtikran se santusht nahin hue the isi sal, unake ek sahayogi ki maut bhi hui thi ek postmaartm karne ke dauran sahayogi ke hath mein kat lag gayaa tha, jiske chalate unaki maut ho gai thi is hadse se semelvis ko kuchh samajhane ka sanket mila 
us jamaane mein sharir ke kisi hisse mein kat lagana, sharirik jokhim ke sath janleva bhi hota tha 
sharir ke kisi hisse ko chaku se katna, chahe kitna hi barik kyon na ho, humesha ke lie khatarnak ho sakata tha, chahe vo sharir vijnan ka anubhvi chikitsk hi kyon na ho  
udahran ke lie charls darvin ke chacha, jinka nam bhi charls darvin hi tha, unaki maut 1 mein ek bachche ke sharir ko chir phaad karne ke dauran lage jakhm ke chalate hui thi 
viyna mein apane sahakarmi ki maut ke bad, semelvis ne yah notis kiyaa ki unake sahakarmi mein bhi vahi lakshn pae gae, the jo prasav ke dauran mahilaon mein aane vale bukhar mein dekha gayaa tha 
iske bad unake man mein yahi saval utha ki kyaa shavon ke sath chirphaad karne ke dauran sanprk mein aae shav ke kanon ko daktr prasuti kakshon tak lekr aate hain? 
semelvis ne dekha ki medikl chhatr postmaartm vale kamare se niklakar sidhe prasuti keandron mein jate rahate haian  
us vakt mein koi bhi daktr yaa karmchari galavs nahin pahanate the, koi dusra surkshatmk upakaran nahin tha, aise mein shavon ke sath chiadphaad karne ke dauran medikl chhatron ke kapaadon par maaans ke tukade yaa phir tishyu ka chipkana aam bat thi
daiyon ko shav ke sath parikshn ke nahin karna hota tha kyaa yahi vo rahasy ki kuanji thi jo semelvis ko sata rahi thi? 
tab roganuon ke bare mein koi samajh nahin thi, aise mein asptalon ki gandgi ko dur karne ka rasta nikalna behd mushkil tha 
prasuti chikitsik jems vai simpsan 111-1 pahale aise phijishiyn the jinhoanne manushyon par klorophrm ke behosh karne vale gunon ka prayog kiyaa tha 
unaka maanna tha ki gandgi ke chalate phailne vale sankrman ko agar niyantrit nahin kiyaa ja sakata to samay samay par asptalon ko puri tarah se nasht karake nae sire se taiyaar karna chahie 
1vin sadi ke sabase mashahur sarjn aur d saians eand aart ph sarjri 1 ke lekhk jan irik iriksn ne isse sahumati jatate hue likha tha, "ek bar jab asptal puri tarah se dushit rakt vale baiktiriyon se sankrmit ho jae to use kisi tarah se bhi svchchh nahin kiyaa ja sakata yah thik vaisi sthiti hogi jaisi chiantiyon ke kabje vali dhahati hui divar ko chiantiyo se mukt karana ho yaa phir purane panir ke tukade mein utpnn kiadon se panir ko svchchh karna"
semelvis, aise kathor upayon ko aavashyk nahin maante the halaanki ve is natije tak pahuanch chuke the ki shavon ke sankrmit kan hi prasuti vali mahilaon mein bukhar ki vajah haian unhoanne asptal mein ek besin lagavayaa jahan klorin yukt chune ka ghol rakha huaa tha 
shavon ke chirphaad vale kamare se prasuti kaksh mein jane vale daktron ke lie yah zaruri tha ki ve is ghol se khud ko saph kar lein, hathon ko dho le
1 mein medikl chhatron ki dekhbhal vale vard mein 1 prasuti mein mauton ki sankhyaa ghatakar 1 rah gai thi 
bavjud iske semelvis apane sahakarmiyon ko yah nahin samajha pae ki prasuti ke dauran mahilaon ke bukhar ka nata shavon ke chirphaad ke dauran hone vale dushit sankrman se hai 
apane hi tarikon ki jaanch karne vale log kai bar chizon ko thik dhang se pesh nahin karate the, jiske chalate parinam utsahvardhk nahin hote 
bairn ech larnr batate hain, "dhyaan dijie ki ve kyaa kah rahe the- bhale ve inhin shabdon mein nahin kah rahe hon lekin ve ve yahi kah rahe the ki medkil chhatr prasuti ke lie aa rahi mahilaon ki hatyaa kar rahe hain, ise svikar karna behd mushkil tha"
vastv mein prasuti keandron mein sankrman rokne ke lie pratirodhi sabunon ka istemaal 1 ke dashak mein shuru ho payaa tha
is vishy par semelvis ne ek kitab likhi, jiski kai nakaraatmk samikshaon ke bad ve apane aalochkon par bhaadk gae unhoanne hath nahin dhone vale daktron ko hatyaare ke rup mein rekhaankit karna shuru kiyaa
iske bad viyna haspitl mein semelvis ka anubandh nahin badhayaa gayaa aur unhein apane desh hangri lautna paada 
hangri lautne ke bad semelvis budapest ke ek chhote se asptal mein sejeant roks haspitl ke prasuti vard mein avaitink kam karne lage 
is asptal aur budapest yunivrsiti ke maitrniti klinik jahan ve bad mein padhane lage the mein prasuti ke dauran mahilaon ke bukhar se grsit hone ki sankhyaa bahut jyaada thi, lekin semelvis ne ise apane dam par khatm kar diyaa 
lekin unake siddhaant ki aalochna thami nahin aur dusri or sahayogi unake tarike ko apanane ko anichchhuk the, is bat ko lekr semelvis ka gussa bhi badhta ja raha tha 
11 aate aate unaka vyvahar bahut anishchit ho gayaa aur char sal bad unhein paglakhane mein bharti karane ki naubt aa gai unaka ek sahayogi unhein nae medikl ianstityut dikhane ke bahane viyna ke paglakhane le gayaa
jab semelvis ko mahasus huaa ki ve paglakhane mein hain to unhoanne vahan se niklane ki koshish ki is koshish mein vahan ke surkshagardon ne unhoanne buri tarike se pita aur iske bad unhein janjiron mein jakaadkar aandheri kothri mein dal diyaa gayaa
do saptah bad, semelvis ki maut daen hath ke jakhm mein phaile sankrman se ho gai thi ve mahaj  sal ke the chikitsa vijnan mein lui pashchr, josef listr aur rarbt koch jis tarah ka badalav lekr aae usamein semelvis koi bhumika nahin nibha pae

ye vishy pahali bar mein hasyaaspd lag sakata hai lekin ye koi chhoti bat nahin hai
ek ausat vykti apani puri ziandgi mein chhah mahine se zyaada ka vaqt tayalet mein bitata hai aur har sal taqribn 1 kilo mal tyaag karata hai iska matalab ye huaa ki ek ausat vykti har sal apane sharir ke bhar ke doguna mal tyaag karata hai
ummid hai ab tak aapako ye samajh aa gayaa ki ye vishy humaare lie kitna mahatvpurn hai aap jante hain ki tayalet mein baithne ka sahi tariqa kyaa hai
ye bat to tay hai ki humamein se har koi tayalet mein thik se nahin baithta 
vin sadi ke madhy mein yuropiy daktron ki ek tim afrika ke gramin ilaqon mein kam kar rahi thi daktr ye dekh kar hairan the ki vahan ke sthaniy logon ko pachn aur pet se juadi takalifein n ke barabr thian
duniyaa ke any kai vikasshil deshon mein bhi aisa hi payaa gayaa daktron ne pata lagayaa ki ye sirf khane mein aantr ki vajah se nahin tha balki logon ke tayalet istemaal karne ke tariqe aur mal tyaag karate samay baithne ki pozishn mein aantr ki vajah se bhi tha
pashchimi deshon mein log jitni bar tayalet mein jate hain, ausatan vo vahan 11-1 sekeand bitate haian iske ulat, bhart samet kai vikasshil deshon mein log tayalet mein ukaadun hokr mal tyaag karate hain aur mahaz 1 sekeand mein nibt lete haian 
vikasshil deshon ke shauchalyon ka dizain bhi aisa hota hai ki use istemaal karne ke lie aapako ukaadun baithna hota hai visheshjnon ka maanna hai ki ukaadun baithne vala tariqa behtar hai
jab hum tayalet sit par baithte hain to humaari guda nalika  aansh ke kon par hoti hai is vajah se humaari maaanspeshiyon mein khianchav hota hai yahi vajah hai ki humamein se kai log tayalet mein baithne par tanav mahasus karate haian
is tanav ki vajah se kai logon ko bavasir, behoshi aur yahan tak ki daure aane jaisi takalifein bhi ho jati haian 
aisa maana jata hai ki pahala sadharn tayalet sabase pahale taqribn  hazar sal pahale mesopotiyaa mein mila tha 
san 1 tak rom mein 1 sarvjanik shauchaly the aur bathrum jana samaajik chalan jaisa ho gayaa tha
pahala flsh vala tayalet sal 1 mein braiten ke jan hairiangtan ne banayaa tha unhoanne ise d ejaiks ka nam diyaa tha 
iske bad varsh 1 mein thams kraipr ne yu-beand ka aavishkar kiyaa aur is aavishkar ke sath bahut kuchh badal gayaa 
yu-beand sidhe tayalet ke niche se mal nikal deta tha aur isse badabu nahin aati thi
is tarah pashchaty shaili ke tayalet yuropiy sabhyta ka pratik ban gae lekin isse kuchh chizein mushkil bhi ho gaian
humamein se bahut log tayalet sit par baithkar gusse mein is tarah daant bhianchte hain aur itna zor lagate hain ki humaare nasein suj jati hain aur dil ki dhaadkanein tez ho jati haian
aisa qbz, badahazami, apach yaa pet ki dusri dikqton ki vajah se bhi ho sakata hai lekin kai visheshjnon ka maanna hai ki yuropiyn shaili ke tayalet bhi aisi samsyaaon ke lie kafi had tak zimmedar haian
1 ke madhy mein kornel yunivrsiti ke praofesr elekzeandr kira ne yuropiy shaili ke tayalets ko sabase buri dizain mein banai gai chiz kaha 
mashahur amariki kalakar elvis praesli ke daktr ka kahana tha ki jis dil ke daure se unaki maut hui thi, vo unhein tayalet mein zyaada zor lagane ki vajah se paada tha
itni sari baadi-baadi samsyaaon ka bahut aasan sa hal hai agar aap yuropiy shaili ke tayalet mein baithte hain to bas itna kijie ki apane ghutnon ko  digri ke bajay  digri kon par moad lijie isse aapake pet aur guda par zor kam paadega aur chizein aasan ho jaeangi
iske lie aap tayalet mein ek chhota sa paydan rakh sakate hain aur apane pair is par tika sakate haian agar aap jaldi mein yaa kahin bahr nahin hain to god mein moti kitabon ka ek bandl yaa aisi hi koi chiz rakh sakate haian
yaani kitabein aur patrikaen tayalet mein bhi kam aa sakati hain!

riport mein sujhav diyaa gayaa hai ki laanchhn ko kam karne ke lie iske lie istemaal hone vale sanbodhn shabdon ko badalana chahie jaise mota vykti ki jagah motape se grst vykti kaha jae
ismein ye bhi kaha gayaa hai ki svasthy karmiyon ko is bat ka prashikshn diyaa jae ki vo vazan kam karne ki bat bahut sahara dene vale aandaz mein karean 
asal mein hal hi mein kaiansr chairiti sanstha ne ek vijnapn abhiyaan shuru kiyaa tha jismein motape par tanz kasane fait shemiang ke lie usaki kafi aalochna ki gai thi 
sal  se 1 ke bich braiten mein motape ka str 1 badha hai aur sktalaiand, vels aur uttri aayaralaiand mein bhi isi anupat mein badhottri hui hai 
yaani, braiten mein char vayaskon mein se ek motape ka shikar hai jabaki do tihai ka vazan zarurt se zyaada hai yaa vo mote haian 
braitish saikoljikl sosaiti ki riport mein kaha gayaa hai ki lekin is badhottri ke pichhe pure braiten mein achank hatotsahit hona karn nahin hai, balki ye usase bhi kahin jatil gutthi hai 
riport mein natija nikala gayaa hai ki kisi vykti mein ichchhashkti ki kami aana iska karn nahin hai 
riport mein kaha gayaa hai ki un logon mein vazan badhne ki sabase adhik aashanka hoti hai jinmein motapa viksit hone ka anuvaanshik khtara adhik hota hai yaa jinki ziandgi mein kam ka dabav, skul aur samaajik maahaul ka dabav adhik hota hai, jisse unamein adhik khane aur nishkriy rahane ki ichchha paida hoti hai  
iske anusar, "garib ilaqon mein rahane vale logon mein  ziandgi mein baade badalav aur sadame ki vajah se tanav ka str bahut adhik hota hai inke aas paados mein bhi mauqe kam hote hain aur sharirik vyaayaam aur poshn yukt saste khane ki suvidha bahut simit hoti hai"
riport mein kaha gayaa hai ki ismein maansik anubhv ki bhi ek baadi bhumika hoti hai motape se chhutkara pane ke lie svasthy seva ki madad lene vale aadhe vayaskon ka bachapan mushkilon se guzara hota hai  
iske alava sarvjanik svasthy abhiyaanon, narson, janaral fijishiyn aur niti nirmaataon ki vajah se, adhik vazan ke karn sharmiandgi jhelne se paida hone vale tanav ka natija aksr ye hota hai ki khane ki aadat badh jati hai aur vazan bhi badh jata hai
braitish kamediyn jems kardn ne hal hi mein fait shemiang ke khilaf bola tha unhoanne kaha tha, "agar mote logon ka mazaq uadane se unaka vazan kam hota to skulon mein kabhi koi mota bachcha hota hi nahian"
is riport ko taiyaar karne vale lekhk aur betfordshayr vishvvidyaaly mein saikolji aur bihaiviyr dizain ke ridr manochikitsk da eangel chaitr ka kahana hai ki manochikitsk apani visheshjnta ka istemaal svasthy karmiyon ko prashikshit karne mein kar sakate hain taki vo motape ke bare mein behtar sanvad kar paean 
vo kahati hain, "agar motape ka ilaj bahut aasan hota, to hum ye bat nahin kar rahe hote aur ye riport nahin taiyaar karni paadti"
unake anusar, "ho sakata hai ki aapaki ichchha shakti puri duniyaa mein sabase adhik ho lekin agar aapako sehtamand bhojn, sahi maahaul, ek achchhi shuruaati ziandgi nahin upabaldh hai to ye bahut mushkil hai"
riport mein kaha gayaa hai ki sarakar ko motape ke bare mein vahi rukh apanana chahie jo dhumrpan ko lekr vo apanati hai  
braitish saikoljikl sosaiti ke mukhy karykari adhikari sarb bajva ke anusar, "dashakon se sabhi stron par isne ehatiyaat barate haian sarakari nitiyon se lekr dhumrpan karne vale ek ek vykti ki madad karne tak, lekin ab hum dekh rahe hain ki dhumrpan ke str mein kafi kami aai hai aur iske karn aane vali svasthygat dikqtein bhi kam hui haian"
"thik isi tarah motape se niptane ke lie svasdhy seva ki madad ke lie manochikitskon ke pas vijnan aur klinikl anubhv paryaapt haian"
"hum madad kar sakate hain, vyktigt logon ko madad pahuanchane ke raste nikalne se lekr sarvjanik niti banane tak mein, joki aisa maahaul paida kar sakata hai jismein log adhik vazan se aasani se bach sakean"

amarika ke krishi vibhag ke anusar sal 1 ke bad se desh mein dudh ki khapat mein  fisdi ki kami aai hai

braitish nyutrishn phauandeshn ke mutabiq, bachchon aur baadon ko jitni maatra mein aayarn, kailshiym, vitamin, ziank aur aayodin ki zarurt hoti hai, vah unaka khana pura nahin kar pata hai aur dudh mein yah sabakuchh payaa jata hai

yah bachchon ke lie kailshiym ka ek achchha srot bhi hai garbhvati mahilaon ko ise pine ki salah di jati hai kyoanki yah bhrun ki haddiyon ke nirmaan aur usake vikas mein madad karata hai
 mililitr dudh ke ek glas mein karib  miligram kailshiym hota hai, jo ek se tin sal tak ke bachchon ki dainik zarurt ka aadha hai

 shilajit ko saf yaa filtr karne ka kam

gazi is puri prakriyaa ke bare mein kahate hain ki "jab banda niche gupha mein utarata hai to niche usake baithne ki jagah hoti hai shilajit nikalne ke bad bori mein dalte hain aur phir pahale boriyon ko upar bhejte hain aur usake bad hum khud vaps usi rassi ke zariye upar chale jate haian" 
is puri prakriyaa mein lagabhag aadha ghanta laga lekin us aadhe ghante ke bare mein vo kahate hain ki "agar rassi bandhte hue kisi ne girh sahi nahin lagai hui ho yaa sefti belt thik n bandhi hui ho to rassi ke khul jane ki aashanka zyaada hoti hai"

is prakriyaa mein un baade patthron ke, jinhein pahaad se layaa gayaa hota hai, chhote tukade kie jate hain aur use ek baadi balti ke aandr dalkar ek nishcht maatra mein pani milakr baade chammch se hilayaa jata hai taki shilajit achchhi tarah se us pani mein ghul jae

"aam taur par lalch, jaldbazi aur paisa kamaane ke chakkr mein log is pani ko sirf kisi kapaade mein se chhankar aur tin se char ghante ke lie ubalte hain jisse vah jaldi gadha ho jata hai aur is tarah yah shilajit taiyaar ho jati hai magar iska fayda kam aur nuqsan zyaada hai"

unake anusar "yahi humaari kamyaabi ka raz hai ki hum shuddh shilajit banate haian"
filtreshn ke bad shilajit ke pani ko ek shishe se bane hue khanon mein rakhate hain aur taqribn ek mahine tak usaka pani sukhta rahata hai jis dauran vah us baratan mein aur bhi shilajit ka pani dalte rahate hain taki vah bhar jae aur yun aaftabi shilajit taiyaar hoti hai jise paikiang ke bad dukanadaron ko saplai kiyaa jata hai

"usaki maatra badhane ke lie log aksr usamein aata vagairh bhi istemaal karate haian aur agar usamein bhi shilajit ki thoadi maatra mila di gai ho to usamein se bhi vaisi hi gandh aaegi jo asali shilajit se aati hai"

 varshon tak kie gae ek adhyyan mein pata chala hai ki jangli gehun mein kuchh faydemand badalav hue hain jinmein badhe hue tapmaan ke anusar dhalana shamil hai

is shodh ke natije praosidiangs f d neshnal akaidmi f saiansez mein  prakashit kie gae haian 
egriklchr eand egri-fud kanada ke ek vaijnanik aur is shodh ke mukhy lekhk yoang-bi fu kahate hain, "humein kuchh bahut hi utsahjanak natije dekhne ko mile haian"

halaanki tim ne adhyyan mein payaa ki alaga-alag namunon ne alaga-alag tarah se pratikryaa di inmein kuchh garm vatavran aur usase juadi paristhitiyon mein nahin bach sake jabaki kuchh aise the jo garm paristhitiyon ka samna karne aur unamein puri tarah se dhalane mein sakshm the
is adhyyan ke tahat israil mein emar gehun ki 1 alag phasalein shamil ki gai thian
da fu ka kahana hai ki tin dashakon mein prithvi ke tapmaan mein do digri selsiys ki badhotri hui hai

"yah myuteshn mahatvpurn hai, aur hum dekh sakate hain ki humein jangli v praakritik jagahon par phasalon ki vividhta ko bachae rakhane ke lie bahut prayaas karne ki zarurt hai"
tim ka kahana hai ki is shodh ke natije humein yah batane mein madad karate hain ki paudhe kis tarah se bhavishy mein hone vale jalavayu parivrtn ke hisab se khud ko dhal sakate haian
da fu ne gret braiten ke vaijnanikon ke kam ka bhi zikr kiyaa jo kheton mein ugai jane vali phasalon mein bimaariyon ke lie pratirodhk kshmata lane ke lie unaki jangli qismon se rog-pratirodhk jin klon karne ki koshish kar rahe haian
unhoanne kaha ki yahi tarika apanakr jangli qismon se jalavayu parivrtn rodhi jins ko klon karake yaa khadyaann paida karne vali maujuda phasalon ko bhi jalavayu parivrtn rodhi banayaa ja sakata hai yah kam krsa-braidiang se bhi ho sakata hai

1 mein rayal sosaiti bayolji letrs jarnl mein prakashit hue ek adhyyan mein duniyaa ke lie paryaapt bhojn ugane ki kshmata par saval uthate hue jalavayu parivrtn se paida hue jokhim par prakash dala gayaa tha
amariki shodhkartaon ki tim ne payaa tha ki  tak jalavayu mein bahut jaldi badalav hoange, ghas aur phasalon ki prajatiyaan nai paristhitiyon ke hisab se khud ko dhal nahin paeangi
