lekin kuchh logon ko aaifon 11 mein lage tripl kaimra ka dizain thoada khatak raha hai ismein traipophobiyaa namk bimaari se grsit log adhik haian
daraasal traipophobiyaa ek tarah ka dar hota hai, jismein chhote chhidron yaa aayaaton se bane jiyomaitrik paitrn kisi shakhs ko pareshan karate haian 
yahi vajah hai ki aaifon 11 ke tripl kaimra ka dizain kuchh logon ko pareshan kar sakata hai
traipophobiyaa se hone vale dar aur pareshani ka sabase udahran kamal ke phul mein dikhne vale bich hain, usamein chhote-chhote chhidr hote hain jo ek khas paitrn se lage hote haian chhidron ka yah paitrn traipophibiyaa se piadit iansan ko pareshan karne lagata hai
isi tarah madhumkkhi ke chhatte par jis tarah ke paitrn bone hote hain, yah bhi kuchh logon ke lie pareshani ka sabab ban jate haian
praophesr arnold vilkians aur daktr jiof kol eseks yunivrsiti mein shodharthi haian inka maanna hai ki kisi khas paitrn se nafrat karna yaa usase darna ek tarah se humaare sharir ki rakshatmk pratikriyaa hoti hai 
ise samajhane ke lie yah donon shodharthi batate hain ki kai logon ko makaadi, saanp yaa bichchhu se dar lagata hai in janvaron ke sharir par bhi isi tarah ke paitrn bane hote haian 
isi dar ki vajah se in logon ko is paitrn mein dikhne vali any chizon yaa aakritiyon se bhi dar lagane lagata hai
halaanki is tarah ke dar ko chikitskiy tarike se pahachana nahin ja sakata, ise paitrn fobiyaa bhi kahate haian
vaise is bar lanch hue aaifon 11, aaifon 11 prao aur aaifon 11 prao maiks ki sabase khas bat usaka tripl kaimra hi hai in kaimron ki madad se ek hi vaqt mein maltipl vidiyo rikrd kie ja sakate haian
aaifon 11 ke prao madal mein teliphoto, vaid aur altra vaid kaimre bhi haian iske sath hi inmein nait mod ke lie alag se pshn hai, jiski madad se kam roshni mein bhi achchhi tasvirein khichin ja sakati haian
lekin aaifon 11 ke ye tamaam dilchasp pahalu un logon ke lie kisi bure sapane ki tarah hain jinhein chhidron ke paitrn se dar lagata hai, jinhein traipophobiyaa hai
in logon ko ye paitrn dekhkar ulti jaisa mahasus hone lagata hai, unaki hridyagati badh jati hai aur chakkr aane lagate haian 
yahi vajah hai ki kuchh logon ne aaifon 11 na khridne ka faisla kiyaa hai
aise hi kuchh logon ne soshl midiyaa par is sanbandh mein apane vichar bhi sajha kie haian 
in logon ne batayaa hai ki jab vo nae aaifon ke baik par lage kaimron ko dekhte hain to unhein kaisa mahasus hota hai
amarika ke nyuyrk shahar mein rahane vali ek chhatra batayaa ki aaiphon ke purane madals se unhein kabhi koi pareshani nahin huaa lekin aaifon 11 ka madal unhein daravna lagata hai 
isi tarah ek mahila ne aaifon 11 prao ke kaimron ki tasvir tvitr par post karate hue likha ki kyaa ye bura lagata hai
aaifon  yaa aaifon xr mein siangl riyr kaimra hai, usamein kuchh alag tarah ka paitrn nahin hai 
jabaki aaifon 11 ke prao aur maiks varjn mein tin kaimre ek khas paitrn mein set kie gae hain, jiski vajah se traipophobiyaa se grsit logon ko pareshani mahasus ho rahi hai
aaiphon ke dizainron ne jab tripl kaimra ko dizain kiyaa to unhoanne is durlbh sthiti ke bare mein shayd nahin socha 
aaifon 11 ke tripl kaimra paitrn ko dekhne ke bad bahut se logon ne traipophobiyaa ke bare mein likhna shuru kiyaa hai kuchh logon ne mazakiyaa aandaz mein aaifon 1 ki tasvir ki kalpna ki hai
yah tasvir traipophobiyaa se grsit logon ko aur zyaada daravni lag sakati hai
daktr jiof kol kahate hain, hum sabhi kisi n kisi str par traipophobiyaa ka shikar hote haian humaara dar is bat par nirbhr karata hai ki hum use kitna sahan kar pate haian
amarika mein harar kahaniyon ki ek siriz ki abhinetri sara palasan aur madal keandl jenr bhi un logon mein shamil hain jinhein traipophobiyaa hai

ye parajivi maada machchhr ke katne se logon mein phailte haian
is bimaari se sankrmit hone par logon ko tez bukhar aata hai aur kanpkanpa dene vali thand lagati hai iske any lakshnon mein enimiyaa bhi shamil hai

vishv ne pahale hi maleriyaa ke khilaf kafi pragati kar li hai 
ye sab machchhron ke katne ko rokne ke tarikon ke karn huaa hai jaise ki kitnashk se machchhron ko maarna, machchhron se bachakar sone ke lie jali ka istemaal karna aur bimaar vyktiyon ko behtar davaiyaan muhaiyaa karana

"yah bat vishesh rup se aphrika ke lie hai, jahan sirf paanch desh vaishvik bojh ka lagabhag aadha hissa hain"

braitish medikl jarnl mein prakashit is shodh mein 1 salon tak  hazar logon ka adhyyan kiyaa gayaa
prati hazar maaans khane valon ki tulna mein vign aur shakahari logon mein hridy ki dhamaniyon siechadi se juade rogon ke 1 kam maamle mile, jabaki strok ke tin adhik maamle pae gae
dait ekspart ka kahana hai ki log shakahari hon yaa maaansahari, unhein vibhinn prakar ki chizein khani chahie, jo unake svasthy ke lie labhdayk hoti haian
ismein ipiaaisi-ksphord ke adhyyan ke aaankadon ka vishleshn kiyaa gayaa hai ipiaaisi-ksphord aahar aur svasthy par ki jane vali ek pramukh dirghkalik shodh pariyojna hai
adhyyan mein shamil aadhe log maaansahari the, jinhein sal 1 se 1 ke bich ismein shamil kiyaa gayaa tha 1 hazar log vign aur shakahari the iske alava  hazar vaise log the, jinhoanne khud ko peseteriyn batayaa, yaani ve machhali to khate the par maaans nahian
un sabhi se shuruaat mein unake aahar ke bare mein puchha gayaa, phir yahi jankari sal 1 mein unase dobara li gai
sirf aahar hi nahin, unake svasthy ka itihas kaisa raha tha, dhrumpan aur sharirik gatividhiyon tak ke bare mein jankari li gai
kul milakr hridy ki dhamaniyon se juade rogon siechadi ke  maamle pae gae vahin strok ke 1 maamle mile, jinmein se dimaag ki nas ke phat jane ke  maamle bhi shamil the
maaansahariyon ki tulna mein peseteriyn mein hridy ki dhamaniyon se juade rogon ka 1 fisdi kam jokhim payaa gayaa, jabaki vign aur shakahari logon mein yah jokhim  fisdi kam tha
lekin shakahari logon mein strok ka jokhim  fisdi adhik payaa gayaa shodhkartaon ke mutabiq yah vitamin bi-1 ki kami ki vajah se ho sakata hai lekin unhoanne yah bhi kaha ki is bat ki pushti ke lie aur adhik adhyyan ki zarurt thi
yah bhi sanbhv hai ki rogon ke jokhim ka logon ki dait se koi lena-dena n ho aur yah sirf unalogon ke jine ke tariqon ke aantr ko darshata ho, jo maaans nahin khate haian
braitish daitetik esosieshan ke da phraianki philips is saval ka javab na mein deti hain kyoanki yah ek aisa adhyyan tha, jismein logon par nazar rakhi gai thi
vo kahati hain, "unhoanne varshon tak logon ke khan-pan par nazar rakhi islie yah ek vajah ho sakati hai lekin yah koi karn aur prabhav nahin hai"
"logon ko ek behtar yojna bana kar aahar aur vibhinn prakar ke khady padarthon ka sevn karna chahie"
"maaans khane valon logon ke lie zaruri nahin hai ki ve har raat alaga-alag tarah ke aahar lein kyoanki ve bina sabjiyon ke maaans aur aalu khakr ji sakate haian"
sal 1 mein shodhkarta adhyyan mein shamil pratibhagiyon ke pas dobara gae aur unase unake dait ke bare mein puchha
lekin da philips ka kahana hai ki vign aur shakahari logon ke dait badal gae hoange
vo kahati hain, "yah vah deta hai jo kuchh dashakon pahale ekatrit kiyaa gayaa tha"
"yah ho sakata hai ki aaj ka shakahari bhojn  se  sal pahale ke shakahari bhojn aur vign se bahut alag ho"
"vign aur shakahari aaharon ki shreni mein baade paimaane par badalava aayaa hai"
praosesd aur red mit zyaada khane se kaiansr ke khtare badhte haian
shakahari aur maaansahari logon ke lie santulit aahar kyaa hona chahie, iska jikr braitish neshnal helth sarvis ki itvel gaid mein kiyaa gayaa hai
lekin vign aur shakahari logon ko kuchh atirikt poshk tatvon ki zarurt hoti hai
udahran ke lie jo log maaans, deyri praodkt aur machhali khate hain unhein aamataur par vitamin bi-1 ki kami nahin hoti yah svasth khun aur narvs sistm ke lie zaruri hota hai
vign ko iski kami ho sakati hai, halaanki vo bi-1 ke lie kai mote anaj vala nashta kar sakate haian
jo log maaans khana pasand nahin karate hain unhein pure anaj se bane aate ki roti, drai phruts aur dal khani chahie

vaijnanikon ne maiksiko ki khaadi se mile ek 1 mitr ki chattan ke ek tukade ka parikshn kiyaa hai 
is chattan mein maujud kuchh aise tatv mile hain jinke bare mein batayaa ja raha hai  ki  karoad sal pahale ek baade kshudrgrh aistraid ke prithvi se takarane ke bad yah jamaa hui thi
iske prabhav ka aandaza is bat se lagayaa ja sakata hai ki yah vahi ulkapiand hai jiske karn vishalkal daynasor vilupt ho gae the  is ulka piand se takarane se vahan 1 kilomitr chauada aur  kilomitr gahara gaddha ban gayaa tha
braitish aur amariki risrchron ki ek tim ne gaddhe kretra ki jagah par driliang karne mein hafton lagae 
in vaijnanikon ne jo natije nikale usamein pahale ke adhyyanon ki hi pushti hui, jinmein pahale hi is vinashkari praakritik ke bare mein vishleshn kiyaa ja chuka hai 
lagabhag  kilomitr chauada kretr maiksiko ke yukatn praaydvip mein hai iske sabase achchhe se sanrkshit ilaqa chikshulub ke bandragah ke pas hai
vaijnanikon ne jis chattan ka adhyyan kiyaa vo senozoik yug ka pramaan ban gayaa hai jise stnapayi yug ke nam se bha jana jata hai 
ye chattan bahut se bikhre hue tatvon ka ek mishrn hai, lekin risrchron ka kahana hai ki ye is tarah se bante hue hain ki ye inke avayavon ki pahachan ho jati hai
niche se pahale  mitr mein zyaadatr kaanchdar malaba hai, jo garmi aur takkr ke dabav ke karn pighli chattanon se bana hai
iska agala hissa pighli chattanon ke tukade se bana hai yaani us visphot ke karn jo garam tatvon par pani paadne se huaa tha ye pani us samay vahan maujud uthale samandr se aayaa tha 
shayd us samay is ulka piand ke girne ke karn pani bahr gayaa lekin jab ye garm chattan par vaps lauta, ek tivr kriyaa hui hogi ye vaisa hi tha jaisa jvalamukhi ke samay hota hai jab maigmaa mithe pani ke samprk mein aata hai 
daynasor ki sadhe chhah fit lanbi jaangh ki haddi mili 
vaijnanikon ka maanna hai ki is prabhav ke pahale ek ghante mein yah sabhi ghatanaen ghati hoangi lekin usake bad bhi pani bahr aakar us kretr ko bharata raha hoga
is chattan ka agala hissa  se  mitr ka hissa us kachare se bana hai jo us samay pani mein raha hoga
chattan ke bhitri bhag se sunami ke pramaan bhi mile haian chattan ke aandr 1 mitr par sunami ke pramaan milte haian chattan mein jamin paratein ek hi disha mein hain aur isse lagata hai ki bahut uchch urja ki kisi ghatana ke karn inka jamaav huaa hoga 
vaijnanikon ka kahana hai ki is prabhav se ek baadi lahar paida hui jo kretr se kai kilomitr dur ke taton tak pahuanchi hogi
lekin ye lahar vaps aai hogi aur chattan ka upari hissa jin padarthon se milkar bana hai, aisa lagata hai ki sunami ki vapsi lahar ka natija hai 
stin mein tekss vishvvidyaaly ke praofesr aur risrch ke saha-lekhk, shan gulik ne bbc ko batayaa, "yah sab ek din mein huaa sunami kisi havai jahaz ki gati se chalati hai aur chaubis ghante laharon ko dur le jane aur phir se vaps lene ke lie paryaapt samay hai"
praofesr gulik ki tim vahan mile kai subuton ke aadhar par sunami aane ki bat par vishvas kar rahi hai kyoanki chattan ke upari paraton mein charkol ka mishrn mila hai, jo is bat ka pramaan hai ki takkr ke karn jo aag paida hui hogi vo aas pas ke zamini ilaqon tak pahuanchi hogi 
dilchasp bat yah hai ki risrch tim ko chattan mein kahin bhi salfr nahin mila hai yah aashchry ki bat hai kyoanki yah ulka piand salfr yukt khanijon se bane samudri tal se takarayaa hoga
kisi karn se salfr vashp mein badal kar khtm ho gayaa lagata hai 
yah natija us siddhaant ka bhi samarthn karata hai ki daynasor prithvi se kaise vilupt hue the
salfr ke pani mein ghulne aur hava mein milne se mausm kafi thanda ho gayaa hoga mausm ke itna thanda ho jane se har tarah ke paudhon aur janvaron ke lie jivit rahana behd mushkil huaa hoga
praofesr gulik kahate hain, "is prakriyaa se nikle salfr ki maatra ka anumaan  giga tan hai yah kraiktoaa jaise jvalamukhi se niklane vali maatra se bahut zyaada hai kraikatoaa se niklane vali salfr ki maatra bhi mausm ko kafi thanda kar sakati"
stnapayi is aapada se ubar gae lekin daynador iske prabhav se nahin bach pae
1 kilomitr chauada ulkapiand, jisne prithvi ke krst mein 1 kilomitr chauada aur  kilomitr gahara chhed bana diyaa 
isse  kilomitr chauada aur kuchh kilomitr gahara kretr ban gayaa 
aaj adhikaansh kretr samudr mein dafn haian  zamin par ye laimston se dhake hue hote haian

nae iphone 11, iphone 11 pro aur iphone 11 pro max phons ki khasiyt yah batai gai hai ki inke kaimre ek sath kai tarah ke pharamait mein vidiyo slomoshn selfi, laiandskep selfi rikrd kar sakate haian

inka praosesr bhi pahale ke aaifons ke muqable badhiyaa lagae gae haian yaani ye fon pahale se bhi adhik tezi se kam kareange

bite kuchh varshon mein mashin larniang aur aartiphishiyl iantelijeans ke kshetr mein bahut kam huaa hai

log ye bhi dava karate hain ki aisa islie hota hai kyoanki unaka mobail unaki niji batchit ko sun raha hota hai
ek mobail surksha kanpni ne in lokpraiy davon, jise aksr log sazish karar dete hain, ki paadtal ki 
kanpni ne pata lagane ki koshish ki ki kyaa vastv mein baadi tek kanpniyaan humaari batchit sun rahi hain?
soshl midiyaa par bhi isse juade post aksr dekhne ko milte hain, jismein log dava karate hain ki fesbuk aur gugl jaisi kanpniyaan unaki jasusi kar rahi hai taki unaki vyktigt zarurton ke hisab se unhein sanbandhit vijnapn dikhayaa ja sake
hal ke mahinon mein soshl midiyaa par kai aise vidiyo vayral hue hain, jinmein praodkts ke bare mein log bat kar rahe hote hain aur phir unhin praodkts ke vijnapn nalain dikhai dete haian
mobail surksha kanpni vaandera ke saibr surksha visheshjnon ne iski sachchai pata karne ke lie ek nalain adhyyan kiyaa aur payaa ki ye dave bilkul galat hain ki aapaka fon aur aip aapaki niji batchit ko sun raha hai
shodhkartaon ne do mobail fon lie, pahala saimsang aur dusra aaiphon 
in donon phon ko unhoanne ek "diyo rum" mein rakh diyaa, jahan  mint tak lagatar kutte aur billi ke khane se juade diyo vijnapn chalae
iske alava, ek dusre shaant kamare mein do ek jaise phon phon rakhe gae
surksha visheshjnon ne in phon mein ianstl fesbuk, ianstagram, krom, snaipchait, yutyub aur amezn ko sabhi paramishn die taki ve diyo, iantrnet, kaimra, gailri ka istemaal kar sakean
iske bad unhoanne sabhi ep plaitpharm aur vebpej par paltu janvaron ke khane se juade vijnapn sarch kie aur dekhe is dauran unhoanne fon ki baitri aur deta ki khapat ka bhi vishleshn kiyaa
unhoanne is prayog ko tin dinon tak ek hi samay par dohrayaa aur payaa ki "diyo rum" mein rakhe fon par paltu janvar ke khane se juade koi bhi vijnapn nahin dikhae gae aur n hi baitri aur deta ki khapat zyaada hui
donon kamaron mein phon par dekhe jane vale vijnapn samaan the sabhi phon ke deta traansphar ko rikrd kiyaa gayaa aur usaki tulna varchual asisteant aip jaise siri aur gugl asisteant ke istemaal kie gae deta se ki gai 
vaandera ke sistm ianjiniyr jems maik ne kaha, "hum logon ne payaa ki  mint mein jitna deta varchual asisteant ep mein kharch huaa, usase kahin kam kharch fesbuk, yutyub, ianstagram, krom, snaipchait, yutyub aur amezn par huaa isse yah pata chala ki ye ep lagatar diyo rikrdiang nahin kar rahe the aur n hi use klaud par apalod kar rahe the" 
unhoanne kaha, "agar ye kanpniyaan humaari jasusi kar rahi hotin to hum ummid kar rahe the ki inka deta upayog varchual asisteant aip ke deta khapat se zyaada hota"
tek kanpniyaan varshon se in davon ko kharij karati rahi hain ki vo humaari jasusi ke lie humaare mobail fon mein lage maaikrofon ka istemaal karate haian
pichhle sal fesbuk pramukh maark zakarabarg ne amariki sansd mein apane bayaan mein jasusi ke aaropon ko kharij kiyaa tha
halaanki logon ka in kanpniyon ke prati avishvas badha hai aur kai yujrs ko ab bhi lagata hai ki unake sath jasusi ho rahi hai
adhyyan mein ek dilchasp bat yah bhi samne aai ki shaant kamare mein rakhe phon ke adhikaansh eandrid aip ne "diyo rum" ke aaiphon aip ki tulna mein adhik deta istemaal kiyaa tha
adhyyan mein jo batein samne aai hain, usake aadhar par kanpni ke saha-sansthapk aur mukhy karykari adhikari eldr tuve ne kaha ki unhein is bat ke koi sabut nahin mile ki ye aip aisa kuchh rahe haian "ho sakata hai ki jasusi dusre tarikon se ki ja rahi ho, jiske bare mein hum nahin jante, lekin main kahuanga ki iski aashanka bahut kam hai"
abhi tak ki paadtal se jo bhi natije samne aae hain, vo suchna surksha udyog ke logon ko nahin chauankaeange kyoanki unhein barason se yah sach pata hai ki baadi tek kanpniyon ko apane grahkon ke bare mein pahale se hi itna kuchh pata hota hai ki unhein logon ki niji batchit sunne ki zarurt hi nahin hai
sachchai ye hai ki vijnapn dene vali kanpniyaan mobail fon istemaal karne vale logon ke bare mein jankari jutane ke lie atyaadhunik tarike apanati haian  
misal ke taur par lokeshn deta, braauziang histri aur piksls ko traik karake is bare mein paryaapt jankari pai ja sakati hai ki mobail fon yuzar kyaa kharidne ke bare mein soch raha hai 
vijnapn dene vali kanpniyaan soshl midiyaa ke zarie logon ke doston tak pahuanch sakati hain aur ye aandaza laga sakati hain ki aap kin chizon mein dilchaspi rakhate haian is tarah ki takanik din pratidin din behtar ho rahi hai
soteriz damitreyu landn ke ianpiriyl kalej mein mobail vijnapn aur surksha visheshjn haian 
vo kahate hain, "jo vijnapn aap apane fon par dekhte hain vo kanpniyon ke pas pahale se maujud deta ka natija hote haian mashin-larniang elgoridma itna taktavar hota hai ki kanpniyon ko aapase pahale pata chal jata hai ki aap kis praodkt mein dilchaspi lene vale haian" 
halaanki aisi ghatanaen bhi zarur hui hain jab payaa gayaa ki kuchh aip yuzars ki aiktiviti vijnapn ke maqsad se rikrd kar rahe haian
pichhle sal jun mein amarika ki narthistrn yunivrsiti ke shodhrktaon ne duniyaa bhar ke alaga-alag aiandrid aip stor ke 1, mobail fon test kie
shodhkartaon ko aisa to koi sabut nahin mila jismein yuzars ki aapasi batein suni ja rahi hon lekin unhein kuchh chhote aip zarur mile jo mobail yuzar ke niji skrinshat aur vidiyo tisre paksh ko bhej rahe the 
halaanki ye bhi devlapameant ke maqsad se kiyaa gayaa tha, vijnapn ke maqsad se nahian
shodhkartaon ki tim ne ye bhi svikar kiyaa ki kuchh sarakari aur khufiyaa vibhag bhi ahum padon par kam karne vale logon ke mobail fon ko jasusi ke lie nishana banate haian
pichhle sal mai mein vatsaip ne maana tha ki haikr iske zariye logon ke mobail fon mein jasusi ke maqsad se saftveyr ianstl karne mein kamyaab rahe the
fesbuk ke svamitv vale vatsaip ne batayaa tha ki haikron ne chunianda logon ke akauant ko nishana banayaa tha halaanki iske bad se is surksha msale ko hal kar liyaa gayaa tha

is vayral tasvir ke sath log yah dava kar rahe hain ki chand ka chakkr laga rahe rbitr ne vikrm laiandr ki ye tharml tasvir li hai jise isro ne jari kiyaa hai
 dinon ki lanbi yaatra ke bad shanivar,  sitanbr 1 ko jab chandryaan- ka vikrm laiandr chand ki satah se mahaj 1 kilomitr dur tha, tab bhartiy aantriksh anusandhan sangthan ke beangluru seantr se usaka sanprk tut gayaa tha
manglavar subh isro ne apane aadhikarik tvitr haiandl se tvit kar yah suchna di hai ki "chandryaan- ke rbitr ne vikrm laiandr ki lokeshn pata kar li hai, lekin usase sanprk abhi tak sthapit nahin kiyaa ja saka hai vikrm laiandr se sanprk banane ki sabhi sanbhv koshishein jari haian"
isse pahale ravivar ko isro pramukh ke sivn ne samaachar ejeansi pitiaai se kaha tha ki "isro ko chand ki satah par vikrm laiandr ki tasvirein mili haian rbitr ne vikrm laiandr ki tharml imej li hai jise dekhkar lagata hai ki vikrm laiandr ki chaand par hard laiandiang hui hai"
lekin jo tasvir soshl midiyaa par vikrm laiandr ki batakr sheyr ki ja rahi hai vo bhramk hai
isro ne apani aadhikarik vebsait ke zariye, aadhikarik fesbuk aur tvitr akauant se yaa fir kisi praes riliz ke zariye vikrm laiandr ki koi tasvir jari nahin ki hai
rivrs imej sarch se pata chalata hai ki jis tasvir ko bhartiy rbitr dvara li gai vikrm laiandr ki tharml imej batakr sheyr kiyaa ja raha hai, vo daraasal amariki spes ejeansi nasa ke mishn apolo-1 ki tasvir hai
1 jun 1 ko nasa ne apani aadhikarik vebsait par ek fichr stori chhapi thi jismein is tasvir ka istemaal kiyaa gayaa tha
is fichr stori ke anusar yah apolo-1 ki laiandiang sait ki tasvir hai
nasa ka apolo-1 lunr laiandiang mishn 1 apraail 1 ko 1 bajakar  mint par amarika ke florida mein sthit kainedi spes seantr se lanch kiyaa gayaa tha
yah chand par utarne ke lie nasa ke ek chalk dal ka vahn tha tin logon ke is chalk dal ki aguvai kamaaandr jan dablyu yang kar rahe the
nasa ke apolo-1 mishn ke dauran tinon aantrikshyaatriyon ne chand par kul 1 ghante, do mint ka vaqt bitayaa tha
is dauran aantriksh yaatriyon ne  ghante, 1 mint mein kul tin alag charanon mein chand par chahalaqdami ki thi 11 dinon tak chala nasa ka yah mishn  apraail 1 ko pura huaa tha
soshl midiyaa khastaur se tvitra par bite kuchh dinon mein bhartiy spes ejeansi aur isro pramukh ke sivn ke nam se kai frzi akauant banaye gae hain jinke sath ye dava kiyaa ja raha hai ki vo unake aadhikarik akauant haian
lekin bhartiy aantriksh anusandhan sangthan ne spsht kiyaa hai ki ye sabhi praofail aur akauant frzi haian
isro ki aadhikarik vebsait par prakashit sabase taza apadet ke anusar ke sivn ka soshl midiyaa par koi parsnal akauant nahin hai unaki tasviron vale frzi akauants se di ja rahin suchnaon par vishvas n karean
isi ke sath isro ne apani aadhikarik vebsait par sangthan ke aadhikarik tvitr, fesbuk aur yu-tyub liank jari kiye haian

pahali nazar mein ye kuchh khas nahin dikhta lekin sal 1 se yah ganitjnon ke lie ek paheli bana huaa hai 
iski vajah kyaa hai? ise samajhane ke lie in kuchh dilchasp tathyon ko dekhieh
aaie ise karake dekhte haianh
ab sankhyaa  ke sath yahi karake dekhte hain-
lekin ho sakata hai ki aap sochein ki ye mahaz sanyog hai to chalie kisi dusre nanbr ke sath ye prakriyaa dohraate haian maan lijie  ko lete haian 
bhartiy ganitjn dattatrey ramchandr kapraekr 1-1 ko sankhyaaon ke sath prayog karna behd pasand tha aur isi prakriyaa mein unaka parichy is rahasymayi sankhyaa 1 se huaa 
sal 1 mein madras mein hue ek ganit sammeln mein kapraekr ne duniyaa ko is sankhyaa se parichit karayaa 
vo kaha karate the, "jis tarah madahosh bane rahane ke lie ek sharabi sharab pita hai sankhyaaon ke maamle mein mere sath bhi bilkul aisa hi hai"
vo muanbi vishvidyaaly se padhe the aur muanbi ke devlali qsbe mein ek skul mein padhate hue unhoanne apani ziandgi guzari thi 
halaanki unaki khoj ka mazaq uadaga gayaa aur bhartiy ganitjnon ne ise kharij kar diyaa aksr unhein skul aur kalejon mein unake vishesh tariqe par bat rakhane ke lie bulayaa jata tha 
dhire-dhire unaki khoj ko lekr bhart aur videshon mein charcha hone lagi aur 1 ke dashak tak amarika ke best seliang lekhk aur ganit mein ruchi rakhane vale maartin gardr ne unake bare mein ek lokpraiy saians maigzin saiantifik amerika mein unake bare mein likha 
aaj kapraekr aur unaki khoj ko maanyta mil rahi hai aur is par duniyaa bhar ke ganitjn kam kar rahe haian

isro ke pramukh ke sivn ne kaha ki, "isro ko chaand ki satah par laiandr ki tasvir mili hai chaand ka chakkr laga rahe rbitr ne vikrm laiandr ki tharml imej li hai"
isro pramukh ne yah bhi kaha hai ki chandryaan- mein lage kaimron ne laiandr ke bhitr prajnan rovr ke hone ki pushti ki hai
in sabhi baton ke bad ab yah ummid lagai ja rahi hai ki kyaa bhart ka sapana, jo shukrvar ki raat adhura rah gayaa tha vo pura ho paega
shukrvar ki raat vikrm laiandr chandrmaa ki satah par pahuanchne se kevl 1 kilomitr ki duri par hi tha jab usaka sanprk grauand steshn se tut gayaa
ke sivn ne kaha hai ki isro lagatar vikrm laiandr se sanprk banane ki koshish kar raha hai halaanki vaijnanik iski bahut kam ummid jata rahe haian
unaka kahana hai ki agar dobara sanprk hota hai to yah ek adbhut bat hogi
vaijnanik gauhr raza ne bbc se kaha, "yah bahut mushkil hai sanprk dobara sadhne ke lie laiandr ka chaand ki satah par sahi salamt utarna zaruri hai, itna hi nahin vo is tarah se utare ki usake paanv satah par hi hon aur usake vo hisse kam kar rahe hon, jisse humaara sanprk tut gayaa tha"
"dusri zaruri bat yah hai ki laiandr is sthiti mein ho ki vo  vat pavr jenret kar sake aur usake solr painl ko surj ki roshni mil rahi ho"
vo bahut ummid nahin rakhate hain ki laiandr ka sanprk rbitr se dobara ho sakega unake mutabik agar dobara sanprk hota hai to yah adbhut bat hogi
halaanki isro ismein kitna kamyaab ho paega, aane vale dinon mein iska pata chal paega 
ke sivn ne laiandr ki tharmla imej lene ki bat kahi hai rbitr mein jo kaimre lage hue hain vo tharmla tasvirein leta hai
har chij, jo shuny digri tapmaan mein nahin hoti hain, usase redieshan hota rahata hai ye redieshan tab tak aaankh se nahin dikhai dete hain, jab tak vo chiz itni garm n ho jae, jisse aankhon se dikhai dene vali roshni n niklane lage
jaise loha garm karate hain to ek simaa ke bad isse roshni niklane lagati hai, lekin isse sadharn tapmaan mein redieshan hota rahata hai
is tharml redieshan ko rbitr mein lage hue kaimre kaipchr karate hain aur ek tasvir banate hain aur isi tasvir ko tharml imej kahate haian ye tasvir thoadi dhuandhli hoti hain, jinki vyaakhyaa karni paadti hai ye vaisi tasvir nahin hoti hain, jaisi hum aam kaimre se lete haian
ek saval yah bhi uth raha hai ki kyaa laiandr durghtanagrst ho gayaa hai yaa phir sahi salamt sthiti mein hai
vaijnanik gauhr raza kahate hain, "ravivar tak praapt suchna ke hisab se laiandr puri tarah tuta nahin hai agar tut ke bikhr jata to hum nahin kah patein ki laiandr ki tasvirein li gai haian"
hard laiandiang mein laiandr ko kitna nuksan pahuancha hai, is bare mein ke sivn ne saf taur par kuchh nahin batayaa hai
vaijnanik iska matalab yah nikal rahe hain ki usaki spid mein itni kami to aa hi gai thi ki satah se takara kar laiandr puri tarah barbad nahin huaa hai
gauhr raza kahate hain, "iska yah bhi matalab hai ki usaki spid tab tak kam hoti rahi, jab tak vo chaand ki satah par utar nahin gayaa"
rbitr ke dvara li gai tasviron ke vishleshn ke bad hi pata chal paega ki laiandr ko kitna nuksan pahuancha hai
is saval ke javab mein gauhr raza kahate hain ki 1 kilomitr par jab humaara sanprk laiandr se tut gayaa tha, us duri se chandrmaa ki satah pahuanchne tak ki sahi suchna humein nahin mil pai thi
"ab laiandr ki tasvirein humein mil gai hain, aise mein ab is bat ka aandaja lagayaa ja sakata hai ki aantim kshnon mein kyaa huaa hoga"
abhi tak vaijnanik yah kayaas laga rahe hain ki aantim vaqt mein laiandr ki spid kantrol nahin ho pai thi yah ek baadi chunauti hoti hai ki ek laiandr ko tay spid par satah par utara jae taki use koi kshti n ho aur usake pair jamin par hi paadean
sapht laiandiang ke lie laiandr ki spid ko 1 hazar kilomitr se  kilomitr prati ghanta karna tha yah kaha ja raha hai ki isro se spid kantroliang mein hi chuk hui aur usaki sapht laiandiang nahin ho pai
laiandr mein charon taraf char raket yaa phir kahe to ianjn lage the, jinhein spid kam karne ke lie phayr kiyaa jana tha jab ye upar se niche aa raha hota hai, tab ye raket niche se upar ki taraph phayr kie jate hain taki spid kantrol kiyaa ja sake
aant mein paanchva raket laiandr ke bich mein laga tha, jiska kam  mitr upar tak laiandr ko jiro spid mein lana tha, taki vo aaram se laiand kar sake, par aisa nahin ho saka pareshani karib do kilomitr upar se hi shuru ho gai thi

tvitr par raat qrib sadhe aath baje aankita shukla ne ek tvit kiyaa is tvit mein unhoanne likha ki unhein madad ki zarurt hai 
mahaj kuchh hi ghanton mein unake is tvit ko saikadon logon ne sheyr kiyaa is par unhein mahila aayog ne javab diyaa aur keandriy mantri smriti irani ne mahila aayog ke tvit ko ri-tvit kiyaa
aankita ne apane tvit mein likha "kripyaa mujhe bacha lijie main ziandgi khtm karne ki qgar par huan mujhe har mint sharirik, maansik aur bhavnatmk shoshn ka samna karna paad raha hai"
aankita ne jo tvit kiyaa hai usamein unhoanne ek shakhs ka fesbuk praofail aur jamashedpur ke saibr kraim thane mein is sanbandh mein darj karai gai apani efaaiaar ko bhi tvit kiyaa hai yah shikayt 1 sitanbr ko risiv ki gai hai
aankita ne apane is tvit mein kaibinet mantri smriti irani, rashtriy mahila aayog aur dilli mahila aayog ko taig bhi kiyaa tha
unake is tvit par pratikriyaa dete hue rashtriy mahila aayog ke adhikrit tvitr haiandl se javab diyaa gayaa
rashtriy mahila aayog ne aankita ke tvit ko ri-tvit karate hue pahala tvit kiyaa "aankita se bat ho gai hai aur unase jankariyaan sajha ki gai haian unake rajy ke dijipi se bhi bat ki gai hai hum aankita ke sath khaade haian"
iske alava rashtriy mahila aayog ki adhyksh rekha sharmaa ne bhi tvit kiyaa hai ki unaki aankita se bat hui hai aur ab vo behtar haian kal subh tak unake pas humaari madad pahuanch jaegi 
iske bad aankita sharmaa ne bhi tvit kar unase batchit hone ki pushti ki hai aankita ne likha hai ki ab vo behtar mahasus kar rahi haian unhoanne mahila aayog aur smriti irani ko dhanyvad kaha hai
aankita shukla ne tvitr par khud ke parichy mein saibr kraim viktim, sikiang help n l soshl midiyaa pletpharms likha hai
unaka tvitr akauant sitanbr mein hi bana hai 
is haiandl se ravivar ki raat  par pahala tvit kiyaa gayaa ismein unhoanne kuchh laadkon ke nam likh kar un par balatkar ki dhamaki dene ka aarop lagayaa tha iske bad is tvitr haiandl se kai tvit kiye gae jismein kai skrin shats lagae gae jismein aapattijnak bhasha ka istemaal kiyaa gayaa hai aankita ka dava ki ye aapattijnak kameants unake lie kiye gae hain aur unhein badanam karne ki koshish ki ja rahi hai 
aankita shukla ne apani shikayt mein kuchh laadkon par aarop lagae hain ki unhoanne unaki tasviron ka galat istemaal kiyaa aur ab unhein dhamaki de rahe haian jin logon par aarop lagae gae hain, unaki kuchh tasvirein soshl midiyaa par vayral ho rahi haian kuchh aisi bhi tasvirein hain jinmein ve bijepi ke kai netaon ke sath haian

bhart ke pradhanmantri modi ne jahan pakistan ka nam lie bina duniyaa ko charamapanth ke khtare se aagah kiyaa vahin shaanti ke lie bhart ki pratibddhta ka jikr kiyaa 
unhoanne kaha ki bhart ne duniyaa ko yuddh nahin balki buddh diyaa haipuri duniyaa ko shaanti ka sandesh diyaa hai 
vahin pakistan ke pradhanmantri imran khan ne n sirf nam lekr bhart par aarop lagae balki bhart prashasit kashmir par bhart sarakar ke rukh ki jamakar aalochna bhi ki unhoanne kashmir ke mudde par duniyaa ke baade deshon ke chup rahane par saval bhi uthae 
modi ka bhashn 1 mint ka tha jismein unhoanne apani sarakar ke kamkaj ki charcha bhi ki vahin imran khan ka bhashn qrib pachas mint lanba tha 
unhoanne duniyaa ko aagah kiyaa ki agar bhart aur pakistan mein jang hogi to ek chhota desh hone ke nate pakistan ke pas paramaanu hathiyaar ke istemaal ke alava dusra koi chara nahin hoga
bhart aur pakistan ke pradhanmantriyon ke bhashn ko lekr soshl midiyaa par jamakar charcha ho rahi hai bhart mein modi aur pakistan mein imran khan ke bhashn ki tariph ki ja rahi hai 
bhart mein soshl midiyaa yuzar nareandr modi aur imran khan ke bhashn ki tulna bhi kar rahe haian 
agar sirf tvitr treand dekhein to bhart mein shuruaati treand yuen mein die bhashn se juade hue hi hai 
bhart mein soshl midiyaa yuzar pradhanmantri modi ke sanbodhn ko praerka bata rahe haian
keandriy grihmantri amit shah, raksha mantri rajnath sianh, kaibinet mantri smriti irani aur kaibinet mantri piyush goyl ne piem modi ko badhai di hai 
bijepi neta aur abhinetri kirn kher ne piem modi ke sanbodhn ko adbhut batayaa hai
unhoanne tvitr par likha hai, "aapane vikas, shaanti aur bhaichare ki bat ki aur aapane duniyaa ko aatankvad ke khilaf ekajut hone ke lie kaha"
tvitr yuzar jagadish likhte hain ki piem modi ne yuen mein jo bhashn diyaa vo zabaradast tha unhoanne tayalet se lekr saadk tak, aatankvad se lekr buddh tak ka zikr kiyaa jabaki imran khan ka bhashn nakaraatmk tha
ek any yuzar sonali likhti hain, "humein humaare pradhanmantri par garv hai"
tvitr yuzar shreyaaansh ne piem modi ke bhashn ki tariph karate hue unhein globl spikra batayaa hai
pakistan mein bhi yuen tap treand mein hai 
pakistan ke soshl midiyaa yuzar pradhanmantri imran khan ke bayaan ko dil jitne vala bata rahe haian kai yuzar piem imran khan ke bhashn ko aitihasik bata rahe haian
pakistan ki abhinetri vina malik ne tvitr par likha hai,"sanyukt rashtr mahasbha mein imran khan ka mukhr sanbodhn mujhe unaki aakramk kriket kaptani ke dinon ki yaad dila gayaa"
pakistan ke purv tez geandbaz shoeb akhtr ne tvit kiyaa hai, "aaj aapane sabit kar diyaa ki aap islam aur pakistan ke sachche pravakta haian aap nishchit taur par shaanti ke dut haian aap vishv neta ban rahe haian itne baade mudde par aapane jis tarah ka sanbodhn diyaa usake lie aapako salam" 
pakistani kalakar shafat ali ne tvit kiyaa hai, "sanbhvata pakistan ke kisi shirsh neta ki or se bhart ko diyaa gayaa ab tak ka sabase prabhavi javab"
muhmmd nadim likhte hain, "mujhe mere pradhanmantri imran khan se pyaar hai" is tvit ke sath nadim ne ek tasvir bhi sheyr ki hai 
aarslan kaisrani ne tvit kiyaa hai "kyaa sochkyaa bhashna"
aruj khan ne tvit kiyaa hai, "is bhashn ko pakistani kitabon mein shamil kiyaa jana chahie"

inmein karporeshn baiank, yuko baiank, aaidibiaai baiank, baiank f maharashtr, aaandhra baiank, iandiyn ovarasiz baiank, seantrl baiank f iandiyaa, dena baiank aur yunaited baiank f iandiyaa shamil haian

is maisej ki sachchai janne ke lie budhvar ko bbc ne vitt mantraly aur aarabiaai ke varishth adhikariyon se sanprk karne ki koshish ki thi
rizarv baiank f iandiyaa ne aadhikarik tvitr haiandl se tvit kar ise mahaz ek afvah ghoshit kiyaa aur kaha ki soshl midiyaa par sheyr ki ja rahi kamarshiyl baiankon ko band kiye jane ki bat galat hai

 agast 1 ko bhart ki vitt mantri nirmla sitarman ne ek sath kai baiankon ke vily ki ghoshna ki thi

haudi modi karykrm ke bad manglavar ko modi aur tranp ki phir mulaqat hui is dvipkshiy varta ke bad tranp aur modi midiyaa se rubru hue
is praes kanphreans mein ek bhartiy patrkar ne modi ki maujudgi mein tranp se kuchh saval puchhe 
in savalon ka tranp ne jo javab diyaa, usaki charcha soshl midiyaa par ho rahi hai ek din pahale jab tranp imran khan ke sath praes kanphreans kar rahe the, tab bhi aisa huaa tha aur pakistani patrkaron ka bhart mein jamakar mazak uadayaa gayaa tha
ab tranp ka aisa hi kuchh bayaan bhartiy patrkaron ke lie bhi aayaa hai
tarikh  sitanbr 1 
pakistani pradhanmantri imran khan se mulakat ke bad amariki rashtrpati donld tranp ki sajha praes kanphreans thi
pakistani riportr kashmir par sanyukt rashtr ke adhyaadesh se juada ek saval tranp se puchhta hai
iske bad ek dusra pakistani riportr tranp se saval puchhta hai-  dinon se kashmir band hai na hi iantrnet, na hi phon kashmir mein maanvadhikaron ka ullanghn ho raha hai aap kashmiri logon ke lie kyaa kar rahe hain?
tranp, imran se kahate hain, aap aise riportr kahan se khojkar late haian ye log kamaal ke haian
amarika mein patrkaron se rashtrpati tranp ke bich kai bar tikhi jang ho chuki hai 
tranp kai mauqon par midiyaa sansthanon aur patrkaron ko fek nyuz phailane vala batate hue mazak uada chuke haian 
1 mein bbc ke jan sopl ki amariki rashtrpati tranp se noankjhoank hui thi  bbc ke jan sopl jab saval karne ke lie khaade hue to tranp ne unhein bich mein hi rokte hue puchha, "aap kahan se?"

patrkar rohini sianh ne tvit kiyaa, "jo log hiandi ko rashtrbhasha banane ki maaang kar rahe hain, unase pahale tamil, telugu aur malayaalm sikhne ko kaha jae phir dekheange ki vo apani murkhtapurn maaang jari rakhate hain yaa nahian"
ye pahali bar nahin hai jab kisi ek bhasha ko baqiyon se upar rakhe jane ke prastav ka virodh huaa hai gair-hiandibhashi rajyon khaskar tamilnadu mein hiandi thope jane ka virodh kafi pahale se hota aayaa hai

es ali raza bukhari likhte hain, "mujhe nahin pata hai ki hum log unaka mazak kyon uada rahe haian unhoanne kam se kam koshish to ki hai aur vo ismein saphal hone ke kafi karib bhi hai ye sirf kharab kismt ki bat thi unhein koshish karne ke lie pure nanbr milne chahie"
altaf batt likhte hain, "allah ke lie ruk jaie, aap saians eand teknolji ministr haian bhart ko unaka mun mishn rokne ka lekchr dene ki jagah aap us tarikh ki ghoshna kar sakate the jab aap bhart se pahale chaand tak pahuancheange ise ek avasar ki tarah lijie"
tvitr yuzar hummaad azij likhte hain, "hum sabhi unhein trol kar rahe hain, jinmein main bhi shamil huan lekin mantri ji, unhoanne koshish to ki hai aur unake aandr apani asaphalata svikar karne ka sahs to hai mazak ki bat chhoad dein to ye is kantineant ke lie ek upalabdhi hai"
iske sath hi ek any chhatr muhmmd vasim likhte hain, "ye humaare saians eand teknolji ministr hain jinki soch hai aantriksh mein ek mishn bhejna aur chaand ki kaksha tak pahuanchna, paglapan se bhara mishn hai aur ye paise ki barbadi hai
pakistani sena ke pravakta aasif gafur ne bhi tvit kar kaha hai, bahut badhiyaa isro kiski galati hai? pahala- begunah kashmiriyon jinhein qaid kar rakha gayaa hai? dusra- muslim aur alpsankhyk ki? tisra- bhart ke bhitr hindutv virodhi aavaz? chautha- aaiesaaai? aapako hindutv kahin nahin le jaega
kashif inayt ne tvit kar likha hai, "diyr aasif sahb, isro ne shandar kam kiyaa hai vaijnanik samuday ke sadasy hone ke nate main isro ko lagabhag saphal mishn ke lie badhai dena chahta huan han, isro phel huaa hai kyoanki ye ek kathin kam tha lekin unhein ahum deta mila hai joki unhein unake agale mishn mein madad dega"
ve likhte hain, "main ye salah dena chahta hun ki paadosiyon ko chidhane ki jagah pakistan ki saiantiphik kamyuniti par dhyaan keandrit karna chahie main ek bar phir isro ko unake prayaason ke lie badhai dena chahuanga"

"bhart ko sabhi bhartiyon ki raksha karni chahie, hianduon ki nahian"
budhvar ko bijepi neta himant bisva saramaa aur l iandiyaa majalis-e-ittehadul muslimin aimim ke neta asaduddin ovaisi ke bich tvitr par kuchh aisi hi tikhi bahas dekhne ko mili
bahas ka mudda tha bhart ke purvottr rajy asam mein enaaarasi yaani neshnal sitijns rajistra vaise to enaaarasi shuru se hi bahas ka vishy raha hai lekin ovaisi aur saramaa ke bich ye bahas manglavar ko shuru hui
daraasal asam ke vitt mantri aur bijepi neta himant bisva saramaa ne kaha tha ki vo enaaarasi ki aakhiri list, enaaarasi adhyksh aur iski puri prakriyaa se nirash haian
unhoanne ek tivi chainl se kaha, "enaaarasi ki prakriyaa mein sal 11 se pahale bhart aae kai baangladeshi hianduon ko list se bahr kar diyaa gayaa kyoanki athariti ne unake sharanarthi sartifiket ko svikar karne se inkar kar diyaa natijn baangladesh se aae kai vaidh hiandu sharanarthiyon ko list mein jagah nahin mili dusri bat ye ki enaaarasi ki prakriyaa mein bahut se logon ne jankari mein herpher karake list mein apani jagah bana li"
tivi par chal rahi is dibet mein himant bisva saramaa ne kaha, "jin hiandu sharanarthiyon ke nam enaaarasi list mein hona chahie the aur nahin hain, asam sarakar fren traybyunl aur nagrikta sanshodhn vidheyk ke jarie unaki madad karegi"
asaduddin ovaisi ne is tivi dibet ka vidiyo sheyr karate hue tvit kiyaa, "ye bilkul spsht hai ki asam mein enaaarasi ke jarie muslamaanon ko hatane ki koshish ki ja rahi hai ab himant bisva saramaa kah rahe hain ki chahe jaise bhi ho, hianduon ko bachayaa jaega"
is tvit ke javab mein himant bisva saramaa ne likha, "agar bhart hianduon ki raksha nahin karega to kaun karega? pakistan? aapaki mukhalft ke bavjud bhart piadit hianduon ka ghar rahega"
iske javab mein ovaisi ne likha, "bhart ko sabhi bhartiyon ki raksha karni chahie, hianduon ki nahian tu-neshn thyori ko pujne valon ko kabhi samajh mein nahin aaega ki yah desh kisi ek dharm se bahut, bahut baada hai sanvidhan kahata hai ki bhart sabhi dharmon, naslon aur jatiyon se samaan vyvahar karega ye hiandu rashtr nahin hai aur ianshaallah, kabhi hoga bhi nahian"
ovaisi yahin nahin ruke unhoanne phir tvit kiyaa, "ek desh ke taur humane kai piadit samudayon hianduon aur muslamaanoan ka svagt kiyaa hai vo sharanarthi hain, sanbhavit nagrik nahian dharm kabhi nagrikta ka aadhar nahin ho sakata humaare purvjon ne is vichar ko tabhi kharij kar diyaa tha jab unhoanne sanvidhan banayaa"
ovaisi ke is tvit ke javab mein himant bisva saramaa ne likha, "bhart ek sabhyta hai, desh nahian kisi desh ka itihas usake sanvidhan se shuru hota hai lekin kisi sabhyta ki shuruaat aur bhi bahut si chizon se hoti hai bhart ek samriddh sabhyta tha aur humesha rahega bhart hianduon ke lie , varshon se zyaada unaki maatribhumi hai"
enaaarasi ko lekr bhart mein rajnitik partiyon ne alaga-alag pratikriyaaen di haian isse pahale himant bisva saramaa ne hiandustan taims ko die iantravyu mein kaha tha ki vo enaaarasi ke aakhiri natijon se n to khush hain aur hi puri tarah nakhush
unhoanne kaha tha, "enaaarasi ke natijon se dukhi hone ke karn haian main khush islie hun ki asam mein nagrikon ka rikrd hai aur ab yah asanbhv hai ki koi aae aur yahan ke hone ka dava kare dusri sakaraatmk bat yah hai ki asam ke anubhv se baki bhart ko bhi sabaq milega"
enaaarasi ki aakhiri list mein kul ,11,1, logon ko shamil kiyaa gayaa hai is list mein se 1,, log bahr haian

ye vo haishtaig hai jo pakistan ki soshl midiyaa mein zor-shor se treand kar raha hai boycottindianproducts yaani bhartiy samaanon ka bahishkar karean 
pakistani soshl midiyaa mein logon ke bhart ke prati gusse ki vajah hai bhart sarakar ka anuchchhed  par haliyaa faisla
kashmir, bhart aur pakistan donon hi deshon ke bich vivad ka mudda raha hai aur aaj bhi hai jammu-kashmir ko mile vishesh darje ko khtm karne ke bhart sarakar ke faisle ke bad ek bar phir donon deshon ke bich kashmir mudda garamaa gayaa hai
ab pakistani soshl midiyaa yuzars pakistan ki janata se bhartiy utpadon ka bahishkar karne yaani bhart mein bane samaan n khridne ki apil kar rahe haian 
pakistani soshl midiyaa mein ek tabaqa logon se kah raha hai, "agar aap bhartiy samaan khrideange to bhart unhin paison se hathiyaar khridega, jiska istemaal kashmiriyon ke utpiadn mein kiyaa jaega"
pakistan ke log tvitr aur fesbuk par boycottindianproducts  ke sath tvit aur post kar rahe hain sath hi anuchchhed  par bhart sarakar ke qdam ki nianda kar rahe haian 
sirf samaan hi nahin, soshl midiyaa mein pakistaniyon se bhartiy filmein, sangit aur tivi siriyl bhi n dekhne ko kaha ja raha hai 
ek pakistani tvitr yuzar ema siddiqi likhte hain, "ek pakistani ke taur par, ye humaari zimmedari hai ki hum apane kashmiri sathiyon ke sath ekajutta dikhane ke lie bhartiy samaanon ka puri tarah bahishkar karean" 
tvit ke sath hi siddiqi ne ek tasvir bhi post ki hai jismein likha hai be pakistani, watch pakistani yaani pakistani banie, pakistani dekhie
ubaid khan ne savekashmir aur facistmodi likhkar tvit kiyaa hai, "ab vaqt hai ki hum apane aikshn ke zarie staiand lein, shabdon ke zarie nahian is muhim ka samarthn karie"
bilal shahid ka tvit hai, "bhart ke lie humaara eyaraspes abhi band nahin haihum ye humaare desh ki zimmedari hai ki hum bhart ke har ek samaan ka bahishkar karean koi bhi samaan khridne se pahale thik se dekh lean agar samaan bhart mein bana hai to use n khridean"
ek any pakistani tvitr yuzar ne freekashmir haishtaig ke sath likha hai, "balivud ganon ka bahishkar karie, balivud filmon ka bahishkar karie, apani plelist se balivud gane hata dijie, bhartiy braaiand ke samaan khridne se bachie aur bhartiy selibraitiz ko anaflo kar dijie"
imaan nam ke pakistani tvitr yuzar ne kai chizon ki list tvit ki aur likha hai ki kashmir ki khatir in sabaka bahishkar karean 
idhar, bhartiy soshl midiyaa mein pakistan ke is treand ka javab diyaa ja raha hai bhartiy boycottindianprodcuts ki aalochna kar rahe hain aur pakistani soshl midiyaa yuzars ke tvit ka javab de rahe haian
anil patil nam ke bhartiy tvitr yuzar ne likha hai, "agar aap vaqi bhartiy samaanon ka bahishkar kar rahe hain to pahale us pani ka bahishkar karie jo bhart se pakistan mein jata hai
sandhyaa ne tvit kiyaa hai, "kashmir humaara hai aur kashmiri humaare log haian agar aap bhartiy samaanon ka bahishkar kar rahe hain to phir urdu ka bhi bahishkar karie kyoanki ye bhasha bhart mein janmi humaari us zamin ko bhi chhoad dijie jo pakistan ne bhart se li aap log humesha bhart ke bare mein hi bat kyon karate rahate hain? chil karie aur pahale apani arthvyvastha bachaie"
instarover nam ke tvitr haiandl se tvit kiyaa gayaa hai, "jo pakistani boycottindianproducts treand chala rahe hain, unase bas itna hi kahana hai ki ismein tera ghata, mera kuchh nahin jata"
jammu-kashmir ko mili sanvaidhanik svaytta khtm karne ke modi sarakar ke faisle par pakistan ne shuruaat se hi kaadi pratikriyaa jatai hai pakistani pradhanmantri imran khan khud is mudde par pakistan ki sansd mein bhi bol chuke haian
unhoanne pakistani nagrikon se ye apil bhi ki thi ki vo kashmir ke lie kam se kam aadhe ghante ka vaqt nikalein aur bhart ke khilaf aavaz uthaean
vahin, bhartiy netritv ka rukh bhi pakistan ke prati aakramk huaa hai kuchh dinon pahale bhartiy rakshamantri rajnath sianh ne ek sabha mein kaha tha ki agar ab pakistan se bat hogi to sirf pioke ke msale par hogi
ab kaangres neta rahul gaandhi ne bhi kashmir mudde par pakistan par nishana sadha hai aur jammu-kashmir mein hone vali hiansa ke lie pakistan ko zimmedar thaharayaa hai 
unhoanne apane taza tvit mein likha hai, "jammu-kashmir mein hiansa hui hai vahan ki hiansa ko ukasava aur samarthn pakistan se mila hai, jise duniyaabhr mein aatankvad ka pramukh himaayti ke rup mein jana jata hai"
